Tel Mithryn Kitchen

**Tel Mithryn Kitchen** is the home of the cook [Ulves Romoran](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulves_Romoran "Skyrim:Ulves Romoran") in [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)").

It is one of the four mushroom structures in the settlement, northwest of [Tel Mithryn Steward's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_Steward%27s_House "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn Steward's House").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Ulves Romoran](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulves_Romoran "Skyrim:Ulves Romoran") |

## Tel Mithryn Kitchen

Tel Mithryn Kitchen interior

The entrance leads into a small circular room comprising the entire interior. To the east is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand over a fire, four samples of [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"), an empty pot, and a cooking spit over a fire. To the south is a table holding another empty pot, six more samples of canis root, a head of [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), a piece of [raw beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef"), a piece of [horse meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Meat "Skyrim:Horse Meat"), and a piece of [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison"). To the west are six crates, an open box holding three heads of cabbage, a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), and an owned bedroll.

# Skyrim:Tel Mithryn Steward's House

## Overview

|  |
| --- |

| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Tel Mithryn Steward's House ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Tel+Mithryn+Steward%27s+House)) | | |

Tel Mithryn Steward's House

**Tel Mithryn Steward's House** is the home of the steward [Varona Nelas](/wiki/Skyrim:Varona_Nelas "Skyrim:Varona Nelas") or [Drovas Relvi](/wiki/Skyrim:Drovas_Relvi "Skyrim:Drovas Relvi") in [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)").

It is one of the four mushroom structures in the settlement, between [Tel Mithryn's tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)") to the east and [Tel Mithryn Kitchen](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_Kitchen "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn Kitchen") to the northwest.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Drovas Relvi](/wiki/Skyrim:Drovas_Relvi "Skyrim:Drovas Relvi") \*\*  [Varona Nelas](/wiki/Skyrim:Varona_Nelas "Skyrim:Varona Nelas") \* |

\* Leaves during the quest [Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward").
\*\* Appears after completing the quest [Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward").

## Tel Mithryn Steward's House

Tel Mithryn Steward's House interior

The entrance leads into a small circular room comprising the entire interior. To the north is a crate, a narrow table, an unowned single bed, a sideboard holding a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and a copy of *[Deathbrand](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_(book) "Skyrim:Deathbrand (book)")*, and another bottle of wine and an [empty wine bottle](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle") on the floor in front of the sideboard. To the east are two crates, a set of shelves holding a [mammoth tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Tusk "Skyrim:Mammoth Tusk"), a [horker tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Tusk "Skyrim:Horker Tusk"), six empty wine bottles, a [swamp fungal pod](/wiki/Skyrim:Swamp_Fungal_Pod "Skyrim:Swamp Fungal Pod"), a bowl of [powdered mammoth tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Powdered_Mammoth_Tusk "Skyrim:Powdered Mammoth Tusk"), and a sample of [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"), a narrow table holding another empty wine bottle, and another set of shelves holding a crate, five more empty wine bottles, and seven common books. To the south are two chairs, a small table holding a bottle of wine, and a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). In the middle of the room are two chairs, two empty wine bottles, and a bottle of wine around a lit brazier.

## Notes

- Although [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") tells you he will reserve a bed and a chest for your use after completing the quest [Old Friends](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Friends "Skyrim:Old Friends"), there will still be no chest clearly reserved for your use, and the bed in the steward's house will remain the only unowned bed or bedroll in the settlement. However, the unowned bed here will often be occupied by the current steward.

## Bugs

- If [Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward") is finished and the [Sun Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Sun_Stone "Skyrim:Sun Stone") has been cleansed, Drovas's sleep package will always be active, and therefore he will be found sleeping indefinitely here.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.5, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Telrav's Request

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Escort [Telrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Telrav "Skyrim:Telrav") back to his camp in [Nilheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Nilheim "Skyrim:Nilheim").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Telrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Telrav "Skyrim:Telrav") |
| Location(s): | Road east of [Nilheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Nilheim "Skyrim:Nilheim") |
| Reward: | None |
| ID: | dunNilheimQST |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |

A pathetic-looking Telrav asks for help getting back to his camp

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Telrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Telrav "Skyrim:Telrav").
2. Escort him to his camp in [Nilheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Nilheim "Skyrim:Nilheim").
3. Kill Telrav and [his men](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_(NPC) "Skyrim:Guard (NPC)").

## Detailed Walkthrough

While passing by [Nilheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Nilheim "Skyrim:Nilheim"), you will see a man sitting by the side of the road next to an overturned cart. He will hail you as you approach: *"Bandits attacked and ransacked my cart. Can you help me?"* The man, [Telrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Telrav "Skyrim:Telrav"), will ask you to escort him to his camp, which he says is just across the bridge in Nilheim. You can refuse at this point; should you agree to help him, Telrav will stand up and walk—with surprising energy for a man who has just been attacked and left for dead—across the bridge to Nilheim.

Once you are across the bridge, however, Telrav will reveal himself. He will stand at the stairs and address the gathered bandits: *"Looks like we've got ourselves another fool."* He's led you into an ambush!

Telrav will attack you along with a swarm of leveled bandits. Telrav himself shouldn't be much of a problem, as he is relatively weak and wears only ordinary clothes. The other bandits may prove a bit challenging. After Telrav and his crew have been dealt with, you are free to loot any of the bodies and containers in the fort—including Telrav, who will sometimes have several hundred septims on his corpse.

Alternatively, you may bypass Telrav when he is on the road and proceed into Nilheim, where the bandits will be disguised as guards. If you kill them all and go talk to Telrav, when he walks across the bridge he will yell *"My men? What did you do? You'll die for this."* and attack you alone.

## Notes

- If you take the alternate route (killing the disguised bandits first), it is relatively easy to back away and hide from Telrav when he attacks. This will sometimes make him neutral and break off the attack. Thus, it can be very difficult to tell if you are in a fair fight or assaulting him. The easy way to tell is to check the number of assaults you have in your statistics and then check again after killing him.
- If you search the cliffs adjacent to the tower you will find a number of dead bodies, suggesting that Telrav and his associates' ploy has been quite effective in the past.
- If you do the bounty of killing the bandit leader while the bandits were still guards, it will not affect the quest. You have to go to Nilheim by climbing the rocks so the bug of bypassing Telrav will not occur. When the quest is initiated, everyone will change from guards to bandits except the bandit leader, who will be dead from the bounty quest.

## Bugs

- If you bypass Telrav and head on to Nilheim, the bandits are labeled as guards and won't attack. If you then return to Telrav to initiate the quest, he will walk up to the camp, tell you to wait for your reward, and when the guards don't attack, he will walk back to where he started and sit back down. He won't give any reward and no further dialogue options are available. If you go ahead and attack him, it counts as an assault but not a murder.
  - He will go back to where he started too if you used sneak to get unseen during the battle.
- Dragon attacks near Nilheim may involve Telrav and his "Guards". If Telrav and his cohorts are spoken to before returning to their respective locations, it is possible to have both the "Escort..." and "Kill..." quest stages simultaneously. The guards return to their camp and then attack as bandits while Telrav returns to his roadside location and remains unresponsive, rendering the "Escort..." quest incompletable and forcing you to attack in order to complete the "Kill..." quest.
- This quest is never stopped once Telrav is dead, leading to the location becoming blocked for [Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant") and the bandit bodies never respawning properly. Similarly, if you kill Telrav while escorting him to the Nilheim camp, the quest will stick at "Escort Telrav to his camp" instead of failing.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=13965))[*verification needed — user reports the fix doesn't work*]
- This quest is set up as a Miscellaneous quest but increments the Side Quests achievement when it isn't supposed to.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Telrav's Request (dunNilheimQST) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I've found an injured merchant and agreed to escort him back to his camp. *Objective 10:* Escort Telrav to his camp. |
| 20 |  | Retrieve your reward from Telrav. |
| 30 |  | Telrav has doublecrossed me and he will pay. *Objective 30:* Kill Telrav |
| 100 | ☑ | Telrav and his men are dead. |
| 150 | ☒ | I have killed Telrav and can no longer lead him to his camp. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage dunNilheimQST stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest dunNilheimQST`.

# Skyrim:Telvanni Research

## Overview

| Reward: | 250 gold, ability to buy spell tome [Conjure Ash Spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Conjure Ash Spawn") from [Talvas Fathryon](/wiki/Skyrim:Talvas_Fathryon "Skyrim:Talvas Fathryon") |

| |  |  | | --- | --- | | Prerequisites: | Conjuration 40; any time after speaking to Neloth during [Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward") except when finding him a new steward | | |

Several live ash spawn

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") in [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)").
2. Collect an ash sample from the remains of an [ash spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn").
3. Return to Neloth for your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

After making your way to [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)"), find and speak to [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") and ask if you can help out. He will give you an extractor, and ask you to obtain an ash sample from an [ash spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn") as he is working on a spell to summon them. He will inform you that the ash sample can only be extracted from a dead ash spawn, but remains confident in your ability to "bring it about."

Find and kill any ash spawn. The wall outside [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") should have plenty of ash spawn if you haven't already completed [March of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:March_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:March of the Dead"). Note that you can still extract the sample from the remains of an ash spawn killed prior to starting the quest, so if you have recently completed March of the Dead, you'll likely still be able to find their remains outside of the city walls.

Searching the corpse of an ash spawn should bring up the option to use the extractor. After using it, return to Neloth for you reward. The spell tome [Conjure Ash Spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Conjure Ash Spawn") should be available for sale from [Talvas Fathryon](/wiki/Skyrim:Talvas_Fathryon "Skyrim:Talvas Fathryon") a day or so after completion of the quest.

## Quest Stages

| 300 | ☑ | Neloth is doing research on ash spawn. I brought him a sample of the ash from one using a special extraction tool. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2TTR3a stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2TTR3a`.

Temple Ancestral Tomb

The **Temple Ancestral Tomb** is a [Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") ancestral tomb in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").

It can only be accessed from within the [Raven Rock Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple "Skyrim:Temple"), the [Morvayn Ancestral Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Morvayn_Ancestral_Tomb "Skyrim:Morvayn Ancestral Tomb"), and the [Ulen Ancestral Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulen_Ancestral_Tomb "Skyrim:Ulen Ancestral Tomb"), as it doesn't have direct access outside. The [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Tomb_Key "Skyrim:Raven Rock Tomb Key") required to unlock the doors between the tomb and these three otherwise separate areas can be obtained as part of the quest [Clean Sweep](/wiki/Skyrim:Clean_Sweep "Skyrim:Clean Sweep").

## Related Quests

- **[Clean Sweep](/wiki/Skyrim:Clean_Sweep "Skyrim:Clean Sweep")**: Clear the Temple Ancestral Tomb of [ash spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn").
- **[Pain in the Necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Pain_in_the_Necklace "Skyrim:Pain in the Necklace")**: Find [East Empire pendants](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") for [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor").

## Temple Ancestral Tomb

The entrance from the Temple leads into a corridor lined with four lit braziers which proceeds north to the tomb room. In the room, to the west is a corridor leading to the key-locked door to the Morvayn Ancestral Tomb, and to the east is a matching corridor leading to the key-locked door to the Ulen Ancestral Tomb. The room and west and east corridors feature a total of nine ash piles littered with bones, with the two central piles surrounded by steps and lit candles. An [East Empire Company strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Strongbox "Skyrim:East Empire Company Strongbox") is partly buried in the ash pile to the north. Also in the area are three ash yam urns to the north and west, two benches to the west, four unusable barrels to the south and east, and six more lit braziers around the central piles and in the west and east corridors.

## Bugs

- The East Empire Company strongbox here is unlocked, rather than expert-locked like almost all other East Empire Company strongboxes.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.5, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Temple of Dibella

## Overview

Temple of Dibella

The **Temple of Dibella** is a small [Aedric](/wiki/Lore:Aedra "Lore:Aedra") temple dedicated to [Dibella](/wiki/Lore:Dibella "Lore:Dibella"), the Aedric goddess of love, beauty, and artistry. It is located in the center of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") above the [Shrine of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Talos "Skyrim:Shrine of Talos"), reached by climbing many flights of stairs. It is home to the [priestesses](/wiki/Skyrim:Priest "Skyrim:Priest") of Dibella, led by [Hamal](/wiki/Skyrim:Hamal "Skyrim:Hamal").

The temple consists of two zones: *[Temple of Dibella](#Temple_of_Dibella)* and *[Inner Sanctum](#Inner_Sanctum)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Anwen](/wiki/Skyrim:Anwen "Skyrim:Anwen")  [Fjotra](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra") \*  [Hamal](/wiki/Skyrim:Hamal "Skyrim:Hamal") [Trainer (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Master)")[Enchanting (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Enchanting (Master)")  [Orla](/wiki/Skyrim:Orla "Skyrim:Orla")  [Senna](/wiki/Skyrim:Senna "Skyrim:Senna") |

\* Only moves here after completing [The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella")

## Related Quests

- **[Speak to Degaine](/wiki/Skyrim:Speak_to_Degaine "Skyrim:Speak to Degaine")**: Ask a [beggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Degaine "Skyrim:Degaine") about money.
- **[The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella")**: Find a new [Sybil](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra") for the Temple of Dibella.
- **[A Night To Remember](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember")**: Find your lost friend, [Sam](/wiki/Skyrim:Sam_Guevenne "Skyrim:Sam Guevenne"), as you recover from a bad hangover.

## Temple of Dibella

The temple's interior

The first time that you enter, you will be approached by [Senna](/wiki/Skyrim:Senna "Skyrim:Senna"), who will advise you that "the temple is closed, but you may still receive your blessing from Dibella"—unless you enter the temple for the first time after participating in a drinking contest with [Sam Guevenne](/wiki/Skyrim:Sam_Guevenne "Skyrim:Sam Guevenne"); see the related [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember") for details.

There are statues of Dibella on either side of the entrance corridor and against each of the four pillars around the main chamber, which is used for worshipping and contains a stone pool filled with holy water on a raised platform in the center. It is classed as her altar where you will be required to prostrate yourself to receive your reward the [Agent of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Agent_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Agent of Dibella") passive ability, once you have completed [The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella") quest. Around the room are several stone shelves, sacks, hanging racks, and baskets holding both raw and cooked [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"), including [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"), [sweet rolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), [vegetables](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Fruit.2FVegetables "Skyrim:Food"); also bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). There are also many [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") used in alchemical preparation, as listed below; all these have been left as offerings. In the center of the north wall is a stone shelf with a [draught of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Strength "Skyrim:Draught of Strength") hidden behind a jug. All of the crockery throughout the temple is of the highest quality and, once the related quest is completed, they are free to take, along with all the other low value items. In the center of the south wall is a [shrine of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Shrine of Dibella"), granting the [Blessing of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessing_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Blessing of Dibella") (a +10 [bonus to Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Persuasion "Skyrim:Fortify Persuasion")) and removing any [diseases](/wiki/Skyrim:Diseases "Skyrim:Diseases"). During [A Night To Remember](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember"), there will also be two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a [giant's toe](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Toe "Skyrim:Giant's Toe"), and a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Repair_Supplies "Skyrim:Repair Supplies") on the floor, which you will need to take as part of the quest unless you pass a speech check with Senna. Until The Heart of Dibella is finished, the four aforementioned items during A Night To Remember are the only ones you can take for free.

|  |
| --- |
| Ingredients:  - 3 [Elves Ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") - 2 [Frost Mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") - 4 [Garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") - 3 [Juniper Berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") - 1 [Lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") - 1 [Tundra Cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") - 1 [Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") |

## Inner Sanctum

The door leading to the Inner Sanctum is expert-locked, beyond which are several flights of stairs leading down to closed door. Beyond this is the main room where, on your first visit, the other priestesses are performing a ceremony known as the "Exalted Protocol of the Dibellan Sybil", which enables them to locate the next Sybil.

On the right is a small area with many food sacks and barrels. Down a few steps is a stone table with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), a bottle of alto wine, and some [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), cheese and [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"). Beside this are more sacks and a basket containing a couple of cheese wheels. On the left of the entrance is a barrel containing ingredients and a path behind where the priestesses sit. There is a dresser on your right with a [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") flower, a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), two [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") coins, and a [silver emerald necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Emerald_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Emerald Necklace"). Further along on the left is a stone shelf with another medium coin purse and a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger") on top. Past this is a second dresser containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"). At the far end are more food sacks and opposite in the western corner is another small area with a barrel containing ingredients and a set of shelves holding several cheese wheels, several [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), and a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage").

Down the center of the room is a path with two sets of shelves at either end opposite each other. There is a circle of stone chairs around a table and with the high priestesses chair on a raised section against the north wall. On the table in the center of the chairs is a bowl containing a filled [greater soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Greater_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Greater Soul Gem"). The first set of shelves on the left hold a bottle of wine, a [potion of extra magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Extra Magicka"), a bowl containing an empty [common soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Common_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Common Soul Gem"), a [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing"), three dragon's tongue flowers, a small coin purse, three gold coins, a [flawless amethyst](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Amethyst "Skyrim:Flawless Amethyst"), and a [flawless sapphire](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Sapphire "Skyrim:Flawless Sapphire"). Opposite the shelves hold a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flower, a bunch of juniper berries, a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a [solution of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Strength "Skyrim:Solution of Strength"), a sprig of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), a bunch of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"), a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), a bottle of alto wine and a [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Magicka").

At the far end the set of shelves on the left holds a bottle of wine, a filled common soul gem, two pieces of cheese, sixteen common books, copies of *[Ghosts in the Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_in_the_Storm "Skyrim:Ghosts in the Storm")*, *[Mystery of Talara, v5](/wiki/Skyrim:Mystery_of_Talara,_v5 "Skyrim:Mystery of Talara, v5")*, *[The Tale of Dro'Zira](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Tale_of_Dro%27Zira "Skyrim:The Tale of Dro'Zira")* and a copy of the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Sun's Dawn, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Sun%27s_Dawn,_v2 "Skyrim:2920, Sun's Dawn, v2")*. The shelves on the right hold a bottle of [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison"), a potion of minor stamina, two [hagraven claws](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Claw "Skyrim:Hagraven Claw"), a bottle of alto wine, a steel dagger, a dragon's tongue flower, a bottle of wine, and a [draught of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Health "Skyrim:Draught of Health").

At the western end of the room, through another level-locked door, down a flight of stairs is another room, containing the [Statue to Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Statue_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Statue of Dibella") that [Degaine](/wiki/Skyrim:Degaine "Skyrim:Degaine") want you to steal. This must be completed prior to speaking with [Hamal](/wiki/Skyrim:Hamal "Skyrim:Hamal") and her instructing you to go to their new Sybil and to escort her to the temple unharmed. The room contains a central stone table with stone chairs at either end unusually facing away from the table with three empty [petty soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem") and a [Dwarven dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Dagger "Skyrim:Dwarven Dagger") on top and at the rear of the room a plinth with the statue on top.

## Notes

- Version 4.1.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch") replaces the 2 bottles of Alto Wine in the temple during A Night To Remember with Holy Water.

## Overview

Temple of Kynareth Exterior

**Temple of Kynareth** is a small temple in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") devoted to the goddess [Kynareth](/wiki/Lore:Kynareth "Lore:Kynareth").

[Danica Pure-Spring](/wiki/Skyrim:Danica_Pure-Spring "Skyrim:Danica Pure-Spring") and [Acolyte Jenssen](/wiki/Skyrim:Acolyte_Jenssen "Skyrim:Acolyte Jenssen") are tending the wounded in the main room. Danica explains that the war between the Imperials and Stormcloaks is overwhelming her with wounded, so she has been neglecting her priestess duties in order to heal them. Apparently one of her duties was to tend the Gildergreen (the large tree outside). When asked about the tree, she offers the quest [The Blessings of Nature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Blessings_of_Nature "Skyrim:The Blessings of Nature").

The interior of the Temple of Kynareth

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Danica Pure-Spring](/wiki/Skyrim:Danica_Pure-Spring "Skyrim:Danica Pure-Spring") [Trainer (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Master)")[Restoration (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Restoration (Master)")  [Acolyte Jenssen](/wiki/Skyrim:Acolyte_Jenssen "Skyrim:Acolyte Jenssen")  [Acolyte Aldren](/wiki/Skyrim:Acolyte_Aldren "Skyrim:Acolyte Aldren")\*\*[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup")  [Maurice Jondrelle](/wiki/Skyrim:Maurice_Jondrelle "Skyrim:Maurice Jondrelle")\*  [Rulnik Wind-Strider](/wiki/Skyrim:Rulnik_Wind-Strider "Skyrim:Rulnik Wind-Strider")\*\*[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup")  [Sickly Farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Sickly_Farmer "Skyrim:Sickly Farmer")  [Wounded Soldier](/wiki/Skyrim:Wounded_Soldier "Skyrim:Wounded Soldier") |

\* This person only appears once you have retrieved [Nettlebane](/wiki/Skyrim:Nettlebane "Skyrim:Nettlebane").
\*\* If [A Dying Wish](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dying_Wish "Skyrim:A Dying Wish") is started.

## Related Quests

- **[A Dying Wish](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dying_Wish "Skyrim:A Dying Wish")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup"): Make a bitter choice.
- **[The Blessings of Nature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Blessings_of_Nature "Skyrim:The Blessings of Nature")**: Restore the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") for [Danica Pure-Spring](/wiki/Skyrim:Danica_Pure-Spring "Skyrim:Danica Pure-Spring").

### Exterior

It is located in the wind district of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). There are several [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") bushes around the area and some stone benches to the southwest and around the Gildergreen to the southeast. The main doors open into the square where the Gildergreen is.

### Temple of Kynareth

There are two entrances into the temple, the main entrance is over a small bridge to the southeast and the other is from the southwest. Around the outside of the central room are a series of wooden benches with three owned [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing "Skyrim:Healing") altars around a tiled central area with a large raised cross mosaic in the floor and shallow water filling the areas between the legs of the cross. The healing altars are to the southwest with a [wounded soldier](/wiki/Skyrim:Wounded_Soldier "Skyrim:Wounded Soldier"), northwest and northeast with a [sickly farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Sickly_Farmer "Skyrim:Sickly Farmer"). The sick and injured are treated and prayed over by [Danica Pure-Spring](/wiki/Skyrim:Danica_Pure-Spring "Skyrim:Danica Pure-Spring") and [Acolyte Jenssen](/wiki/Skyrim:Acolyte_Jenssen "Skyrim:Acolyte Jenssen"). There are a couple of [health potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), a plate and a bunch of lavender to the right of the northwest healing altar. There are six planters around the room each holding two lavender bushes.

In the middle of the northwest wall is a narrow table with a [Shrine of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Shrine of Kynareth") on top. To the southwest there are two semi-partitioned areas separated by the entrance, one with a wooden bench, the other a small bedroom with a single owned bed used by Acolyte Jenssen and a narrow table with a level-locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") underneath and a [goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"), a [plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate"), a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge") on top. To the northeast is another semi-partitioned area with an owned single bed used by Danica Pure-Spring, with an end table beside it. On the end table is a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl") and goblet. Along the northeast wall is a small wardrobe with more bowls, goblets and a plate on top, with a bookcase beside it holding various strength [healing potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a [jug](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug "Skyrim:Jug"), thirteen common books and a copy of the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Withershins](/wiki/Skyrim:Withershins "Skyrim:Withershins")*. Opposite the bed is a table with a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a plate, a goblet, some common books, and various healing and health [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions").

## Notes

- Activating the Shrine of Kynareth cures all diseases, bestows the [Blessing of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessings#Blessing_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Blessings") for 8 hours, and removes any other shrine blessing.
- A copy of the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Withershins](/wiki/Skyrim:Withershins "Skyrim:Withershins")* can be found in the northeast room on the bookshelf.

## Bugs

- The bed markers in the temple have no pillows, causing NPCs to have their heads suspended over nothing.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Temple of Mara

## Overview

The temple's exterior

**Temple of Mara** is a temple in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") devoted to the [Aedric](/wiki/Lore:Aedra "Lore:Aedra") goddess [Mara](/wiki/Lore:Mara "Lore:Mara"), one of the Eight [Divines](/wiki/Lore:Divines "Lore:Divines") and goddess of mortal understanding, love and compassion.

It is home to three Priests of Mara: [Briehl](/wiki/Skyrim:Briehl "Skyrim:Briehl"), [Dinya Balu](/wiki/Skyrim:Dinya_Balu "Skyrim:Dinya Balu"), and [Maramal](/wiki/Skyrim:Maramal "Skyrim:Maramal"). [Alessandra](/wiki/Skyrim:Alessandra "Skyrim:Alessandra"), a Priestess of [Arkay](/wiki/Lore:Arkay "Lore:Arkay") who spends her days in the temple's [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Riften) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Riften)"), also lives here.

## Residents

| Name |
| --- |
| [Alessandra](/wiki/Skyrim:Alessandra "Skyrim:Alessandra")  [Briehl](/wiki/Skyrim:Briehl "Skyrim:Briehl")  [Dinya Balu](/wiki/Skyrim:Dinya_Balu "Skyrim:Dinya Balu")  [Maramal](/wiki/Skyrim:Maramal "Skyrim:Maramal") |

## Related Quests

- **[The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love")**: Help the Temple of Mara spread the cause of love throughout Skyrim.
- **[The Bonds of Matrimony](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bonds_of_Matrimony "Skyrim:The Bonds of Matrimony")**: Find someone in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") to [marry](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").
- **[Spread the Love](/wiki/Skyrim:Spread_the_Love "Skyrim:Spread the Love")**: Distribute religious [literature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warmth_of_Mara "Skyrim:The Warmth of Mara") to the citizens of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").

### Exterior

It is located between [Riftweald Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Riftweald_Manor "Skyrim:Riftweald Manor") and [Black-Briar Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Manor "Skyrim:Black-Briar Manor") in the eastern part of the city. It has its own courtyard with a flight of stairs flanked by lit braziers leading up to the entrance. The [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Riften) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Riften)") is beneath the temple.

### Temple of Mara

The temple's interior

The main entrance leads directly into the main room for worship with the centerpiece of the temple, a statue of [Mara](/wiki/Lore:Mara "Lore:Mara"), against the east wall. There are rows of wooden benches facing the altar in front of the statue. On the altar is a copy of *[Gods and Worship](/wiki/Skyrim:Gods_and_Worship "Skyrim:Gods and Worship")* and a [Shrine of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Mara "Skyrim:Shrine of Mara"). When activated, the shrine confers the [Blessing of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessing_of_Mara "Skyrim:Blessing of Mara"), which reduces the cost of [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") spells by 10%. There are two additional shrines in the main room on narrow tables, one on either side of the entrance at the rear of the room. At either side of the statue of Mara are planters containing a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), a [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") plant, and [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") and [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") plants. Above these hang banners of Mara. In front of the altar is a long master-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest").

Against the east wall are a wooden bench and two sets of shelves which hold copies of *[Aedra and Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Aedra_and_Daedra "Skyrim:Aedra and Daedra")*, *[A Children's Anuad](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Children%27s_Anuad "Skyrim:A Children's Anuad")*, *[The Monomyth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Monomyth "Skyrim:The Monomyth")*, and *[Trials of St. Alessia](/wiki/Skyrim:Trials_of_St._Alessia "Skyrim:Trials of St. Alessia")*. Beside the books are a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"), a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), several [cups](/wiki/Skyrim:Cup "Skyrim:Cup") and [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"), and a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute") leaning against one of the shelves. There are two doors: one to the northeast and the other around the corner in the northwestern corner. Against the south wall is another wooden bench and set of shelves which hold a complete set of all eight volumes of *[The Song of Pelinal](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Song_of_Pelinal "Skyrim:The Song of Pelinal")*, a couple of [candlesticks](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlestick "Skyrim:Candlestick"), and goblets. A third door is in the southwestern corner. Opposite that door, in the southeast corner, is an alcove with a couple of barrels of [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food").

Briehl and Dinya Balu's sleeping quarters

The door to the southwest leads into the bedroom used by two of the priests, [Briehl](/wiki/Skyrim:Briehl "Skyrim:Briehl") and [Dinya Balu](/wiki/Skyrim:Dinya_Balu "Skyrim:Dinya Balu"). It consists of two single beds coming out from the west wall, a small round wooden table and two chairs against the south wall, and a set of shelves against the east wall. On the table rests a copy of *[A Kiss, Sweet Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Kiss,_Sweet_Mother "Skyrim:A Kiss, Sweet Mother")*, a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Ceremony "Skyrim:Argonian Ceremony") from [Talen-Jei](/wiki/Skyrim:Talen-Jei "Skyrim:Talen-Jei") to [Drifa](/wiki/Skyrim:Drifa "Skyrim:Drifa") related to the quest [Sealing the Deal](/wiki/Skyrim:Sealing_the_Deal "Skyrim:Sealing the Deal"). The set of shelves holds a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), and several pieces of cheese.

The door in the northeastern corner leads to a cooking and dining area with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand against the west wall with a couple of food barrels to the left. A cupboard, a round wooden table, and a set of shelves all line the east wall. The cupboard holds a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") and a bottle of alto wine. On the table are two [baked potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), and cheese. On the shelves are five [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), a couple of loaves of bread, and several pieces of cheese. Hanging from the ceiling are two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, three bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), and three bunches of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). There is also a door to the south that opens into Maramal's bedroom. There is an owned double bed coming out from the middle of the south wall with a dresser at its foot. On the dresser are a bunch of lavender along with purple, blue, and [red mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"). To the right of the bed is a chair. A [ruined book](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book"), a potion of minor healing, a potion of minor stamina, and a bottle of alto wine rest on the table by the east wall. Beside the door against the north wall is a wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes").

The third door in the northwestern corner of the main room opens to a flight of stairs leading down to the cellar, with a couple of food barrels beside the top of the stairs and more at the bottom of the stairs in a storage area. There is a door in the east wall and another in the south wall. To the right of the second of these is a cupboard and set of shelves. The cupboard only holds clutter, while the shelves hold three bottles of Nord mead, two bottles of alto wine and a bottle of wine. Under the stairs is a large vat and a pile of firewood. Hanging from the ceiling are three [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), three garlic braids, two bunches of elves ear, and a bunch of frost mirriam.

The door to the south leads to the *Hall of the Dead*. The door to the east opens into a bedroom used by [Alessandra](/wiki/Skyrim:Alessandra "Skyrim:Alessandra"), Priestess of [Arkay](/wiki/Lore:Arkay "Lore:Arkay"). This bedroom consists of an owned single bed coming out from the south wall, with an end table to the right and a chair to the left. On the end table is a bottle of wine. Against the east wall is a wardrobe and against the north wall is a long wooden table and chair. The table holds a ruined book, a bottle of wine, a baked potato, some bread, and cheese.

## Notes

- If you spare [Erandur](/wiki/Skyrim:Erandur "Skyrim:Erandur") at the end of [Waking Nightmare](/wiki/Skyrim:Waking_Nightmare "Skyrim:Waking Nightmare") and bring him here afterwards, he will comment: *"I've always wanted to make a pilgrimage here to the Temple of Mara. Thank you for bringing me here... you've made me quite happy."*

# Skyrim:Temple of Miraak

## Overview

This article is about the location. For the quest, see [The Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:The Temple of Miraak").

The Temple of Miraak

The **Temple of Miraak** is a [Nordic temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Temples "Skyrim:Temples") west of [Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall") containing [cultists](/wiki/Skyrim:Cultist "Skyrim:Cultist"), [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). It contains two zones: *[Temple of Miraak](#Temple_of_Miraak)* and *[Temple of Miraak Sanctum](#Temple_of_Miraak_Sanctum)*.

Its [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaches part of the [Dragon Aspect](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Aspect "Skyrim:Dragon Aspect") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). The temple is dedicated to the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)"). The Tree Stone is in the center of the exterior structure. Once cleansed by completing the quest [At the Summit of Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:At_the_Summit_of_Apocrypha "Skyrim:At the Summit of Apocrypha"), this stone gives you the power to [make](/wiki/Skyrim:Root_of_Power "Skyrim:Root of Power") all [spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Spells "Skyrim:Spells") cost 75% less to cast for 60 seconds. Once you use this power, it disappears from the Powers menu, and you must return to the Tree Stone to obtain it again.

## Related Quests

- **[The Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:The Temple of Miraak")**: Uncover the source of [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)")'s power in the Temple of Miraak.

### Exterior

The Temple of Miraak

The main approach to the temple is from the west. Climbing the wide flights of stairs past the bones of fallen dragons, you will pass under a pair of large stone arches fitted with construction scaffolding. [Herkja](/wiki/Skyrim:Herkja "Skyrim:Herkja"), [Sirkjorg](/wiki/Skyrim:Sirkjorg "Skyrim:Sirkjorg"), and three [reavers](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver "Skyrim:Reaver") are working on the arches. They take no notice of you, as all are enthralled by Miraak through his control over the Tree Stone in the center of the compound.

At the top of the stairs are two stone lookout arches, one pointing southeast and the other pointing southwest. Wooden scaffolding is set against the circular temple wall to the north, allowing two more reavers access to their work. Ascend the wooden ramps to overlook an amphitheater, with the Tree Stone in the center. Approaching the stone will complete the quest [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_(quest) "Skyrim:Dragonborn (quest)") and start the quest [The Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:The Temple of Miraak"). However, activating the stone will cause you to become enthralled as well; break free by moving away from the area.

Frea pleading

The Tree Stone

As you approach the area around the stone, you will hear [Frea](/wiki/Skyrim:Frea "Skyrim:Frea") pleading with the enthralled [Oslaf](/wiki/Skyrim:Oslaf "Skyrim:Oslaf") and [Yrsa](/wiki/Skyrim:Yrsa "Skyrim:Yrsa") to leave the temple. Speak with her to learn she is here to save or avenge her people. When you tell her Miraak tried to have you killed, she will say you both must find a way inside. At this point, part of the circular stone floor around the stone will drop to reveal a ramp, and two cultists will emerge from the temple entrance at the bottom and attack. Once they have been dealt with, enter the temple.

### Temple of Miraak

The circular table

The entrance leads into a passage leading north. The first room on the left contains a large circular stone table with five stone thrones and two seated lootable skeletons, with a third lootable skeleton on the floor. The table holds a random [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"). Small recessed shelves lining the walls hold a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl") containing an [emerald](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald "Skyrim:Emerald"), a [garnet](/wiki/Skyrim:Garnet "Skyrim:Garnet"), and a [flawless amethyst](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Amethyst "Skyrim:Flawless Amethyst"), a random [potion of resist magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Magic "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Magic"), and two random [potions of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing").

Returning to the passage, the first room on the right contains a lit brazier between separate areas to the left and right. The area on the left has four cages suspended over a fire, three of which contain [burnt corpses](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Burnt_Corpse "Skyrim:Containers"). The area on the right has a stone table holding a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and an unlootable skeleton crushed by fallen masonry. Returning again to the passage, the next room on the left contains a broken stone table in front of a wooden wall, with a chest and a set of shelves holding three [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison") on the other side of the wall.

Enemies

The passage descends a short flight of stairs and turns west, leading to a room with two patrolling cultists. Just inside the room is a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that triggers a [poison dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap"). In the southwest and southeast corners are ominous upright sarcophagi. Not surprisingly, the southwest sarcophagus bursts open to release a draugr. The path continues down a flight of stairs to the west, turning south into a semicircular room like those found in many [barrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") across Skyrim. Along the east wall is a set of shelves holding an empty [common soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Common_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Common Soul Gem"). On the dais in the middle of the room are two soul gem stands, one of which holds another empty common soul gem. The room also contains two [urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") and four [burial urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn"). The next room widens to the left, with two pressure plates activating a [battering ram](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram") to the left and straight ahead. The path continues to the northwest, descending a flight of stairs to a portcullis which may be raised by using the pull chain to the right. Beyond the portcullis is a huge square chamber lit by four large braziers hanging from the ceiling, with a stairwell leading down into a large sunken area in the center. Four cages containing lootable skeletons hang from the ceiling as well.

There may be trouble ahead...

To the northeast is a short flight of stairs leading up to a balcony, but as the upper steps have collapsed, the balcony cannot be reached directly. Instead, climb to the landing, then turn east to find a lootable skeleton and a potion of healing at the foot of the angled stone buttress. Climb the buttress, and jump onto the balcony from there. The balcony features a chest and a throne overlooking the room.

From the balcony

Returning to the main level, along the east wall are two sets of shelves holding two random [potions of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka") and a random [potion of extra magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Extra Magicka"). A stone table nearby holds a [dead draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Draugr "Skyrim:Containers"). At the top of the central stairwell near the west wall are three upright sarcophagi. One sarcophagus is already open, with the draugr dead on the ground, and the other two will burst open to release two hostile draugr. This will alert the three cultists at the bottom of the stairwell to your presence.

Descend the stairwell to the bottom, where five dead draugr are stacked in and near a cart. Opposite the corpses is a stone table holding three bowls of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal") and a bowl containing a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulb and two [grass pods](/wiki/Skyrim:Grass_Pod "Skyrim:Grass Pod"), with two urns next to the table. The path continues to the north before descending a flight of stairs to the crypt area. A handle on a plinth raises the nearby portcullis at the start of the crypt. Beyond the portcullis, a draugr slumbers in a burial alcove to the northeast. Proceed northeast, passing a lootable skeleton on the ground and two more dead draugr in the alcoves. Another slumbering draugr is ahead, and two more will be alerted by any fighting. Near the end of the section leading northeast are three urns and a burial urn near three sets of shelves holding two [salt piles](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a bowl of [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts"), a random [potion of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength"), a random [enchanter's potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanter%27s_Potion "Skyrim:Enchanter's Potion"), and a bowl containing three potions of healing.

East of the shelves, a sitting draugr will awaken as you approach. Two dead draugr are in alcoves nearby, and to the northwest is a chest flanked by two more dead draugr on stone tables, one of which has been broken by fallen rubble. Returning to the main passage, a pressure plate activates a [spike wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall"), and a second pressure plate activates two battering rams ahead and to the left.

Five draugr attacking

Just past the second pressure plate is an intersection where the path branches to the north and the northwest. Up to five draugr will converge on the junction and attack. Nine dead draugr are stacked in the intersection, with three more in a cart. Both branches merge again ahead, so take the path on the right north past another dead draugr in an alcove to an urn and a chest. The path then turns west to join the end of the northwest branch, which is guarded by a draugr. Ahead to the west is a pressure plate in front of a set of iron doors that causes the doors to close and [flamethrowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Flamethrower_Statues "Skyrim:Flamethrower Statues") to fire from the walls. There is just enough room between the pressure plate and the flames to avoid damage. Beyond the doors, a series of ten [swinging blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Blades "Skyrim:Swinging Blades") begin to scythe across the wide corridor ahead. The lever at the end of the corridor will stop the swinging blades and raise the adjacent wall of spears, allowing you to proceed. On the ground around the spears are the remains of a [puzzle door](/wiki/Skyrim:Puzzle_Door "Skyrim:Puzzle Door") that had clearly been broken open.

Follow the passage down to the west, then south to a set of iron doors. Beyond the doors is a room with rubble and a barred window to the south ahead, and a portcullis to the west. Move around the rubble to find a concealed door on the east wall with a pull chain to the right. The door reveals a tunnel that leads to a small room with a chest and a stone table holding an empty [black soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Black Soul Gem"), a filled black soul gem, and a bowl containing an empty [petty soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem"), an empty [lesser soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem"), and an empty common soul gem. Returning to the previous room, beyond the doorway to the south is an upright sarcophagus that bursts open to release a leveled draugr. Follow the corridor to the east and north to the two barred windows, where a handle on a plinth raises the portcullis.

Beyond the portcullis are three strings of [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") in front of a wooden ramp that falls into place as you approach. Three more wooden ramps to the south on the far side of the room also drop down to reveal two high-level draugr and a high-level cultist. A pressure plate at the bottom of the entry ramp activates a poison dart trap, as do three more pressure plates at the base of each of the three ramps to the south. All three ramps ascend to the same foyer, where a set of iron doors leads to the *Temple of Miraak Sanctum*.

### Temple of Miraak Sanctum

Ambush!

Entrance tunnel

The entrance leads into a passage that descends a short flight of stairs to a bone-strewn caged walkway crossing over a large room below. Six skeletons will arrive as you cross the walkway and start looking for you. On the far side of the walkway, the passage rises to the west before descending a short flight of stairs to the south. As soon as you start to descend, a pair of battering rams will swing across the passage, and two draugr will emerge from upright sarcophagi on either side. A pressure plate in the middle of the passage also activates the rams. Proceed through a round cage, and when you emerge, look to the south to find a partly buried cage section covering a hole large enough to enter.

Down below

At the bottom of the hole, continue up a flight of stairs and east and north around a corner to a doorway. Beyond the doorway is a small room containing a set of sideboards holding a random [paralysis poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Paralysis_Poison "Skyrim:Paralysis Poison"), a random [potion of invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Brief_Invisibility "Skyrim:Potion of Brief Invisibility"), two empty petty soul gems, a [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") spell tome, eight loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), a small coin purse, two medium coin purses, an [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") spell tome, an empty [greater soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Greater_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Greater Soul Gem"), and a potion of healing. The path continues east and north down a short flight of stairs to rejoin the previous main passage. Ahead to the northeast is the room below the caged walkway, patrolled by two cultists. To the northeast is a short flight of stairs leading up to a small balcony, where an upright sarcophagus will burst open to release a draugr. Stairs along the west wall descend north to the lowest level, which features another upright sarcophagus concealing a hostile draugr, a broken sarcophagus containing a dead draugr, three burial urns next to the broken sarcophagus, and a random enchanted [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword") on the ground near a skeletal arm. Returning to the upper level, continue north down a flight of stairs along the east wall by the small balcony. A pressure plate at the top of the stairs activates a battering ram ahead.

The word wall

Proceed north and west to a lit brazier with stairs leading down on either side. Descending the stairs, you will hear the sounds of a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") which teaches part of the [Dragon Aspect](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Aspect "Skyrim:Dragon Aspect") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). In the small room at the bottom of the stairs, the skeleton of a dragon hangs from the ceiling over a chest next to an upright sarcophagus ahead, the word wall is to the left, and a row of five more upright sarcophagi is to the right. Learning the word causes all five sarcophagi to the right to burst open and release three leveled draugr and two dead draugr, while the [Gatekeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Gatekeeper "Skyrim:Gatekeeper"), a unique draugr carrying the [Temple of Miraak key](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak_Key "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak Key"), emerges from the sarcophagus next to the chest. The Gatekeeper's sarcophagus contains a locked set of iron doors that requires the key. It is possible to avoid a difficult fight by using rune magic to cause each of the sarcophagi to open individually before learning the word.

Beyond the doors in the sarcophagus is a room containing a long stone table with two thrones, both occupied by dead draugr. The corpse on the left wears an [ancient Nord helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Helmet "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Helmet"), and the corpse on the right holds an [ancient Nord battle axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Battle_Axe "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Battle Axe"). Behind the thrones is another locked set of iron doors that requires the same key, beyond which is a narrow room with a window into the next room ahead. Continue to the left to a large dining room containing several sets of shelves and two long stone tables. There is nothing of interest in this room, so exit in the northwest corner.

The kitchen

Follow the corridor as it leads north past another narrow corridor on the right to end in a kitchen. Several sets of shelves and sideboard hold a variety of alchemical ingredients, including two [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flowers, two samples of [creep cluster](/wiki/Skyrim:Creep_Cluster "Skyrim:Creep Cluster"), a bowl of [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts"), four salt piles, a bowl containing a [chicken's egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), a [pine thrush egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"), and a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"), a sample of [bear claws](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Claws "Skyrim:Bear Claws"), a bowl of [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts"), two [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") flowers, and three bowls of bone meal. On a work table is a potion of healing, two bowls of [spriggan sap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan_Sap "Skyrim:Spriggan Sap"), a salt pile, and a sample of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"). Hanging from the ceiling are four bunches of dried elves ear, four bunches of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), and four garlic braids. In the northeast corner is a set of shelves holding a random potion, a random [skill potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Alteration "Skyrim:Potion of Alteration"), an empty black soul gem, and a bowl containing a filled lesser soul gem and an empty greater soul gem. Along the east wall is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") built into a sideboard.

Return to the nearby narrow corridor through either the southwest or southeast doorways. In the alcove near the east end of the corridor is a handle on a plinth that opens a concealed door in the south wall of the dining room. Follow the twisting tunnel beyond the door to a room with a circular grate in the floor covering a spiral staircase. Two sets of shelves in the room hold three potions of magicka, two samples of frost mirriam, a sample of elves ear, and six [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot"). In the southwest corner is a doorway to another room with a [trap door](/wiki/Skyrim:Trap_Door "Skyrim:Trap Door") in the floor over another spiral staircase. Near the west wall, beneath a bizarre three-headed relief, is a handle on a plinth.

Trap door handle

Pulling the handle opens the trap door, allowing you to descend the staircase. At the bottom is a path that leads past an urn and a sideboard holding two filled random soul gems to the first spiral staircase seen in the previous room. At the bottom of this staircase, the path continues to the west and turns south. Another handle on a plinth at the end of the corridor lowers the structure ahead to reveal a spiral stone staircase leading down. At the bottom is a set of wooden doors.

Dragon skeleton display

Beyond the doors is a dragon head statue. Continue south around the statue to a large room where a wide flight of stairs lined with stone sculptures rises ahead. Several draugr patrol the room. A dragon skeleton is arranged in a macabre display in the middle of the stairs, with another hanging above. Two [tripwires](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") on the right side of the stairs activate two sets of [falling boulders](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders"), while another tripwire on the left side activates a third set of boulders. Four draugr and four skeletons guard the south end of the room near the top of the stairs. At the top, the boss chest is at the base of a large unusual statue. Behind the statue is a pull chain that opens a rotating door.

Beyond the door is a twisting tunnel that leads to a strange circular room with a pedestal in the center holding the *[Black Book: Waking Dreams](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Waking_Dreams_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Waking Dreams (book)")*. A second doorway to the east connects to another twisting tunnel that leads to an exterior exit, which emerges north-northeast of the temple a short distance southwest of the [Wind Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Wind_Stone "Skyrim:Wind Stone").

## Notes

- The Tree Stone also appears in *[Bloodmoon](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Tree_Stone "Bloodmoon:Tree Stone")*.

## Bugs

- Some draugr that emerge from sarcophagi, including the one near the end of the *Temple of Miraak*, may fall from the sarcophagi as dead draugr deathlords.
- The Temple is not visible on the game map or from a distance on the ground.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
- The two Cultists outside the Temple may respawn despite the dungeon being classed as a "no reset zone". They may also never despawn once the dungeon is clear.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.8, fixes this bug.

  Temple of Miraak Sanctum

# Skyrim:Temple of Talos

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Temple: Temple of Talos ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Temple+of+Talos)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| WindhelmTempleofTalos | |
| Region | |
| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | |
| Location | |
| [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") | |

The Temple of Talos in the city of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm")

The **Temple of Talos** is located just northwest of [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").

After the Empire signed the [White-Gold Concordat](/wiki/Lore:White-Gold_Concordat "Lore:White-Gold Concordat") with the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor"), the worship of [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Talos "Lore:Talos") was outlawed. However under the protection of [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak"), it is now the only formal Temple of Talos in Skyrim.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Jora](/wiki/Skyrim:Jora "Skyrim:Jora")  [Lortheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Lortheim "Skyrim:Lortheim") |

## Temple of Talos

.jpg)

Interior

It contains a [shrine of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Talos "Skyrim:Shrine of Talos") in front of the statue of [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Talos "Lore:Talos") in the main room with a row of five wooden benches facing it. It is tended by [Lortheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Lortheim "Skyrim:Lortheim") and [Jora](/wiki/Skyrim:Jora "Skyrim:Jora"), who also reside in the single sleeping quarters behind the statue. There are arched doorways on either side of the statue that lead to the sleeping quarters. They consist of an owned double bed coming out from the south wall with a set of shelves against the east wall holding various clutter, a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). Opposite, against the west wall are a series of three wall shelves holding copies of *[Aedra and Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Aedra_and_Daedra "Skyrim:Aedra and Daedra")*, *[The Song of Pelinal, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Song_of_Pelinal,_v1 "Skyrim:The Song of Pelinal, v1")*, *[v4](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Song_of_Pelinal,_v4 "Skyrim:The Song of Pelinal, v4")* and *[v5](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Song_of_Pelinal,_v5 "Skyrim:The Song of Pelinal, v5")*, *[The Amulet of Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Amulet_of_Kings "Skyrim:The Amulet of Kings")*, *[The Monomyth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Monomyth "Skyrim:The Monomyth")*, *[A Kiss, Sweet Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Kiss,_Sweet_Mother "Skyrim:A Kiss, Sweet Mother")* and two copies of *[A Children's Anuad](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Children%27s_Anuad "Skyrim:A Children's Anuad")*. There is also a chair under the shelves.

Jora will happily reveal that the Shatter-Shields, [Hillevi Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillevi_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:Hillevi Cruel-Sea") and Ulfric Stormcloak frequent the temple.

## Notes

- The temple will remain open for Talos worship, even after the [Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm").

## Bugs

- After completing Battle for Windhelm, the Stormcloak banners don't change for the Imperial one. **?**
