# Skyrim:Temple of the Divines

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Temple: Temple of the Divines ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Temple+of+the+Divines)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| SolitudeTempleoftheDivines | |
| Location | |
| In [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), by [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour") | |

Entrance to the Temple of the Divines in Solitude

The **Temple of the Divines** is the main temple of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") and [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"), housing [shrines](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines "Skyrim:Shrines") to the [Eight Divines](/wiki/Lore:Eight_Divines "Lore:Eight Divines").

It is located on the eastern side of the Castle Dour's courtyard, northwest of the Blue Palace.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Freir](/wiki/Skyrim:Freir "Skyrim:Freir")  [Rorlund](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorlund "Skyrim:Rorlund")  [Silana Petreia](/wiki/Skyrim:Silana_Petreia "Skyrim:Silana Petreia") |

## Related Quests

- **[Double-Edged](/wiki/Skyrim:Double-Edged "Skyrim:Double-Edged")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Leather "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Leather"): Determine the fate of a Thalmor agent.
- **[Gift of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Gift_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Gift of Kynareth")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail "Skyrim:Lord's Mail"): Recover a legendary [Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail_(item) "Skyrim:Lord's Mail (item)") and obtain the blessing of [Kynareth](/wiki/Lore:Kynareth "Lore:Kynareth").
- **[Bound Until Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death")**: Assassinate [Vittoria Vici](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici") at her own wedding.
- **[The Wolf Queen Awakened](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen_Awakened "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen Awakened")**: Potema must be stopped.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Temple of the Divines

In front of the entrance is a private courtyard with two arches providing entry from [Castle Dour's](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour") courtyard. One to the south and one to the west. This second gated arch is blocked by the gate being lowered after starting the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") quest [Bound Until Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death") Where you interrupt the wedding of [Vittoria Vici](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici"). In addition to a couple of rows of wooden benches facing two thrones, once the quest is started there are [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") plants in pot either side of the thrones, other pots planted with [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes and [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") plants, and wooden tables against the side walls of the courtyard holding platters and bowls of various foods, including [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), [tomatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato"), [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), [boiled creme treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"), [sweet rolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), [honey nut treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat"), etc. and bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). These all remain for the remainder of the game. The entrance to the temple is never locked. Everything inside the temple is marked as owned and taking anything will be considered stealing.

Temple shrine room

Entering brings you directly into the main chamber with the eight shrines at the far end in individual alcoves with an empty alcove where the [shrine of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Talos "Skyrim:Shrine of Talos") stood. There are rows of wooden benches facing the shrines for visitors to sit in worship. At the rear of the chamber is a narrow table on your left with a sprig of snowberries on top and to your right is a small wardrobe containing [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") with a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health") on top. Beside this is a chair and low table with a common [book](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books") on top and In the southern corner is another narrow wooden table with a [chaurus egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs"), a [hagraven claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Claw "Skyrim:Hagraven Claw") and a stone bowl containing a bunch of lavender, a sprig of snowberries, a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") and a [purple](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") and [blue mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"). A vase to the left holds another bunch of lavender. [Freir](/wiki/Skyrim:Freir "Skyrim:Freir") spends much of her time standing at the rear of the room welcoming any and all worshippers.

There are stairs up to the northwest and southeast. Beyond a large pillar is a [juniper](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper "Skyrim:Juniper") tree and as you move forward several pots contain snowberry bushes or [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flowers. Part way along the southeast wall is an open crate on the floor containing a complete set of *[The Song of Pelinal](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Song_of_Pelinal "Skyrim:The Song of Pelinal")*, with an extra copy of *[v3](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Song_of_Pelinal,_v3 "Skyrim:The Song of Pelinal, v3")*. Near the front is an area to the northwest with a small wardrobe, another snowberry bush in a pot, and a narrow wooden table with a stone bowl on top containing a [potion of extra magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Extra Magicka") and a potion of health. There are stairs leading down to the southwest, in the corner. To the southeast is a short corridor leading to another small wardrobe and snowberry bush.

Climbing the stairs to the northwest, there is a small vase holding a bunch of tundra cotton and to the right stacks of eleven common books part way up the stairs against the wall. At the top of the stairs, on your right is a small unit holding a deathbell flower, a bunch of lavender and a copy of the *[Argonian Account, Book 2](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Account,_Book_2 "Skyrim:Argonian Account, Book 2")*. further along on the right is a small area with a chair, low table and narrow wooden table with an opening to look down upon the main chamber below. The low table has a plate of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and cheese on top, while the narrow table has two [baked potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a sweet roll, a cheese wheel and two [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") on top. Further to the northeast are the sleeping quarters containing three single owned beds; one in the southern corner, one coming out from the middle of the northeast wall and one coming out from the middle of the northwest wall. In the eastern corner there is a large round table and two chairs with a plate of bread and cheese and a [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration") on top the table. Beside this is an opening, through which you can see a potion of regeneration on a ledge half way up the wall opposite. The use of the [Telekinesis](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis "Skyrim:Telekinesis") spell makes retrieving it simple. To the left of the table is a narrow table and wash basin. To the right of the second bed is an end table with a potion of health and a [draught of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Strength "Skyrim:Draught of Strength") on top. In the northern corner is another wash basin, with small wardrobes either side, along the northeast and northwest walls, both have a common book on top, but the one against the northeast wall also has a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") on top. There is a basket by the wash basin containing another small coin purse. To the left of the third bed is an end table and to the southwest is a small area containing two tall wardrobes and a dresser containing fine clothes and an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot.

Climbing the stairs to the southeast are the living quarters. At the top of the stairs there is an end table to the left and a small cupboard to the right with a potion of regeneration on top. Against the southeast wall is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand with wooden benches either side. On the left is a small cupboard and bookcase holding a bottle of alto wine, a potion of health, five common books and a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute") and with a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum") on top. Beside this is a long wooden table coming out from the northwest wall with a bench and chair on either side. On the table is a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish") steak, a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a loaf of bread, several pieces of cheese, a bottles of alto wine, a bunch of tundra cotton, and a potion of regeneration. To the right are more openings to see down to the chamber below. In the northern corner is a large round table and chair with two salmon steaks, a loaf of bread, a pieces of cheese and a bottle of alto wine on the table top. A small cupboard is beside this. Another small cupboard is further along the wall to the right with a vase holding a bunch of tundra cotton on top. To the right of this is a narrow wooden table with a stone bowl containing a bunch of lavender and a potion of regeneration on top. To the southeast is a door that leads out onto the wall surrounding the courtyard.

At the bottom of the stairs descending to the southwest is a room with a gate opposite that requires a key to open. To the left of this is a long wooden table and bench. On the table is a salmon steak, a slaughterfish steak, a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), two [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), a loaf of bread and an [empty wine bottle](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle"). Above the table are two wall shelves with a potion of health and a potion of regeneration, two [goat cheese wheels](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), a loaf of bread and five more empty wine bottles. In the eastern corner are a stack of five [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels and a door that opens into another bedroom containing a single owned bed in the eastern corner with an end table holding a common book and an empty wine bottle beside it. Above the head of the bed are a pair of wall shelves holding a set of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") and several [hats](/wiki/Skyrim:Hat "Skyrim:Hat"). At the foot of the bed is a [firebrand wine case](/wiki/Skyrim:Firebrand_Wine_Case "Skyrim:Firebrand Wine Case") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots"). In the southern corner is a square table with a common book and three empty wine bottles on top and a tall wardrobe containing clothes. In the northern corner is another tall wardrobe with more empty wine bottles on top. There are several food sacks near the door.

The [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Potema%27s_Catacombs_Key "Skyrim:Potema's Catacombs Key") to open the locked gate is given to you by [Styrr](/wiki/Skyrim:Styrr "Skyrim:Styrr"), the priest of [Arkay](/wiki/Lore:Arkay "Lore:Arkay"), who looks after the [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Solitude) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Solitude)") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). The key is given near the beginning of [The Wolf Queen Awakened](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen_Awakened "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen Awakened") quest initiated by [Falk Firebeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Falk_Firebeard "Skyrim:Falk Firebeard"). Beyond the gate is a storage area with a food barrel immediately on your right with a [potion of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka") on top. In front is a set of shelves holding an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese") and a [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel") and beside this is a cupboard holding only clutter. On the left is another set of shelves and a cupboard both of which hold nothing much of interest. There is a round wooden table and two chairs in the middle of the room, a dresser to the southeast with an iron dagger on top. In an alcove to the southwest is a large vat. In the corner is a fenced area holding many [Honningbrew mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead") barrels. Opposite this is another set of shelves filled with empty wine bottles. To the southeast is a corridor with a hole in the wall at the far end leading into [Potema's Catacombs](/wiki/Skyrim:Potema%27s_Catacombs "Skyrim:Potema's Catacombs"). On the right is a stack of crates with a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") on top.

## Notes

- The shrine to the Ninth Divine, [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Talos "Lore:Talos"), is not present due to the ban on Talos worship as demanded by the [White-Gold Concordat](/wiki/Lore:White-Gold_Concordat "Lore:White-Gold Concordat"). There is an empty alcove where his shrine sat before being removed. However, a shrine to him will later appear within if you join the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") and [capture Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Solitude "Skyrim:Battle for Solitude").
- The [Prima guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide") states that it was formerly called the **Temple of the Nine Divines**.

## Bugs

- After completing Battle for Solitude, the Imperial banners don't change for the Stormcloak ones. **?**
- Some of the items are owned by the MarkarthHagsCureFaction, making them free to take if you help [Bothela](/wiki/Skyrim:Bothela "Skyrim:Bothela"). **?**
- The priests here don't perform their package routines properly due to the packages targeting the wrong markers.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.7, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Temple

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

This article is about the building in Raven Rock. For the heretical cult added by Ghosts of the Tribunal, see [Tribunal Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Tribunal_Temple "Skyrim:Tribunal Temple").

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Temple: Temple ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Temple)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC2RRTemple | |
| Region | |
| [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") | |
| Location | |
| [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") | |

Temple

The **Temple** is a [Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") place of worship in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").

It is up a flight of stairs opposite the pier between [Morvayn Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Morvayn_Manor "Skyrim:Morvayn Manor") and [Caerellius House](/wiki/Skyrim:Caerellius_House "Skyrim:Caerellius House"), above the [Morvayn](/wiki/Skyrim:Morvayn_Ancestral_Tomb "Skyrim:Morvayn Ancestral Tomb") and [Ulen](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulen_Ancestral_Tomb "Skyrim:Ulen Ancestral Tomb") Ancestral Tombs.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Elder Othreloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Othreloth "Skyrim:Elder Othreloth")  [Galdrus Hlervu](/wiki/Skyrim:Galdrus_Hlervu "Skyrim:Galdrus Hlervu")  [Reclamation Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Reclamation_Priest "Skyrim:Reclamation Priest") [CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal") |

## Related Quests

- **[Clean Sweep](/wiki/Skyrim:Clean_Sweep "Skyrim:Clean Sweep")**: Clear the [Temple Ancestral Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_Ancestral_Tomb "Skyrim:Temple Ancestral Tomb") of [ash spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn").
- **[Ghosts of the Tribunal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal_(quest) "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Decide the fate of a [heretical cult](/wiki/Skyrim:Tribunal_Temple "Skyrim:Tribunal Temple").
- **[Her Word Against Theirs](/wiki/Skyrim:Her_Word_Against_Theirs "Skyrim:Her Word Against Theirs")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Spread the word of the Goddess [Almalexia](/wiki/Lore:Almalexia "Lore:Almalexia").

### Exterior

At the top of the stairs, to the northwest is a circular ash pile garden plot growing five [scathecraw](/wiki/Skyrim:Scathecraw "Skyrim:Scathecraw") plants, and to the southeast are three food urns and three ash yam urns near another flight of stairs up to the top of [the Bulwark](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bulwark "Skyrim:The Bulwark"). To the left of the entrance are three more ash yam urns and a lit brazier. To the right of the entrance is another ash yam urn and a lit brazier. A [Redoran guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redoran_Guard "Skyrim:Redoran Guard") is posted outside the entrance, which is unlocked.

### Temple

The entrance leads into the upper floor of the temple. Along the east wall is an open box containing six ash yams and a bench. Along the west wall is another bench opposite the first. Along the north wall between the benches is an open doorway to the main worship area. In the middle of the room, stairs lead down to the lower floor, with four lit braziers and seven ash yam urns around the sides of the stairs.

Shrine of Boethiah

In the main worship area, pairs of benches flank the entrance to the south and each of the three shrine alcoves to the west, north, and east. The west alcove contains the Shrine of Boethiah, which bestows the [Blessing of Boethiah](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessing_of_Boethiah "Skyrim:Blessing of Boethiah"). The shrine is in the center of a circular ash pile plot growing an ash yam and three scathecraw plants, with two baskets and an open box around the plot containing a total of ten more ash yams and a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), and two more small coin purses, a large coin purse, and a copy of *[The Reclamations](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reclamations "Skyrim:The Reclamations")* on the floor around the box. The north alcove contains the Shrine of Mephala, which bestows the [Blessing of Mephala](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessing_of_Mephala "Skyrim:Blessing of Mephala"). The shrine is in the center of another circular ash pile plot growing two scathecraw plants, with an open box in front of the plot containing four ash yams, a loose [coin](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), and an [amethyst](/wiki/Skyrim:Amethyst "Skyrim:Amethyst"), and a small coin purse, a medium coin purse, eight loose coins, two [garnets](/wiki/Skyrim:Garnet "Skyrim:Garnet"), and an ash yam on the edge of the plot and on the floor next to the box. The east alcove contains the Shrine of Azura, which bestows the [Blessing of Azura](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessing_of_Azura "Skyrim:Blessing of Azura"). The shrine is in the center of another circular ash pile plot growing two ash yams and two scathecraw plants, with an open box in front of the plot containing three more ash yams, a medium coin purse, and a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick"), and two small coin purses, two [emeralds](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald "Skyrim:Emerald"), and four ash yams on the edge of the plot and on the floor next to the box. In the middle of the area is a fourth circular ash pile littered with bones and surrounded by eight lit braziers.

At the bottom of the stairs, on which lies a copy of *[History of Raven Rock, Vol. I](/wiki/Skyrim:History_of_Raven_Rock,_Vol._I "Skyrim:History of Raven Rock, Vol. I")*, is a corridor with rooms beyond doors to the west and east and a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Tomb_Key "Skyrim:Raven Rock Tomb Key")-locked door ahead to the north leading to the [Temple Ancestral Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_Ancestral_Tomb "Skyrim:Temple Ancestral Tomb"). The key can be obtained as part of the quest [Clean Sweep](/wiki/Skyrim:Clean_Sweep "Skyrim:Clean Sweep").

Elder Othreloth's room

The room to the west is Elder Othreloth's bedroom. Along the south wall is a set of shelves holding seven bowls of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal") and copies of both volumes of *[The Red Year](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Red_Year "Skyrim:The Red Year")*, with two food barrels to the right of the set of shelves. Along the north wall are two chairs and a small table holding two bottles of [sujamma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sujamma "Skyrim:Sujamma"), a bottle of [shein](/wiki/Skyrim:Shein "Skyrim:Shein"), copies of *The Reclamations* and both volumes of *[Bone](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone "Skyrim:Bone")*, and an expert-locked [strong box](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox"). Near the west wall is a chair, a single owned bed, and two unusable barrels, one of which has a copy of *[The Five Far Stars](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Five_Far_Stars "Skyrim:The Five Far Stars")* on top.

Galdrus Hlervu's room

The room to the east is Galdrus Hlervu's bedroom. Along the north wall is an ingredient barrel with two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") on top, and a chair and a small round table holding a bottle of sujamma, a bottle of shein, and a copy of *[Deathbrand](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_(book) "Skyrim:Deathbrand (book)")*, with another bottle of wine on the floor next to the table. Along the south wall is a chest and a set of shelves holding copies of all three volumes of *[History of Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:History_of_Raven_Rock "Skyrim:History of Raven Rock")*, *[The House of Troubles](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Troubles "Skyrim:The House of Troubles")*, and *[The Doors of the Spirit](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Doors_of_the_Spirit "Skyrim:The Doors of the Spirit")*. Near the east wall is a single owned bed.

## Bugs

- Several buildings in Raven Rock, including the temple, were incorrectly assigned the [music](/wiki/Skyrim:Music "Skyrim:Music") heard in [Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha "Skyrim:Apocrypha") rather than the default Solstheim music heard in other houses.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.1, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=11969))

# Skyrim:Temples

## Overview

Temple of Kynareth

This page lists all the named **temples**, including those to the [Nine Divines](/wiki/Lore:Nine_Divines "Lore:Nine Divines"), in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").

:   **[Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella")** — A small Aedric temple dedicated to Dibella, the Aedric goddess of love, beauty, and artistry. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Temple+of+Dibella)
:   **[Temple of the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Temple of the Divines")** — The main temple of Solitude and Skyrim, housing shrines to the Eight Divines. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Temple+of+the+Divines)
:   **[Temple of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Temple of Kynareth")** — A small temple in Whiterun devoted to the goddess Kynareth. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Temple+of+Kynareth)
:   **[Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara")** — A temple in Riften devoted to the Aedric goddess Mara, one of the Eight Divines and goddess of mortal understanding, love and compassion. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Temple+of+Mara)
:   **[Temple of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Talos "Skyrim:Temple of Talos")** — Located just northwest of Candlehearth Hall in Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Temple+of+Talos)
:    **[Temple of Xrib](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Xrib "Skyrim:Temple of Xrib")** — A medium-sized cave south-southwest of Winterhold containing Falmer and chaurus. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sightless+Pit)

A Snow Elf temple, added by the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") official add-on, is found in the [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale").

:   **[Inner Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Inner_Sanctum_(Vale) "Skyrim:Inner Sanctum (Vale)")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A relatively well-preserved portion of the Chantry of Auri-El in the Forgotten Vale.

Other temples, added by the [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") official add-on, are found on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim").

:   **[Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple "Skyrim:Temple")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A Dunmer place of worship in Raven Rock. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Temple)
:    **[Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A Nordic temple west of Thirsk Mead Hall containing cultists, draugr, and skeletons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Temple+of+Miraak)

# Skyrim:Tending the Flames

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project"). The secret of [Dead Men's Respite](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Men%27s_Respite "Skyrim:Dead Men's Respite")

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Locate the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College").
2. Learn about the Festival and [Jarl Elisif the Fair](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair")'s plan to cancel it.
3. Travel to [Dead Men's Respite](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Men%27s_Respite "Skyrim:Dead Men's Respite") to receive a missing Verse.
4. Return to the Bards College and pay a visit to the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace").
5. Participate in the Festival.

### The Burning of King Olaf

All over Skyrim, the [Bards](/wiki/Skyrim:Bard "Skyrim:Bard") performing at the various inns and taverns will point you towards the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). When you enter the building, you will be greeted by Headmaster [Viarmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Viarmo "Skyrim:Viarmo"); he will explain a bit about the college and will proceed to hand you a task as part of your application to join. He explains that the ancient college ritual The Burning of King Olaf has been canceled due to the recent assassination of [High King Torygg](/wiki/Skyrim:High_King_Torygg "Skyrim:High King Torygg"). The grieving widow, the recently appointed Jarl of Solitude, [Elisif the Fair](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair") reasons that burning a King in effigy is distasteful at this time and wants the festival shut down. The Festival itself is centuries old and is, according to Viarmo, held to celebrate Solitude and the heroic acts of the mythical King Olaf who apparently slew Numinex, a fearsome dragon who terrorized Skyrim during the First Era.

### The Poetic Edda

To ease the mind of Elisif and thus save the Festival, Viarmo wants to recite King Olaf's Verse, originally a part of the Poetic Edda, but lost for thousands of years. The Poetic Edda is a living history of Skyrim, written by each bard studying at the College and as such, a precious item. King Olaf's Verse was [Svaknir](/wiki/Skyrim:Svaknir "Skyrim:Svaknir")'s contribution to the Edda and dared to question the heroic acts of King Olaf, the very King to whom the Festival is held. Because of the Verse, King Olaf sentenced Svaknir to death and all copies of the Verse burned. The residing Dean of History, [Giraud Gemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Giraud_Gemane "Skyrim:Giraud Gemane"), suspects that the lost Verse can be found inside [Dead Men's Respite](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Men%27s_Respite "Skyrim:Dead Men's Respite"), which he also believes to be the burial tomb for King Olaf himself.

### Dead Men's Respite

Locating the lost verse

The ancient barrow is located in the mountains southwest of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") and you will, immediately upon entering, notice a strange ghost wave at you, then disappear through the sealed entrance to the north. Pick up the [Ruby Dragon Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby_Dragon_Claw "Skyrim:Ruby Dragon Claw") from the table, which will cause four of the previously dead [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") enemies to reanimate and attack (you can kill them by sneak-attacking them before taking the claw), but will also raise the gate and allow you to follow the ghost. It soon becomes clear that the ghost shows you the correct path, so follow it and pull the chain at the dead end. The next area is a maze-like tomb where you will have to pull several chains to open up different areas. Use your map to your advantage and make sure to access the easternmost room for a copy of the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill book *[The Buying Game](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Buying_Game "Skyrim:The Buying Game")*, guarded by a well-placed [Battering Ram](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram"). Watch out for several draugr and [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") and continue north. Beware of the pressure plate at the foot of the stairs, which will release a [flame trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Spout_Trap "Skyrim:Flame Spout Trap"). Fight the spiders in the next room, loot the shelves for some potions and soul gems then pull the chain, which will open the grating in the floor and reveal a watery pit. Take the jump and proceed forward to a chamber with several enemies, including an archer on the ledge above. Proceed to the level above and open the gate, which will trigger several [swinging blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Blades "Skyrim:Swinging Blades") traps (at the bottom-right corner of the gate you will find a trigger for the trap, which you can remove by picking the adept lock), so cross the bridge carefully and pull the chain to make them stop. Go up another level and open the huge door.

### The Executed Bard

At the end of the next tunnel, use the Arcane Enchanter if you must, then turn around and watch your ghostly guide disappear through another doorway to the right. Due to a magical seal the door ahead of you is blocked, so make your way through the doorway to the right and through another set of catacombs to fight the residing draugr. The locked door hides a master-locked treasure chest, with a boss-leveled amount of gold. In the next chamber, the gate will shut behind you and five draugr will attack. After the battle, explore the southeastern room for a chest, but beware of the [dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") protecting it. Pull the chain and head down the path. Activate the handle and watch the rock wall lower and behold the sight of the ghost sitting next to the mummified corpse of [Svaknir](/wiki/Skyrim:Svaknir "Skyrim:Svaknir"), the Bard executed for questioning the King in ancient times. You cannot interact with the ghost, but the corpse still holds the forbidden [Verse](/wiki/Skyrim:King_Olaf%27s_Verse "Skyrim:King Olaf's Verse"), so claim it and learn the truth behind the annual Festival in Solitude. As soon as you take the Verse, the ghost disappears and you will have no choice but to backtrack through the Catacombs.

### Confront the King

On your way back, you will encounter the Ghost of Svaknir near the magically sealed door. He will turn towards the door, break the barrier, and run headfirst into the Chamber. Follow Svaknir to a Nordic [puzzle door](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Puzzle_Door "Skyrim:Traps"); it is finally time to investigate the [Ruby Dragon Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby_Dragon_Claw "Skyrim:Ruby Dragon Claw") you found when you initially entered the barrow, so take an extra look and you will find the symbols **Wolf—Hawk—Wolf**, so adjust the corresponding images for the three rings on the door, then insert the claw in the keyhole. Proceed forward and equip yourself for a lengthy battle.

In the final chamber, the ghost of Svaknir will stand in the middle of a small pond, surrounded by draugr all seated on thrones. There are twenty-one on the ground floor, and an additional four on the ledge in the other end of the room. Everything seems quiet, until you get close to the ghost. He will then shout out:

Svaknir and King Olaf One-Eye fighting

:   :   ***Olaf! It is time!***

His words will make the entire room tremble and the first wave of draugr enemies will rise from their thrones. Eleven out of the twenty-one draugr on the ground floor will attack, ten of them will remain seated and unmoving. As a ghost, Svaknir is immortal and will pick up the fight, so you can do your best to help him out, or simply hide and wait for him to win. When all eleven enemies are slain, Svaknir will shout:

:   :   ***Arise, Olaf! My vengeance is at hand!***

This will make the four draugr on the ledge rise and attack, so once again help Svaknir get his revenge. These draugr are all higher level than the first ones, but Svaknir will once again prove his skills and help you defeat them. When they are dead, he will finally shout out: *"Olaf!"* This will finally cause [Olaf One-Eye](/wiki/Skyrim:King_Olaf_One-Eye "Skyrim:King Olaf One-Eye") himself to burst out of his coffin screaming: *"Insolent Bard. Die!"* He will then attack the both of you, so do your best to avoid his attacks and beware of his ability to disarm you. He can be a tough opponent, but will eventually fall to the ground and die.

The tormented soul of Svaknir will finally be set free; he will head to the nearby door, pull out his lute and disappear in a ray of light. Loot Olaf's corpse for a leveled weapon and the key to his treasury, then examine the wall behind his coffin to learn a [word](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_of_Power "Skyrim:Word of Power") of [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint"). Unlock the treasury door and examine the area for considerable loot, then pull the lever and make your way out of the barrow.

### A Bit of Improvising

Back in the College, Viarmo will be overwhelmed with joy when you hand him the Verse, but will soon be disappointed. He complains about the quality of the rhymes themselves, and, even worse, that some of the writing is unreadable due to age. He will, however, accept a suggestion about making the missing parts up, simply to save the Festival. The next step will involve him reciting the poem and you making up the missing parts. Reading the book *[Olaf and the Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_and_the_Dragon "Skyrim:Olaf and the Dragon")*, found in the upstairs library, will give more background about the deceitful King. Although there is no correct version, how much the court likes what you make up will affect your reward. The persuade options in particular will be very well received at court. Once Viarmo is convinced that the Verse is worth reciting to the Jarl, he will leave the College and head towards the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace"), inviting you along.

Each choice gives you the listed number of points (the higher the number, the better the verse is received). The total of the two choices determines your reward.

**Choice #1**

1. Olaf found him asleep. *(2 points)*
2. Olaf made a deal with Numinex. *(1 point)*
3. Olaf was Numinex. A dragon in human form! (Persuade) *(3 points, requires Speech 25)*

**Choice #2** (Note: There are multiple [bugs](#Bugs) with this choice.)

1. Olaf ordered disguised troops to attack Solitude? *(3 points)*
2. He convinced Solitude to attack Winterhold. *(1 point)*
3. He sacked it and used magic to blame Solitude. *(2 points)*
4. Olaf sacked it in dragon form! (Persuade) *(4 points, only available if Persuade was used in Choice #1, requires Speech 50)*

**Rewards**

| Levels | Total Points | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 2 | 3-4 | 5-6 | 7+ |
| 1-9 | 250 | 400 | 500 | 750 |
| 10-19 | 400 | 600 | 750 | 1,000 |
| 20-29 | 500 | 800 | 1,000 | 1,250 |
| 30-39 | 600 | 1,000 | 1,250 | 1,500 |
| 40+ | 750 | 1,200 | 1,500 | 1,800 |

### Truth be Told

In the Blue Palace, you will find Viarmo in the lobby, waiting for his audition with Jarl Elisif the Fair. Ask him if he's ready and follow him up the stairs, then watch while he recites the embarrassing truth about the legendary King Olaf to the Court.
The verse:

*"O, Olaf, our subjugator, the one-eyed betrayer"*

*O, Olaf, our subjugator, the one-eyed betrayer;*
*death-dealing demon and dragon-killing King.*
*Your legend is lies, lurid and false;*
*your cunning capture of Numinex, a con for the ages.*
*No shouting match between dragon and man, no fire or fury did this battle entail.*
**(Olaf found Numinex asleep)**: *Olaf captured a fast-sleeping dragon, a mighty feat which the meek would not fail.*
**(Olaf made a deal with Numinex)**: *Olaf struck a deal to make himself king, Numinex let go though none tell that tale.*
**(Olaf was Numinex. A dragon in human form!)**: *Olaf was Numinex in human form, on moonless nights he would spread wings and sail.*

*Olaf grabbed power, by promise and threat;*
*From Falkreath to Winterhold, they fell to their knees;*
*But Solitude stood strong, Skyrim's truest protectors.*
*Olaf's vengeance was instant, inspired and wicked.*

The "convinced Solitude to attack" and "sacked it in dragon form" options are both bugged, causing the "disguised troops" line to be read instead. See the [bugs](#Bugs) section for more detail.

**(Olaf ordered disguised troops to attack Solitude)**: *Olaf gave orders, Winterhold disguises. An attack on Solitude total destruction to follow. His men dressed up and then went out to fight, but they reversed Olaf's orders much to Winterhold's sorrow.*

**(Olaf convinced Solitude to attack)**: *Olaf sent word to Solitude's Jarl, cajoling and mocking and begging for a fight. From Winterhold Olaf had sent every message, upon attack he was nowhere in sight.*
**(Olaf sacked Winterhold and used magic to blame Solitude)**: *Because Solitude would not soon bend knee, Olaf would hurt them while his status accrued. He sacked Winterhold his only true ally, and used magic bold to blame Solitude.*
**(Olaf sacked it in dragon form!)**: *Because Solitude would not soon bend knee, Olaf would hurt them while his status accrued. He sacked Winterhold in dragonform, and bent their minds to blame Solitude.*

*So ends the story of Olaf the liar, a thief and a scoundrel we of Solitude commit to the fire.*
*In Solitude bards train for their service, they also gather each year and burn a King who deserves it.*

At the conclusion of the verse, Elisif will admit that Olaf was indeed a thief and a scoundrel and that the Festival is a celebration of Solitude and a condemnation of false Kings. She will reinstate the Festival and promise Viarmo a decent reward for the College. Viarmo will then turn to you and express his gratitude, even if he still will not promote you to Bard; you will have to wait until the Festival, when he will declare you a Bard in front of all College members.

### The Burning of a False King

*"With the lighting of the effigy..."*

Citizens cheering the burning King

He then tells you to seek out [Jorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorn "Skyrim:Jorn") and tell him to finish the preparations for the Festival. He will then leave Blue Palace and you are free to decide when to start the festival. Back in the College, Jorn will be excited about the news and will start right away, with a request to meet him after dark, and then the festival will be on. Wait around until 8pm then approach him again. He will then lead you around the College, to the courtyard where every member of the College is gathered, along with several residents and the resident Bards from the local inns. Talk to [Bendt](/wiki/Skyrim:Bendt "Skyrim:Bendt"), [Sorex Vinius](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorex_Vinius "Skyrim:Sorex Vinius"), or [Evette San](/wiki/Skyrim:Evette_San "Skyrim:Evette San") for free snacks, then watch and listen as Viarmo sets the effigy on fire and declares you the newest addition to the Bards College. All guests will applaud and Viarmo himself will seek you out and explain that several College professors will have jobs for you and that the burning of the King will now be a weekly event. Finally, he will hand you your reward, a leveled amount of gold, and leave you alone with the burning King Olaf.

After you finish the quest, guards in all 9 Holds will recognize you as a bard. Solitude Guards will also recognize you as the one who restored the Fire Festival.

## Festival Reactions

The following Solitude residents and Bards College members will be present at the Festival:

| Name | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |

## Notes

- If the quest [Bound Until Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death") is active, it must be completed before the last step of this quest, as Jorn will tell you to wait until the marriage in the temple is over.
- During the festival, [Sorex Vinius](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorex_Vinius "Skyrim:Sorex Vinius") will be handing out free meat pies; however, as meat pies do not exist in the game, you will actually receive an apple pie from him.
  - Version 1.2.3 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") adds meat pies as a replacement item for this quest.
- During part of [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"), Elisif is away from the Blue Palace. If this has happened, you should complete that quest before going to Dead Men's Respite.

## Bugs

- Sometimes King Olaf's verse will not be found next to Svaknir's body, with the indication arrow pointing to where it is supposed to be.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.5, fixes this bug.
  - If the book appears to be absent, it is embedded in the ground. A fireball or other explosion may dislodge it.
- After he triggers the first wave of draugr, Svaknir might simply stand in the middle of the room with King Olaf's body, not triggering the next wave. **?**
  - Attempting to damage him may cause him to proceed. He is immune to Unrelenting Force.
  - Raising any of the undead in the area can cause this. Waiting for it to expire or unsummoning it can resolve the issue.
- If you choose "He convinced Solitude to attack Winterhold" for Choice #2, the recitation and scoring will both act as if you had instead selected "Olaf ordered disguised troops to attack Solitude?" *and* as if you had selected "Olaf made a deal with Numinex" in Choice #1, regardless of what you had previously chosen. The line that should have been read for this choice cannot currently be heard in game.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- If you choose "Olaf sacked it in dragon form!" for Choice #2, the recitation and scoring will both act as if you had instead selected "Olaf ordered disguised troops to attack Solitude?" The line that should have been read for this choice cannot be heard in game without the USKP. This also makes the highest reward unavailable, though your Speech skill will still be advanced normally for a Persuade check if you choose this option.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- When he burns the effigy, Viarmo may tap it with a hammer rather than applying the torch, then after completing the quest he will still be seen holding the torch he used.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
  -  To fix this use console on Viarmo, then type: first `removeitem 0001d4ec 1`, second `equipitem 0001d4ec`, and third `removeitem 0001d4ec 1`.
  - Attack Viarmo until he kneels down on the floor; he won't die as he is essential. Once he does that, he shouldn't be holding the torch any longer. A bounty will be earned if you use this method. Another method is by reverse-pickpocketing another torch into his inventory. This fixes the issue with minimal bloodshed. From then on, he will only equip the torch when appropriate.
  - This also seems to have been fixed with the [Special Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition "Skyrim:Special Edition").
- If the dragon claw door does not work, check [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Puzzle_Totems#Bugs "Skyrim:Puzzle Totems") for possible fixes.
- Viarmo may not read out the verses at all, and when you speak to him in the Blue Palace, it will sometimes skip to the next part, as if he had made his performance. This doesn't affect the rest of the quest at all, and it can still be completed normally.
- Viarmo approaches the throne to read out the verses but the jarl is not present. Viarmo stands in front of the throne and does not say the verses. He will say "not now" if approached.
  - This will happen if you have begun the Season Unending quest and Elisif has gone to High Hrothgar for the negotiations. Going to High Hrothgar and completing the negotiations returns her to Solitude to hear Viarmo.
  - Otherwise, simply waiting for an hour may fix this. Wait without using the "wait" function and they will all walk in.
  - It can also happen if Viarmo has simply arrived too late in the day and Elisif has gone to her bedroom to sleep. In this case, wait till the morning - or revert to the auto-save that was made when you entered the palace, and don't talk to Viarmo in the downstairs lobby. He won't go upstairs to perform until you talk to him, wait to do this until Elisif \*is\* upstairs sitting on her throne. (In this case this is probably not a bug but a feature.)
  - If that doesn't work, you can commit any crime to incur a bounty (just a small one will do), and then pay it off. The court will leave as if he read the verse and you can continue the quest.
  -  You can use the console to move the jarl to you by entering `prid 000198C1` and then `moveto player`.
- If you take the dragon claw before the ghost disappears the draugr may not rise and the door won't open.
  - Jumping on the pressure plate where the claw spawns fixes it
- When Viarmo burns the effigy, it is possible for him to repeat his burning animation indefinitely, preventing the festival from finishing. Talking to him may allow you to continue the ceremony but he may be permanently stuck. **?**
  - Disrupting the crowd gathering for the festival before it starts (e.g. attack people with a shout and then calm them with a spell) may fix this.
  -  Another way to fix this loop is to use the console command `kill` on [Pantea](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea_Ateia "Skyrim:Pantea Ateia"). After closing the console, she will fall dead. Go to Viarmo and talk to him; he will stop setting the fire and finish the quest. To revive Pantea, simply return to her and use the command `resurrect 1` on her.
  -  Alternatively, you can use `kill` and `resurrect 1` on Viarmo to have a similar, if not more, immediate effect. Viarmo is essential, so he will not die but instead go into recovery mode.
  -  This may also be fixed by targeting Viarmo in the console and using the `disable` command followed by the `enable` command.
  -  Before Pantea arrives at her position in the festival but after Viarmo starts his speech, use disable on Pantea. After he says "...he becomes a full fledged member of the.." you can re-enable.
  -  You may also complete the quest through the console after speaking to Jorn in order to start the festival. Jorn will leave the Bards College to set up the festival, and once he leaves, enter the console and write the following: `completequest ms05`, upon leaving the college the festival should be set up. Then run to Viarmo as he will start his speech about the burning. Quickly, open your map and fast travel to a location and then back. Once you arrive, Viarmo will have completed his animations and welcome you to the Bards College. (This will allow you to attend the festival as well as complete the quest).
- The *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* lists the "Gift of the Gab" reward for this quest, though it does not work in the official release.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, addresses this issue. A reward was added that causes Speech to increase 15% faster.
- Even after the quest has finished, NPCs seem to keep the festival running every night with their related behaviors. **?**
  -  There is a hidden Quest running the Festival, sometimes ending seems to get stuck. With `setstage MS05KingOlafsFestival 200` you can bring them back to Normal
- If you wait during the burning of King Olaf, [Silana Petreia](/wiki/Skyrim:Silana_Petreia "Skyrim:Silana Petreia") may randomly die in the place where she is meant to stand. **?**
- King Olaf's Festival was intended to run every week, on Loredas (Saturday) once this quest is completed, but certain constraints made that impossible. To fix this, the following changes were made with version 2.0.1 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"):
  - KingOlafsFestivalStarter needed 3 of its aliases set to optional since they're not even required anyway and two of the NPCs could be dead.
  - Viarmo's alias in the Festival scene needed to be set independently since his alias will be invalid by this point.
  - Viarmo's inventory would get a new torch every time this ran, so all the torches in his inventory will be taken from him when the quest shuts down.
  - Stage 20 of the Festival would attempt to set stage 290 of the quest each time it runs, but this only needs to be done once.

## Quest Stages

| Tending the Flames (MS05) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 75 |  | I have applied at the Bards College. As part of the Application, Headmaster Viarmo wants me to find and bring to him King Olaf's Verse. *Objective 75:* Find King Olaf's Verse |
| 100 |  | *Objective 100:* Return to the Bards College |
| 125 |  | I have applied at the Bards College. As part of the Application, Headmaster Viarmo asked me to retrieve King Olaf's Verse. Parts of the verse have decayed, I must help Viarmo reconstruct it so he can present it in court. *Objective 125:* Help Viarmo reconstruct Olaf's Verse |
| 135 |  | *Objective 135:* Meet Viarmo at the Blue Palace |
| 150 |  | I have applied at the Bards College. As part of the Application, I helped Headmaster Viarmo reconstruct King Olaf's Verse. I should go watch Viarmo present the verse to the court at the Blue Palace. *Objective 150:* Watch Viarmo perform Olaf's Verse |
| 175 |  | I have applied at the Bards College. As part of the Application, I helped Headmaster Viarmo reconstruct King Olaf's Verse. The court has accepted the Verse I should speak to Viarmo about my application. *Objective 175:* Speak to Viarmo |
| 200 |  | I am to be inducted into the Bards College at the Burning of King Olaf festival. I've been told to speak to Jorn who is preparing the effigy of King Olaf. *Objective 200:* Speak to Jorn |
| 225 |  | I am to be inducted into the Bards College at the Burning of King Olaf festival. Unfortunately the festival cannot begin until the effigy is done and Jorn will not complete it without General Tullius' Coat. I must steal the coat and return to Jorn. *Objective 225:* Steal General Tullius' Coat |
| 250 |  | I am to be inducted into the Bards College at the Burning of King Olaf festival. I must speak to Jorn who is in charge of preparing the Effigy. *Objective 250:* Speak to Jorn |
| 253 |  | *Objective 253:* Speak to Jorn after dusk |
| 254 |  | I am to be inducted into the Bards College at the Burning of King Olaf festival. Unfortunately the festival cannot begin until the effigy is done and Jorn will not complete it without General Tullius' Coat. I must place the coat on the effigy. |
| 255 |  | I am to be inducted into the Bards College at the Burning of King Olaf festival. I should attend the festival in the Bards College courtyard in Solitude. *Objective 255:* Attend The Burning of King Olaf |
| 260 |  | *Objective 260:* Place the Coat on the Effigy |
| 300 | ☑ | I have been inducted into the Bards College in Solitude. |
| *Unknown* |  | *Objective 90:* Give Viarmo King Olaf's Verse |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 10, 90, 145, 265, 290.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MS05 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MS05`.

Thalmor Embassy

**Thalmor Embassy** is the [Aldmeri Dominion](/wiki/Lore:Aldmeri_Dominion "Lore:Aldmeri Dominion")'s diplomatic mission to [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") northwest of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). It contains five zones: *[Thalmor Embassy](#Thalmor_Embassy)*, *Thalmor Embassy, Barracks*, *[Thalmor Embassy, Elenwen's Solar](#Thalmor_Embassy.2C_Elenwen.27s_Solar)*, *[Thalmor Embassy, Dungeon](#Thalmor_Embassy.2C_Dungeon)*, and *[Reeking Cave](#Reeking_Cave)*.

The party

The embassy is a gated complex serving as the center of [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") activity in Skyrim. [Elenwen](/wiki/Skyrim:Elenwen "Skyrim:Elenwen") is the resident ambassador, known for hosting the province's most powerful men and mer at lavish ambassadorial parties. You infiltrate the building via an ill-gotten invitation as part of the [main quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Main_Quest "Skyrim:Main Quest").

## Residents

| Name | Job |
