## Related Quests

- **[Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity")**: Infiltrate a party at the Thalmor Embassy.
- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.

### Exterior: Front Courtyard

The front courtyard

You will arrive inside the courtyard after speaking with [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine") during the quest [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity"). There are two sets of double metal gates leading into the courtyard from the outside, and a separate building nearby containing the barracks; the door to the barracks is locked and requires a key to enter. In the courtyard is the carriage you arrived on and [Razelan](/wiki/Skyrim:Razelan "Skyrim:Razelan"), a fellow party guest. There are also two Thalmor guards and a Thalmor wizard standing in the courtyard: one of the guards patrols the courtyard, the other guard at the bottom of the stairs will check your invitation, and the wizard stands near the entrance to the interior.

### Thalmor Embassy

As soon as you enter, you'll be in the reception room, where the party is already in full swing. Elenwen will immediately approach; however, [Malborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Malborn "Skyrim:Malborn") will interrupt her, enabling you to avoid a lengthy conversation. There is a small wardrobe to your left containing [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes"). To your right is a small cupboard containing clutter. The guests present vary depending on several factors; see the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity") for details. In addition to Elenwen, there are two guards, [Illdi](/wiki/Skyrim:Illdi "Skyrim:Illdi") the bard (or [Grete](/wiki/Skyrim:Grete "Skyrim:Grete") if Illdi is dead), the serving girl [Brelas](/wiki/Skyrim:Brelas "Skyrim:Brelas"), and Malborn in the room. Everything in the embassy can be freely taken, except where specifically stated. The room is fairly square, with heavily vaulted sections around the east, south, and west sides, and a fireplace in the middle of the north wall. There is a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush in a vase to the right, with wooden benches on either side.

Speaking to Brelas will grant you a bottle of [Colovian Brandy](/wiki/Skyrim:Colovian_Brandy "Skyrim:Colovian Brandy"), but you are limited to a single bottle in your possession. It is marked as a quest item and can not be dropped. Behind Brelas is a small set of shelves holding some [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet") and a [red mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"). In the southeastern corner is a table laid with two platters holding seven [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish") steaks, two [baked potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), three [tomatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato"), and two portions of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"). Between two of the arches is another narrow table with a stack of [plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate") and a [platter](/wiki/Skyrim:Platter "Skyrim:Platter") holding two [sweet rolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll") and two [honey nut treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat"). Against the south wall is a narrow table with a bowl of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and a plate of a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese") with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") on top. To the right of this table is another table laid with two platters holding a [leg of goat roast](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat_Roast "Skyrim:Leg of Goat Roast"), two [pheasant roasts](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Roast "Skyrim:Pheasant Roast"), a [horse haunch](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Haunch "Skyrim:Horse Haunch"), three sweet rolls, and an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie").

In the southwest corner is yet another table laid with a platter of bread and cheese, a bowl of three [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), a bunch of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"), two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and a [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"). Against the west wall is a small round table with three common [books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books") on top near one of several wooden benches against the walls of the room. There are two internal doors in this room: one to the south with a guard beside it, and one to the west behind Malborn, who is behind a counter serving drinks. On the counter is a bottle of alto wine and one of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), several goblets, and a small mead barrel. Malborn will instruct you to arrange a diversion so that he can slip you out of the room.

Through the door behind Malborn is a narrow storage area with three sets of shelves holding seven bottles of alto wine, four bottles of wine, and two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), with two stacks of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels opposite. Malborn will lead you through the kitchen, where [Tsavani](/wiki/Skyrim:Tsavani "Skyrim:Tsavani") the cook will ignore you after Malborn threatens her. In the kitchen are three sets of shelves, two sets of wall shelves, two tables for preparing food, several open crates, many loaves of bread and pieces of cheese, four food sacks, and a food barrel. In the middle of the west wall is an oven, with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") on an unusable block to the right. The following food and ingredients can be found in the kitchen:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Food and Drink:**  - 4 Alto Wine - 1 [Nord Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") - 2 Wine - 2 Baked Potato - 2 [Gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") | - 7 [Cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") - 1 [Dog Meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog_Meat "Skyrim:Dog Meat") - 1 Grilled Leeks - 2 [Horse Meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Meat "Skyrim:Horse Meat") - 2 [Leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") | - 1 [Pheasant Breast](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast") - 19 [Potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") - 1 [Raw Beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef") - 1 [Raw Rabbit Leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg") - 5 Red Apples | - 3 [Salmon Meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Meat "Skyrim:Salmon Meat") - 1 [Salmon Steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak") - 1 Seared Slaughterfish - 6 Tomatoes - 1 [Venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison") | **Ingredients:**  - 5 [Chicken's Eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") - 6 [Dried Elves Ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear") - 2 [Dried Frost Mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Dried Frost Mirriam") - 1 [Fly Amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") - 10 [Garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") | - 8 [Garlic Braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid") - 1 [Orange Dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing") - 4 [Pine Thrush Eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg") - 1 [Rock Warbler Egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg") |

Tsavani does not like unexpected guests in her kitchen

The storage room where Malborn smuggled your gear

Malborn leads you through a door in the east wall into another storage room, where you find an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing any gear he smuggled in for you, seven food sacks, and a small cupboard with an open crate on top containing two leeks and five tomatoes. Hanging from the ceiling are two [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), a bunch of dried elves ear, a bunch of dried frost mirriam, and three garlic braids. Three wall shelves hold a bottle of alto wine, a bottle of wine, and several cheese wheels. There is a second door in the southeastern corner that leads to a corridor. Malborn will be in a hurry for you to pass through this door so that he can lock it behind you before he is missed at the party. You will need to move a few paces along the corridor in order for him to lock the door.

Two Thalmor guards can be found here laughing about the potential demise of their mage cohorts

Once you are in the corridor, Malborn will explain you are on your own, then lock the door behind you. You can hear two guards talking in a room through an open door on the left about a group of mages sent to help with the dragon problem. There is a cupboard on your immediate left with a bottle of alto wine and a [thistle branch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch") on top. There is a second cupboard on the far side of the door, and a narrow table with a bottle of alto wine and a [potion of light feet](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Light_Feet "Skyrim:Potion of Light Feet") on top at the end of the corridor. There is also an open door on the right, which opens to a room containing a low table with a set of [Thalmor robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Robes "Skyrim:Thalmor Robes") and [gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Gloves "Skyrim:Thalmor Gloves") on top and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Boots "Skyrim:Thalmor Boots") on the floor beside it. The room is used as a storage room for unused furniture and other items, with cobwebs and dust all around. There is a mead barrel containing bottles of Nord mead, a food barrel with a basket containing potatoes on top, several rolled up rugs, various items of fine crockery and [candlesticks](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlestick "Skyrim:Candlestick"), and a couple tables and sets of shelves, but nothing else of interest.

After a few moments, the two guards will return to their patrols, allowing you to either sneak through or deal with them individually. The room they are in has a small counter on the immediate right with some bread and cheese on top. A narrow table behind the counter has an iron dagger on top, a food sack below, and a wall shelf above holding two bottles of Nord mead and a bottle of alto wine. On the left is the second door seen in the reception room where the party continues, and a partition beyond the door. In the southeast corner is a low table and bench with a plate of bread and cheese and a bottle of alto wine on top. Beside this is a set of shelves holding a bunch of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"), a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), a [draught of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Strength "Skyrim:Draught of Strength"), a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), a [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), and a common [book](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books"). In the south wall is a doorway into another storeroom containing two cupboards holding a set of fine clothes, a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots"), a gourd, three garlic bulbs, a bunch of tundra cotton, a single loose [coin](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), and two food sacks. In the southwestern corner is a flight of stairs leading up with a small wardrobe to the left and a basket beside it hiding a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). At the east end of the room is a corridor heading south, with a small cupboard and a table with a candlestick on top and a vase containing a snowberry bush. Around the corner is a door leading outside, flanked by another small cupboard with a thistle branch on top and a set of shelves holding two pairs of Thalmor boots, two bottles of wine, and a basket containing two bunches of lavender.

A corridor leading to rooms containing loot

The stairs lead up to another corridor running east to west. To the east is a table with a copy of *[Dwemer History and Culture](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_History_and_Culture "Skyrim:Dwemer History and Culture")* on top, a set of shelves holding seven common books, and past a doorway into another room is a small wardrobe with a copy of *[Uncommon Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:Uncommon_Taste "Skyrim:Uncommon Taste")* on top. The room contains a long dining table in the middle with two bottles of alto wine, a potion of regeneration, two seared slaughterfish steaks, two baked potatoes, a portion of grilled leeks, and a bunch of tundra cotton on top. A small table at one end holds a bottle of wine, and a small shelving unit at the other end holds another bottle of alto wine and has a small mead barrel on top. On the east wall are two sets of shelves holding two random [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), a random [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), a random empty [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), and a common book. In front of these shelves is a low table and chair with a bottle of wine and another common book on top. Against the south wall is a small cupboard with an owned bunch of [juniper berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") on top, and to the right is an open crate containing two more empty random soul gems, a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a random potion of magicka, and an owned bunch of lavender. Finally, against the west wall is another set of shelves holding a [draught of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Strength "Skyrim:Draught of Strength"), a potion of health, a potion of regeneration, a bunch of tundra cotton, a common book, and two bunches of lavender in a basket.

To the west down the corridor, there is a room on the right at the end, and an open area to the left in front of a door leading outside. The room is a bedroom containing a large owned double bed coming out from the north wall, with end tables on either side holding candlesticks, and a long unlocked chest at the foot of the bed. To the right is a narrow table with a bottle of [frostbite venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Venom "Skyrim:Frostbite Venom") on top. In the northeast corner is a small wardrobe, and against the south wall is a tall wardrobe, both containing fine clothes and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots "Skyrim:Fine Boots"). There is also a low table with a bottle of alto wine, a plate of bread and cheese, and a potion of regeneration on top. By the door is an open crate containing a bunch of tundra cotton and a red mountain flower, and next to the crate is a wash basin. To the left in the open area are two small cupboards, with a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum") and a potion of health on top of one of the cupboards, and three wall shelves holding a bottle of alto wine, two bottles of Nord mead, a [potion of plentiful healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Healing"), and a bunch of lavender. There is also a low table and chair, with a common book, a bottle of wine, and a plate of bread and cheese on top.

### Exterior: Rear Courtyard

The rear courtyard

Through the door to the outside is the end of a path around the outside wall of the courtyard. There is one guard standing against a wall to your left by a gap in the wall, another patrolling the courtyard, a Thalmor wizard also wandering the courtyard, and a second wizard standing in front of the entrance to *[Thalmor Embassy, Elenwen's Solar](#Thalmor_Embassy.2C_Elenwen.27s_Solar)*. There are two planters in the middle of the courtyard containing three lavender plants, a [thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle "Skyrim:Thistle"), and a [blue mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"). Hidden on the roof of the solar are two [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"): a leveled [invisibility potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions#Potion_of_Brief_Invisibility "Skyrim:Potions") and a random leveled [fortifying potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions#Standard_Potions "Skyrim:Potions"). If the embassy is leveled to level 30 or higher, a [Potion of Prolonged Invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions#Potion_of_Prolonged_Invisibility "Skyrim:Potions") will spawn and roll off into the courtyard below; otherwise, both potions remain on the roof and can be pulled down with [Telekinesis](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis "Skyrim:Telekinesis"). They are barely visible at the edge of the highest point of the roof facing the planters below.

### Thalmor Embassy, Elenwen's Solar

Elenwen's Solar entrance area

If you are sneaking when you first enter, you are able to sneak past a Thalmor guard standing in front of you, facing away. To the right at the rear of the room is a small storeroom. From there, you are able to overhear a conversation between a Thalmor agent and an informant named [Gissur](/wiki/Skyrim:Gissur "Skyrim:Gissur"). They are discussing an old man they are trying to locate. In the storeroom is a small cupboard with a drum, a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flower, and a potion of health on top, with a wall shelf holding three common books above it, and two sets of shelves holding two bottles of frostbite venom, two deathbell flowers, a bowl of [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts"), a bowl of [glow dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust"), two samples of [slaughterfish scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales"), a [potion of haggling](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Haggling "Skyrim:Potion of Haggling"), five common books, a basket containing two bunches of lavender, and another basket containing a bunch of tundra cotton. The main part of the room has a small counter with six bottles of wine and a platter holding two sweet rolls, three red apples, and two [boiled creme treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"). Along the east wall is a table holding a bowl containing a bunch of tundra cotton and an iron dagger. Against the south wall is a small shelving unit holding a bottle of alto wine. There is a small table to the left of the counter with a bottle of wine on top, and a low table in the middle of the room with a common book, a bottle of wine, and a plate of bread and cheese on top. There are stairs opposite the entrance leading up, with vases of snowberry bushes on either side.

To the west and in the northwestern corners are two rooms. The first room to the west is an office, and contains a desk with two [rolls of paper](/wiki/Skyrim:Roll_of_Paper "Skyrim:Roll of Paper") on top and a basket containing more rolls beside it. Behind the desk are three bookcases holding a total of twenty common books, a flute, a drum, a potion of health, a basket containing two bunches of lavender, and a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick"), a random potion of stamina, and a [solution of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Strength "Skyrim:Solution of Strength"). Against the west wall is a set of shelves holding two bottles of frostbite venom, a deathbell flower, a bowl of void salts, a bowl of glow dust, two samples of slaughterfish scales, and a potion of haggling. Next to these shelves is an expert-locked display case containing two crossed [elven daggers](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Dagger "Skyrim:Elven Dagger"), a [gold and ruby circlet](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_and_Ruby_Circlet "Skyrim:Gold and Ruby Circlet"), and a [gold and emerald circlet](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_and_Emerald_Circlet "Skyrim:Gold and Emerald Circlet"). Against the north wall is a tall wardrobe containing fine clothes and boots. There is also a doorway on the north wall to a flight of stairs leading down.

The other room on this floor is also an office, and contains a desk with a bottle of alto wine, a potion of health, a potion of regeneration, and two rolls of paper on top, and another basket containing more rolls of paper beside it. Behind the desk is a small set of shelves holding two more rolls of paper and an iron dagger, a wall shelf holding three bottles of alto wine and a bottle of Nord mead, and an unlocked chest containing the information you need for the quest and a copy of the [interrogation chamber key](/wiki/Skyrim:Interrogation_Chamber_Key "Skyrim:Interrogation Chamber Key"). There is a small table to the right with a bunch of tundra cotton on top, and farther to the right another table with bread and cheese on top. To the right of the door are two bookcases holding nineteen common books and copies of *[Argonian Account, Book 2](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Account,_Book_2 "Skyrim:Argonian Account, Book 2")* and *[Book 4](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Account,_Book_4 "Skyrim:Argonian Account, Book 4")*, *[Lost Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends")*, *[Short History of Morrowind](/wiki/Skyrim:Short_History_of_Morrowind "Skyrim:Short History of Morrowind")*, and *[The Adabal-a](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Adabal-a "Skyrim:The Adabal-a")*. There is also a large vase containing a sprig of snowberries in the northeastern corner to the right of another doorway, which leads to another flight of descending stairs.

Elenwen's bedroom

Climbing the stairs in the main room leads to a landing overlooking the downstairs area, with rooms at either end. There is a small wardrobe on the landing to the east. The room at this end is Elenwen's bedroom, and contains a large, owned four-posted bed coming out from the south wall, with end tables on either side and a long unlocked chest at the foot of the bed. To the right is a small wardrobe, a wash basin, and a narrow table with a bottle of frostbite venom on top. Beside the door is a set of shelves holding four common books, a solution of strength, and a random potion of stamina. To the left of the bed is a low table with a bottle of alto wine, a potion of regeneration, and a plate of bread and cheese on top, and another table beside it with a platter holding a sweet roll, two baked potatoes, and a cheese wheel on top. Above this table is a wall shelf holding two common books and a deathbell flower. To the left is a large vase containing a snowberry bush. There is another small wardrobe in the northeast corner, and to the left a doorway into a storage area featuring a tall wardrobe containing fine clothes and boots, an open crate containing two bunches of tundra cotton, an unlocked [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Safe "Skyrim:Safe") containing a range of loot, and a set of shelves holding a draught of strength, a potion of health, a potion of regeneration, a bunch of tundra cotton, and a basket containing two bunches of lavender.

To the west are two rooms. The first room is a small storeroom, and contains a small cupboard holding three common books and a deathbell flower and a small shelving unit with a bottle of alto wine. The second room is another bedroom, and contains a single bed coming out from the southwestern corner, with an end table to the left, a small table to the right with a red and a [green apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") on top, and an unlocked wooden chest at the foot of the bed. There is a [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") in a large vase against the west wall, a small table holding a candlestick, a small desk with a common book and rolls of paper on top and in a basket beside it, a tall wardrobe by the door, and in the southeast corner, a low table and chair with a potion of regeneration and a plate of bread and cheese on top.

Descending the stairs from the ground floor office with the chest containing the relevant information leads to an area with a small wardrobe, and under the stairs a cupboard holding two [goat cheese wheels](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), two loaves of bread, and a sheaf of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat"). The door at the bottom of the stairs leads into *[Thalmor Embassy, Dungeon](#Thalmor_Embassy.2C_Dungeon)* and is master-locked, but opened by the key found in the chest upstairs. Descending the stairs from the office in the room to the west leads to a similar area, with a cupboard holding a set of fine clothes, a pair of boots, a gourd, three garlic bulbs, a single loose coin, and a bunch of tundra cotton. Under the stairs are several food barrels and an unlocked chest containing minor loot.

### Thalmor Embassy, Dungeon

Through the latter door is a balcony overlooking the dungeon proper, with several food barrels and a small table with a random [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield") and a random potion of healing on top. At the far end are stairs that lead down to the main area, where you can hear the Thalmor torturing someone for information, but the person keeps claiming to have told them everything. There are two Thalmor at the bottom: a guard doing the torturing, and a wizard named [Rulindil](/wiki/Skyrim:Rulindil "Skyrim:Rulindil") asking the questions, seated at a table with more rolls of paper in front of him. An unlocked chest beside Rulindil contains a [Thalmor Dossier: Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Dossier:_Esbern "Skyrim:Thalmor Dossier: Esbern"). Under the stairs are more food barrels, with an unlocked chest on top containing minor loot. Beside the barrels is a pile of straw with more barrels, a set of [iron armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Iron Armor"), and humanoid bones.

If you enter the dungeon from the stairs off the office with the chest, you emerge on a small balcony behind Rulindil, with a short passage containing several dusty crates to the stairs leading down. There are many more food barrels and more humanoid bones under these stairs, and, through a doorway into the main area, a set of shelves on the left holding an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"). In the center of this area is a torture rack, a table beside it with a garlic bulb on top, and a small shelving unit against the south wall with a common book on the shelf. Along the east wall are three cells. The first contains [Etienne Rarnis](/wiki/Skyrim:Etienne_Rarnis "Skyrim:Etienne Rarnis"), who was the one being tortured, the next cell is empty, and the third cell is only occupied if you used [Erikur](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur "Skyrim:Erikur") and Brelas for your distraction, in which case Brelas will be shackled to the wall. Opposite this cell is a trapdoor leading to *[Reeking Cave](#Reeking_Cave)* and your escape. The trapdoor is locked and requires a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Trap_Door_Key "Skyrim:Trap Door Key"), and there are humanoid bones all around the trapdoor. To the right is an unlocked chest and more food barrels. Stairs lead up to another balcony with several crates, a dresser with a set of [banded iron armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Banded Iron Armor") on top, and a table at the end with two bottles of Nord mead on top.

Speak to Etienne Rarnis or read the dossier on Esbern to progress the quest. As soon as the quest updates, Malborn will appear on the balcony up the southern stairs with two Thalmor guards, having been arrested for his treachery in helping you. Both the guards are carrying a copy of the key to the trapdoor. You can free Brelas in addition to Etienne and Malborn if she is present and if you wish. Use the key to escape the embassy and enter *Reeking Cave*.

### Reeking Cave

As soon as you enter through the trapdoor in the embassy, you are on a ledge with [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") growing in front of you. The ledge overlooks the main part of the cave, which contains a [frost troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll"). Everyone you've freed will immediately attack, so if you want them to live, you will have to move fast. Once the troll is dealt with, in the southwest corner you will find the body of a [novice conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Novice_Conjurer "Skyrim:Novice Conjurer"), a large coin purse, a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel"), a copy of the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Before the Ages of Man](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Ages_of_Man "Skyrim:Before the Ages of Man")*, and an [unusual gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") (see [notes](#Notes)).

## Notes

- [Official Patch 1.4](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch") moves the unusual gem in the embassy to *Reeking Cave*, next to a dead conjurer near the trapdoor used to escape the dungeon.
- If you return to the embassy compound after completing Diplomatic Immunity, you can enter the grounds and the barracks but not the embassy building.
  - If you return with a [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses "Skyrim:Horses"), you can use it to gain access to a tree to the left of the embassy inside the first section of the compound. Jump repeatedly and you will climb up the tree and eventually clear the fence. The entire embassy except the reception room and the kitchen will then be accessible.
  - It is also possible to reenter the embassy through *Reeking Cave* using platforming and the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). *Reeking Cave* is west-northwest of the embassy. There is no icon on the map for the cave entrance, but it is near the northwest corner of the embassy and the end of the road as shown on the map. Once in the cave, in order to get up the ledge, you must walk to the top of the log, aim the crosshair slightly above the right side of the ledge you are trying to reach, and use Whirlwind Sprint. You can also reach the trapdoor by turning collision off by inputting the console command `tcl` (to turn collision back on, input the command `tcl` again).
  - It is possible to reenter the embassy via the outer wall using a kettle and Whirlwind Sprint. Starting outside the main gate looking in, go to the left and around the corner. Where the wall again turns left, drop the kettle, then pick it up to eye level and slowly walk to the wall. When the kettle appears to have a hole in the bottom, Whirlwind Sprint in.
  - It is possible to reenter the embassy using the wooden plate trick and walking through the front door. The exterior does respawn guards, but not the interior. Repeat the wooden plate trick inside to access locked rooms.
  - It is possible to [summon Arvak](/wiki/Skyrim:Summon_Arvak "Skyrim:Summon Arvak")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") on the other side of the stone fence by jumping from the snow pile onto the corner of the fence then riding [Arvak](/wiki/Skyrim:Arvak "Skyrim:Arvak"). You will then be on the blocked side of the fence.
- During Diplomatic Immunity, anyone who escapes the embassy with you will run toward Solitude after exiting Reeking Cave, eventually end up near the [Dainty Sload](/wiki/Skyrim:Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:Dainty Sload") and vanish if not killed by a hostile random encounter. Their deaths can also be avoided by fast-traveling once you are outside Reeking Cave.
- After completing Diplomatic Immunity, if you sprint and bump into a Thalmor, all Thalmor on the grounds of the embassy will become hostile.
- The two guards who appear with Malborn after you read the Esbern dossier will not become hostile and will not attack Malborn if you are a High Elf wearing elven or glass armor.
- If you start [Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound") as a High Elf, [Hadvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadvar "Skyrim:Hadvar") will say: *"You're not with the Thalmor Embassy, are you high elf? No, that can't be right..."*

## Bugs

- Do not attempt to enter the embassy to acquire the [Stone of Barenziah](/wiki/Skyrim:Stone_of_Barenziah "Skyrim:Stone of Barenziah") within for the quest [No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned") until you have received the quest Diplomatic Immunity. Doing so will trigger an event that changes the dialogue options for any NPCs that are also visiting the embassy for the party. This can and likely will be detrimental to any quests related to those NPCs (such as jarls or [Maven Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar")), causing you to be unable to start or complete quests requiring those NPCs until you have finished Diplomatic Immunity. **?**
  -  It is unconfirmed whether completing Diplomatic Immunity using console commands would fix this error. However, entering the embassy before starting Diplomatic Immunity may cause Delphine to no longer give the quest-related dialogue that begins the quest in the first place.
  - With Official Patch 1.4 or later, there is no problem with entering *Reeking Cave* for the unusual gem as long as you keep well away from anyone in the embassy itself until Diplomatic Immunity.
- Before Diplomatic Immunity has started, entering the embassy causes stage 180 of the quest to be completed. Stage 180 is thought to be an invalid stage, but may in fact be the stage that changes the dialogue for the NPCs visiting the party. **?**
- If for whatever reason the embassy guards have died prior to Diplomatic Immunity (a dragon attack, for example), they may not respawn for the quest once it starts and that will result in the quest being uncompletable.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.5, fixes this bug.
- The safe in Elenwen's Solar may be facing the wrong way, with the door to it aimed at the wall instead.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- The Thalmor Embassy Barracks isn't marked as owned by the Thalmor faction, making it possible to enter and take everything inside without penalty.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.9, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Thalmor Headquarters

## Overview

|  |

Thalmor Headquarters

**Thalmor Headquarters** is a building in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") within the walls of [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour").

The entrance is at the top of a long straight flight of stairs leading up from the courtyard in Castle Dour, to the right of the door guarded by two [Solitude guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Guard "Skyrim:Solitude Guard") that leads to [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius").

## Thalmor Headquarters

Despite its name, the building is bereft of [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") and anyone else. It appears to have been abandoned suddenly: upon entering, immediately on the left is a wooden bench, with a large vase holding a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush next to it and a small cupboard opposite. Ahead, in the main part of the room, is a table with a tactical map of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") marking the current status of the [civil war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"). On the left, against the southwest wall, is a bookcase holding eight common books, a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), and a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"). Against the northwest wall is a small square wooden table and two chairs, with a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), three [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), and a [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration") along with [plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate") and [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"). Beside this table are two smaller round tables holding [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and cheese and a sample of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton").

The northeast wall has a stairwell in the middle with flights leading up and down. To the left is a small cupboard, while to the right is a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl") of bread and a plate holding a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese") and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). To the right, against the southeast wall are two more bookcases holding a [potion of extreme stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extreme_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Extreme Stamina"), a [solution of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Strength "Skyrim:Solution of Strength"), and eleven common books. Farther to the right is an unlocked display case containing a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") and [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"). There are two more vases holding snowberry bushes, one halfway up the stairs and another at the top.

At the top of the stairs is a very large bedroom with a large double four-poster bed coming out from the southwest wall, with a basket containing a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") to the right, a small round table to the left with copies of *[Death of a Wanderer](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_of_a_Wanderer "Skyrim:Death of a Wanderer")* and *[Killing - Before You're Killed](/wiki/Skyrim:Killing_-_Before_You%27re_Killed "Skyrim:Killing - Before You're Killed")* on top, a long unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot of the bed, and a wall shelf above the bed on the southwest wall holding a common book and a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flower. In front of this is a narrow wooden table with a [platter](/wiki/Skyrim:Platter "Skyrim:Platter") on top holding an [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), three [tomatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato"), and two loaves of bread. Against the southwest wall, to the right of the bed is a washbasin on a stand next to a small wardrobe containing [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes"). Against the northwest wall is a small cupboard containing clutter and three vases, two of which hold snowberry bushes with the third holding tundra cotton. Farther to the right is a narrow table with a platter holding two [sweet rolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll") and two [honey nut treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat") and a plate holding a [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"). In front of the narrow table is a chair and a low table holding a plate of bread and cheese, a goblet, and a potion of regeneration.

In the eastern corner is a large planter with holding a plant. Against the southeast wall is a set of shelves holding a potion of health, a [potion of enhanced stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Enhanced_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Enhanced Stamina"), a potion of regeneration, a [potion of extra magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Extra Magicka"), two common books, a flute, and a drum. Next to this is a small set of shelves holding a bottle of alto wine and a vase with a bunch of tundra cotton in it. In front of the sets of shelves is a chair and a low table with a plate of bread and cheese, a goblet, and a potion of regeneration on top. In the southern corner is an open area with three tall wardrobes containing a collection of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") and fine clothes and a set of shelves holding two samples of [slaughterfish scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales"), a [potion of haggling](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Haggling "Skyrim:Potion of Haggling"), a bowl of [glow dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust"), two bottles of [frostbite venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Venom "Skyrim:Frostbite Venom"), a deathbell flower, a bowl of [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts"), and a basket holding two bunches of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender").

Descending the stairs leads to another room, this one covered in cobwebs and dust as if it hasn't been used in a while, with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand by the bottom of the stairs on the right. There are two single beds coming out from the rear wall, with a wall separating them. Both areas are the same with a single bed and a low empty table in each. In the enter of the room is a small square wooden table and chair, with a common book and [empty wine bottles](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle") on top of the table. Against the southeast wall is a small set of shelves holding a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") and a mead barrel, while against the northwest wall is a cupboard holding a few more empty bottles and other clutter. To the right, in the northern corner is a second cupboard, this one holding two sweet rolls, a bowl of tomatoes, a few loaves of bread, and several pieces of cheese, with a haunch of raw [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison") on top and [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels on either side.

## Notes

- Unless you are aligned with the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") or have completed [Search and Seizure](/wiki/Skyrim:Search_and_Seizure "Skyrim:Search and Seizure") for [Ondolemar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ondolemar "Skyrim:Ondolemar"), entering the headquarters is considered [trespassing](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime "Skyrim:Crime"), and taking anything in the building is considered stealing. However, as no NPCs are normally present in this cell, you are extremely unlikely to be caught. The building is therefore an easy place to target if the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") accepts a [bedlam job](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bedlam_Job "Skyrim:The Bedlam Job") contract in Solitude.

## Bugs

- The navmesh inside the building is incomplete.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
- After completing Battle for Solitude, the Imperial banners don't change for the Stormcloak ones. **?**

Become Thane of Eastmarch

## Radiant Options

This is a radiant quest which you can receive from either [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter") or [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak"), whichever is the jarl of Eastmarch. The jarl lives in the [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Befriend the Jarl of Eastmarch by progressing through the [civil war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") questline and complete quest [Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice").
2. Assist five people of Eastmarch.
3. Purchase [Hjerim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjerim "Skyrim:Hjerim").
4. Return to the jarl for your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

This is an umbrella quest, involving several other quests that must be completed if you wish to become Thane of Eastmarch. You will have to capture [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_from_Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Rescue from Fort Neugrad") for the Stormcloaks and complete quest [Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice") (if you joined the Stormcloaks) or complete the [Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm") (if you sided with the Imperials) before this quest becomes available. Once you have completed the prerequisite, speak with the jarl again and he will ask you to [assist the people of the hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Making_Friends_and_Influencing_People "Skyrim:Making Friends and Influencing People"). You must assist five people in the hold, usually by completing [favor quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Favors "Skyrim:Favors") for them. Note that many of the quest givers are non-essential NPCs, so their deaths would result in a loss of potential quests to complete. If they die after you assist them, they still count towards your Thane status. Also, you can befriend merchants if you have the [Investor](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor") perk by investing in their stores.

You must also purchase [Hjerim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjerim "Skyrim:Hjerim"), which costs 8,000 to 12,000 gold. Simply purchasing it is enough; there is no requirement to decorate, although it becomes more useful if decorated. Note that it cannot be decorated unless you have completed [Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice"), and if you have not started that quest yet you should start it before entering Hjerim.

### Eastmarch Favor Quests

Highlighted quests can be easily completed without any skill use. If any citizen offers multiple favor quests, only the first completed one will count towards Thaneship.

| Quest Giver | Giver Location | Quest | Objective(s) |

- Note that completing [Harsh Master](/wiki/Skyrim:Harsh_Master "Skyrim:Harsh Master") does not count towards this objective, as [Kjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Kjar "Skyrim:Kjar") is erroneously designated as a Winterhold citizen.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.

### Eastmarch Stores

[Investing](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor") 500 gold in certain stores will count towards Thaneship if you have not befriended the store's owner by other means. If the original owner dies and you had already invested in their store, you [can / cannot [*verification needed*]] also befriend their replacement.

| Merchant Name | Store Name | Store Location | Merchandise |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Nurelion](/wiki/Skyrim:Nurelion "Skyrim:Nurelion") ([Quintus Navale](/wiki/Skyrim:Quintus_Navale "Skyrim:Quintus Navale")) | [The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(place) "Skyrim:The White Phial (place)") | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") | Apothecary |
| [Oengul War-Anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Oengul_War-Anvil "Skyrim:Oengul War-Anvil") ([Hermir Strong-Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Hermir_Strong-Heart "Skyrim:Hermir Strong-Heart")) | [Blacksmith Quarters](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith_Quarters "Skyrim:Blacksmith Quarters") | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") | Blacksmith |
| [Revyn Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Revyn_Sadri "Skyrim:Revyn Sadri") | [Sadri's Used Wares](/wiki/Skyrim:Sadri%27s_Used_Wares "Skyrim:Sadri's Used Wares") | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") | General |
| [Wuunferth the Unliving](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuunferth_the_Unliving "Skyrim:Wuunferth the Unliving") | [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings") | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") | Spells |

### Other Quests

The following quests also increase the disposition of citizens of Eastmarch, and therefore count towards this objective:

- **[Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost")**: Help an orphaned [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") avoid being returned to a sadistic [caretaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind").
- **[Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East")**: Help the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") take care of some [pirates](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_Horker "Skyrim:Blood Horker").

### Reward

*How can I serve you, my Thane?*

After helping five inhabitants and purchasing [Hjerim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjerim "Skyrim:Hjerim"), the journal tells you to return to the jarl. The reward, the [Axe of Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Axe_of_Eastmarch "Skyrim:Axe of Eastmarch"), is a random, leveled, enchanted axe. There is a 50% chance that it will be a war axe (one-handed), and a 50% chance it will be a battleaxe (two-handed). You will also receive a housecarl named [Calder](/wiki/Skyrim:Calder "Skyrim:Calder"), who will be waiting for you at Hjerim.

## Notes

- Interestingly, when naming you Thane, Ulfric and Brunwulf do not say *"Wouldn't want them to think you're part of the common rabble, now."* like most other Jarls do.

## Bugs

- After finishing the quest "Battle for Windhelm" for the Imperials, Brunwulf Free-Winter sometimes won't appear in the Palace of the Kings. All Stormcloak-supporting jarls and their housecarls will be there sitting at a table, but without Brunwulf in the palace. Without him, you are unable to purchase Hjerim or become Thane of Eastmarch.
  - One of the possible fixes: use the Unrelenting Force shout on everyone at the dinner table. This will give you a bounty in each of the holds that the jarls are from. Travel out of Windhelm and return.
  - Using console command addfac 00050920 1 gives him new dialogue, but he still will not reside in the Palace of Kings. However, he should give you the Thane dialogue if you have already helped 5 citizens.
- After finishing the quest "Blood on the Ice", Ulfric Stormcloak sometimes won't offer the thaneship.

## Quest Stages

| Thane of Eastmarch (Favor254) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Purchase a house in Windhelm |
| 20 |  | *Objective 15:* Return to <Alias.ShortName=QuestGiver> |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 15, 25, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage Favor254 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest Favor254`.

Become Thane of Falkreath

## Radiant Options

This is a radiant quest which you can receive from either [Siddgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Siddgeir "Skyrim:Siddgeir") or [Dengeir of Stuhn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dengeir_of_Stuhn "Skyrim:Dengeir of Stuhn"), whichever is Jarl of Falkreath. The Jarl lives at the [Jarl's Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl%27s_Longhouse_(Falkreath) "Skyrim:Jarl's Longhouse (Falkreath)") in [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath").

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Befriend the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath").
2. Assist three people of [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold").
3. Return to the Jarl for your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

The invitation from the Jarl([HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"))

This is an umbrella quest for several other quests that must be completed if you wish to become Thane of Falkreath. In order to receive it, you must first aid the current Jarl of Falkreath. If Siddgeir is Jarl, the previous quest will usually be to [kill a Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader (Jarl)"); however, if he was ousted from Falkreath during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") and reinstated following [The Battle for Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Neugrad"), that is sufficient to begin this quest. If Dengeir is Jarl, whether he was installed via [Rescue from Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_from_Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Rescue from Fort Neugrad") or [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"), then the completion of that quest is sufficient to fulfill the prerequisite.

Once you have completed the prerequisite, speak with the jarl again and he will ask you to [assist the people of Falkreath hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Making_Friends_and_Influencing_People "Skyrim:Making Friends and Influencing People") three times in order to become Thane. This can be difficult as there are only a limited number of quests in the hold and the quest givers are non-essential, which could result in their death and irrevocable loss of potential quests. Note, however, that you can also befriend merchants if you have the [Investor](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor") perk by investing in their stores.

### Falkreath Favor Quests

Highlighted quests can be easily completed without any skill use.

| Quest Giver | Giver Location | Quest | Objective(s) |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Hert](/wiki/Skyrim:Hert "Skyrim:Hert") | [Half-Moon Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Half-Moon_Mill "Skyrim:Half-Moon Mill") | **[Chop Wood](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood")**: Get paid to chop firewood. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant")) | - Sell [Firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") to Hert |
| [Dengeir of Stuhn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dengeir_of_Stuhn "Skyrim:Dengeir of Stuhn") | [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"), [Dengeir's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Dengeir%27s_House "Skyrim:Dengeir's House") | **[Some Light Theft](/wiki/Skyrim:Some_Light_Theft "Skyrim:Some Light Theft")**: Do a favor by stealing an item. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant")) | - Steal the Private Letter for Dengeir - Bring the Private Letter to Dengeir |
| [Mathies](/wiki/Skyrim:Mathies "Skyrim:Mathies") | [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"), [Corpselight Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Corpselight_Farm "Skyrim:Corpselight Farm") | **[Gather Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat")**: Get paid to gather crops. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant")) | - Gather crops for Mathies |
| [Runil](/wiki/Skyrim:Runil "Skyrim:Runil") | [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"), [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Falkreath) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Falkreath)") | **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant")) | - Find Runil's Journal inside <Alias=Dungeon> - Return Runil's Journal to Runil |
| [Thadgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Thadgeir "Skyrim:Thadgeir") | [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"), [Dengeir's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Dengeir%27s_House "Skyrim:Dengeir's House") | **[Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery "Skyrim:Delivery")**: Deliver an item to an associate. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant")) | - Deliver Berit's Ashes to Runil |

Note that [Dark Ancestor](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Ancestor "Skyrim:Dark Ancestor") does not count towards this objective, as [Some Light Theft](/wiki/Skyrim:Some_Light_Theft "Skyrim:Some Light Theft") is a prerequisite and therefore nullifies the disposition increase. If Dengeir is Jarl, he will not give out either of his personal quests, but if you completed Some Light Theft for him before making him Jarl, then it will still count towards assisting the citizens of Falkreath.

### Falkreath Stores

[Investing](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor") 500 gold in certain stores will count towards Thaneship if you have not befriended the store's owner by other means.

| Merchant Name | Store Name | Store Location | Merchandise |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Solaf](/wiki/Skyrim:Solaf "Skyrim:Solaf") | [Gray Pine Goods](/wiki/Skyrim:Gray_Pine_Goods "Skyrim:Gray Pine Goods") | [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") | General; sells [Blue Mage Robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Blue Mage Robes") |

### Reward

After helping three inhabitants, the journal tells you to return to the jarl. The reward, the [Blade of Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Blade_of_Falkreath "Skyrim:Blade of Falkreath"), is a random, leveled, enchanted sword. There is a 50% chance that it will be a sword ([one-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed")), and a 50% chance it will be a greatsword ([two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed")). You will also receive a pittance of [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") and the title of Thane for Falkreath Hold. With the [Hearthfire add-on](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"), you will also be rewarded a personal [housecarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl"), [Rayya](/wiki/Skyrim:Rayya "Skyrim:Rayya").

## Notes

- Favours to Falkreath citizens done as part of Daedric quests do not count toward the total.
- The quest may become nearly impossible to complete if you finish the [Rescue from Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_from_Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Rescue from Fort Neugrad") quest of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") before you enter Falkreath, because the game does not accept radiant quests as favours.
  -  This can be fixed with the console codes `setstage favorjarlsmakefriends 95` and `setstage favor258 20`
- Assistance to citizens done prior to accepting this quest counts towards the total.

## Bugs

- Siddgeir may become stuck in a "Foe" relationship with you if you've killed his housecarl for the Dark Brotherhood (even if you did it secretly). If so, he'll never grant you Thaneship.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, addresses this issue. The relationship will only be harmed if you are caught killing the housecarl.
  -  You can fix this with the console command `player.setrelationshiprank 00019822 2`
  - If Siddgeir is no longer Jarl, the new Jarl will grant you Thaneship.
- [Zaria's](/wiki/Skyrim:Zaria "Skyrim:Zaria") store cannot be invested in with the Investor perk.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, addresses this issue. You can now befriend her by investing in her shop, which will count towards Thaneship.

## Quest Stages

| Thane of Falkreath (Favor258) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 15:* Return to <Alias.ShortName=QuestGiver> |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 10, 25, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage Favor258 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest Favor258`.

# Skyrim:Thane of Haafingar

## Overview

| |  |  |  | | --- | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Elisif's Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif%27s_Tribute "Skyrim:Elisif's Tribute") | **Concurrent** [Making Friends and Influencing People](/wiki/Skyrim:Making_Friends_and_Influencing_People "Skyrim:Making Friends and Influencing People") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Elisif's Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif%27s_Tribute "Skyrim:Elisif's Tribute") | | Concurrent | [Making Friends and Influencing People](/wiki/Skyrim:Making_Friends_and_Influencing_People "Skyrim:Making Friends and Influencing People") | | |

Become the Thane of Haafingar

## Quest Giver

This is a radiant quest. However, you can only receive it from [Elisif the Fair](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair"), as she is always the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar").

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Befriend the Jarl of Haafingar by completing her [favor quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif%27s_Tribute "Skyrim:Elisif's Tribute").
2. Assist five people of Haafingar.
3. Purchase [Proudspire Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proudspire_Manor "Skyrim:Proudspire Manor").
4. Return to the Jarl for your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

This is an umbrella quest for several other quests that must be completed if you wish to become Thane of Haafingar. The jarl requires you to buy the house in town as well as performing five favors for the townsfolk. Once this is achieved you can become Thane.

In order to receive this quest you must first aid the current jarl, [Elisif the Fair](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair"), by [investigating disturbances in a nearby cave](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen_Awakened "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen Awakened") and then completing her [favor quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif%27s_Tribute "Skyrim:Elisif's Tribute"). Once you have completed the prerequisite, speak with the jarl again and she will ask you to [assist the people of the hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Making_Friends_and_Influencing_People "Skyrim:Making Friends and Influencing People"). You must assist five people in the hold, usually by completing [favor quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Favors "Skyrim:Favors") for them. Note that many of the quest givers are non-essential NPCs, so their deaths would result in a loss of potential quests to complete. If they die after you assist them, they still count towards your Thane status. You can also befriend merchants if you have the [Investor](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor") perk by investing in their stores.

You must also purchase [Proudspire Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proudspire_Manor "Skyrim:Proudspire Manor"), which costs 25,000 gold. Simply purchasing it is enough, there is no requirement to decorate, although it becomes more useful if decorated.

### Haafingar Favor Quests

Highlighted quests can be easily completed without any skill use. If any citizen offers multiple favor quests, only the first completed one will count towards Thaneship.

### Haafingar Stores

[Investing](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor") 500 gold in certain stores will count towards Thaneship if you have not befriended the store's owner by other means. If the original owner dies and you had already invested in their store, you [can / cannot [*verification needed*]] also befriend their replacement.

### Other Quests

The following quests also increase the disposition of citizens of Haafingar, and therefore count towards this objective:

- [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity"), if you help [Erikur](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur "Skyrim:Erikur") talk to [Brelas](/wiki/Skyrim:Brelas "Skyrim:Brelas").
- **[The Man Who Cried Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Man_Who_Cried_Wolf "Skyrim:The Man Who Cried Wolf")**: Investigate reports of strange happenings in [Wolfskull Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave").
- **[Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames")**: Unveil the truth about a deceitful [King](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_One-Eye "Skyrim:Olaf One-Eye") and become a member of the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College").
- **[The Wolf Queen Awakened](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen_Awakened "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen Awakened")**: Potema must be stopped.

### Reward

After helping five inhabitants and purchasing [Proudspire Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proudspire_Manor "Skyrim:Proudspire Manor"), the journal tells you to return to the jarl. The reward, the [Blade of Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Blade_of_Haafingar "Skyrim:Blade of Haafingar"), is normally a random, leveled, enchanted sword or greatsword. Due to a [bug](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Bugs "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"), however, maces are also occasionally rewarded. You will also receive a housecarl named [Jordis the Sword-Maiden](/wiki/Skyrim:Jordis_the_Sword-Maiden "Skyrim:Jordis the Sword-Maiden"), who will be waiting for you at Proudspire Manor.

## Notes

- [Bryling](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling "Skyrim:Bryling") is also set up to give you this quest; she's part of the relevant faction, is included in the related scripting, and has the lines recorded in her voice type. However, since at no point in the final game is there an opportunity for Bryling to become Jarl of Haafingar, this functionality goes completely unused.
- If the quest [Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames") is active, Elisif might not give the dialogue option to start this quest until after the Tending the Flames quest is complete.

## Bugs

- When you become Thane of Haafingar under Imperial rule, the guards do not recognize you as such and there is no thane option to forgive you of petty crime. However, Stormcloak guards in the same city do have this option.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
  - If you become Thane of Haafingar while it is under Imperial rule, and it later is conquered by the Stormcloaks, you retain your Thane status and can use it to remove a bounty then.
- If you complete all five favors before being given the quest to do so, the quest will not update correctly, leaving you with a journal entry "Assist the People of Haafingar 5/5".
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
  - To fix this, complete a sixth favor, such as the Tending the Flames quest, which will give you the message "Completed: Assist the People of Haafingar 6/5", thus allowing you to continue on as intended.
  -  Use the console command `player.setobjectivecompleted favorjarlsmakefriends 30 1` to update it and remove it from your journal.
- The quest may not track how many favors you have performed, making it impossible to complete the quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
- If you have the quest "Tending the Flames" active, Elisif will not give you the quest until you reach the stage where you need to speak to Jorn. **?**

## Quest Stages

| Thane of Haafingar (Favor252) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Purchase a house in Solitude |
| 20 |  | *Objective 15:* Return to <Alias.ShortName=QuestGiver> |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 15, 25, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage Favor252 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest Favor252`.

Become the Thane of Hjaalmarch

## Radiant Options

This is a radiant quest which you can receive from either [Idgrod Ravencrone](/wiki/Skyrim:Idgrod_Ravencrone "Skyrim:Idgrod Ravencrone") or [Sorli the Builder](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorli_the_Builder "Skyrim:Sorli the Builder"), whichever is the Jarl of Hjaalmarch. The jarl lives in [Highmoon Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Highmoon_Hall "Skyrim:Highmoon Hall") in [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). You must assist three people.

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Befriend the Jarl of Hjaalmarch.
2. Assist three people of Hjaalmarch.
3. Return to the jarl for your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

This is an umbrella quest for several other quests which must be completed if you wish to become Thane of Hjaalmarch. In order to receive this quest, you must first aid the current jarl. You must usually complete [Laid to Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Laid_to_Rest "Skyrim:Laid to Rest") first if the jarl is Idgrod; however, you can begin the quest if she was ousted from Morthal during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") and reinstated following [The Battle for Fort Snowhawk](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Snowhawk_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Snowhawk (Imperial)"). You can also begin the quest if the jarl is Sorli, whether she was installed via [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") or [The Battle for Fort Snowhawk](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Snowhawk_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Snowhawk (Stormcloaks)").

Once you have completed the prerequisite, speak with the jarl again and she will ask you to [assist the people of the hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Making_Friends_and_Influencing_People "Skyrim:Making Friends and Influencing People"). You must assist three people in the hold, usually by completing [favor quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Favors "Skyrim:Favors") for them. Note that many of the quest givers are non-essential NPCs, so their deaths would result in a loss of potential quests . If they die after you assist them, they still count towards your Thane status. You can also befriend merchants if you have the [Investor](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor") perk by investing in their stores.

### Hjaalmarch Favor Quests

Highlighted quests can be easily completed without any skill use.

| Quest Giver | Giver Location | Quest | Objective(s) |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Benor](/wiki/Skyrim:Benor "Skyrim:Benor") | [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"), [Guardhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Guardhouse "Skyrim:Guardhouse") | **[Fight! Fight!](/wiki/Skyrim:Fight!_Fight! "Skyrim:Fight! Fight!")**: Prove your strength by wagering on a fist fight with another. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant")) |  |
| [Gestur Rockbreaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Gestur_Rockbreaker "Skyrim:Gestur Rockbreaker") | [Stonehills](/wiki/Skyrim:Stonehills "Skyrim:Stonehills"), [Rockwallow Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Rockwallow_Mine "Skyrim:Rockwallow Mine") | **[Mine Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore")**: Get paid to [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") ore. | [Jorgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorgen "Skyrim:Jorgen") | [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"), [Jorgen and Lami's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorgen_and_Lami%27s_House "Skyrim:Jorgen and Lami's House") | **[Chop Wood](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood")**: Get paid to chop firewood. Note that [Falion's Secret](/wiki/Skyrim:Falion%27s_Secret "Skyrim:Falion's Secret"), [Payment Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Payment_Delivery "Skyrim:Payment Delivery") and [Rising at Dawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Rising_at_Dawn "Skyrim:Rising at Dawn") do not count towards this objective, as they do not affect anyone's disposition.

### Hjaalmarch Stores

[Investing](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor") 500 gold in certain stores will count towards Thaneship if you have not befriended the store's owner by other means.

| Merchant Name | Store Name | Store Location | Merchandise |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Lami](/wiki/Skyrim:Lami "Skyrim:Lami") | [Thaumaturgist's Hut](/wiki/Skyrim:Thaumaturgist%27s_Hut "Skyrim:Thaumaturgist's Hut") | [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") | Apothecary |

### Reward

After helping three inhabitants, the journal tells you to return to the jarl. Note that Idgrod in this context refers to [Jarl Idgrod (The Elder)](/wiki/Skyrim:Idgrod_Ravencrone "Skyrim:Idgrod Ravencrone"), not her daughter [Idgrod the Younger](/wiki/Skyrim:Idgrod_the_Younger "Skyrim:Idgrod the Younger"). The reward, the [Blade of Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Blade_of_Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Blade of Hjaalmarch"), is a random, leveled, enchanted sword. There is a 50% chance that it will be a sword (one-handed), and a 50% chance it will be a greatsword (two-handed). Due to a [bug](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Bugs "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"), however, maces are also occasionally awarded. You also gain the title of Thane of Hjaalmarch and, if [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") is installed, a personal housecarl, [Valdimar](/wiki/Skyrim:Valdimar "Skyrim:Valdimar").

## Quest Stages

| Thane of Hjaalmarch (Favor255) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 15:* Return to <Alias.ShortName=QuestGiver> |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 10, 25, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage Favor255 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest Favor255`.
