Become the Thane of the Pale

## Radiant Options

This is a radiant quest which you can receive from either [Skald](/wiki/Skyrim:Skald "Skyrim:Skald") or [Brina Merilis](/wiki/Skyrim:Brina_Merilis "Skyrim:Brina Merilis"), whichever is the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of the Pale. The Jarl lives in [The White Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Hall "Skyrim:The White Hall") in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar").

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Befriend the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale").
2. Assist three people of the Pale.
3. Return to the jarl for your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

This is an umbrella quest for several other quests that must be completed if you wish to become [Thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") of [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale"). In order to receive this quest you must first aid the current [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl"). If [Skald](/wiki/Skyrim:Skald "Skyrim:Skald") is Jarl of the Pale, then normally, you must first complete [Waking Nightmare](/wiki/Skyrim:Waking_Nightmare "Skyrim:Waking Nightmare") and then [Kill the Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Giant_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Giant (Jarl)") in order to befriend him. If Skald was ousted from [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"), and then reinstated after [The Battle for Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Dunstad_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Dunstad (Stormcloaks)"), that will also befriend him. If [Brina](/wiki/Skyrim:Brina_Merilis "Skyrim:Brina Merilis") is Jarl of the Pale (whether she was installed via [The Battle for Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Dunstad_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Dunstad (Imperial)") or [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending")), then she is automatically friendly to you.

Once you have completed the prerequisite, speak with the jarl again and he or she will ask you to [assist the people of the hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Making_Friends_and_Influencing_People "Skyrim:Making Friends and Influencing People"). In order to assist the people of the hold, you must befriend three people who are citizens of the Pale. Usually you do this by completing [favor quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Favors "Skyrim:Favors") on their behalf. All of the favor quests in the Pale are for people in Dawnstar, except for Aeri, who lives at [Anga's Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Anga%27s_Mill "Skyrim:Anga's Mill"). Note that you can also befriend merchants if you have the [Investor](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor") perk by investing in their stores.

### The Pale Favor Quests

Highlighted quests can be easily completed without any skill use. If any citizen offers multiple favor quests, only the first completed one will count towards Thaneship.

| Quest Giver | Giver Location | Quest | Objective(s) |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Beitild](/wiki/Skyrim:Beitild "Skyrim:Beitild") | [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), [Iron-Breaker Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron-Breaker_Mine "Skyrim:Iron-Breaker Mine") | **[Mine Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore")**: Get paid to [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") ore. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant")) |  |
| [Captain Wayfinder](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Wayfinder "Skyrim:Captain Wayfinder") | [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), [The Sea Squall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Sea_Squall "Skyrim:The Sea Squall") | **[Salty Sea-Dogs](/wiki/Skyrim:Salty_Sea-Dogs "Skyrim:Salty Sea-Dogs")**: Find some [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine-Cut_Void_Salts "Skyrim:Fine-Cut Void Salts") for an inexperienced [sea captain](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Wayfinder "Skyrim:Captain Wayfinder"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant")) | - Find the Fine-Cut Void Salts for Wayfinder - Bring the Fine-Cut Void Salts to Wayfinder |
| [Frida](/wiki/Skyrim:Frida "Skyrim:Frida") | [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), [The Mortar and Pestle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mortar_and_Pestle "Skyrim:The Mortar and Pestle") | **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant")) | - Find Ring of Pure Mixtures inside <Alias=Dungeon> - Return Ring of Pure Mixtures to Frida |
| [Karl](/wiki/Skyrim:Karl "Skyrim:Karl") | [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), [Iron-Breaker Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron-Breaker_Mine "Skyrim:Iron-Breaker Mine") | **[Quest all Drunks Have](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_all_Drunks_Have "Skyrim:Quest all Drunks Have")**: Make a drunk dance for joy. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant")) |  |
| [Leigelf](/wiki/Skyrim:Leigelf "Skyrim:Leigelf") | [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), [Quicksilver Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Mine "Skyrim:Quicksilver Mine") | **[Mine Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore")**: Get paid to [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") ore. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant")) |  |
| [Rustleif](/wiki/Skyrim:Rustleif "Skyrim:Rustleif") | [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), [Rustleif's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Rustleif%27s_House "Skyrim:Rustleif's House") | **[Rare Gifts](/wiki/Skyrim:Rare_Gifts "Skyrim:Rare Gifts")**: Do a favor by finding a rare item. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant")) | - Bring one Night Falls on Sentinel to Rustleif |
| [Aeri](/wiki/Skyrim:Aeri "Skyrim:Aeri") | [Anga's Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Anga%27s_Mill "Skyrim:Anga's Mill"), [Aeri's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Aeri%27s_House "Skyrim:Aeri's House") | **[Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery "Skyrim:Delivery")**: Deliver an item to an associate. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant")) | - Deliver Aeri's Note to Skald |
| **[Chop Wood](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood")**: Get paid to chop firewood. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant")) |  |

### The Pale Stores

[Investing](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor") 500 gold in certain stores will count towards Thaneship if you have not befriended the store's owner by other means.

| Merchant Name | Store Name | Store Location | Merchandise |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Frida](/wiki/Skyrim:Frida "Skyrim:Frida") | [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") | [The Mortar and Pestle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mortar_and_Pestle "Skyrim:The Mortar and Pestle") | Apothecary |
| [Rustleif](/wiki/Skyrim:Rustleif "Skyrim:Rustleif"); [Seren](/wiki/Skyrim:Seren "Skyrim:Seren") | [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") | [Rustleif's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Rustleif%27s_House "Skyrim:Rustleif's House") | Blacksmith |

### Reward

After helping three inhabitants, the journal tells you to return to the jarl. The Blade of the Pale is awarded along with the title. The Blade of the Pale is a randomly-leveled and randomly-enchanted sword. There is a 50% chance that it will be a [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), and a 50% chance it will be a [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"). If you have [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") installed, then [Gregor](/wiki/Skyrim:Gregor "Skyrim:Gregor") will also be assigned to you as a housecarl.

## Notes

- It is possible to become Thane of the Pale and receive a leveled Blade of Pale twice. First from Skald and then from Brina.

- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage Favor256 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest Favor256`.

# Skyrim:Thane of the Reach

## Overview

|  |
| --- |

Become Thane of the Reach

## Radiant Options

This is a radiant quest which you can receive from [Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund") or [Thongvor Silver-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Thongvor_Silver-Blood "Skyrim:Thongvor Silver-Blood"), whichever is Jarl of the Reach. The jarl lives in [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep") in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). The jarl can be found in multiple places - arguing with [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo"), roaming the halls, sleeping in his bedroom or sitting on the throne.

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Befriend the Jarl of the Reach.
2. Assist five people of the Reach.
3. Purchase [Vlindrel Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Vlindrel_Hall "Skyrim:Vlindrel Hall").
4. Return to the jarl for your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

This is an umbrella quest for several other quests that must be completed if you wish to become Thane of the Reach. The Jarl requires you buy the house in town as well as performing five favors for the townsfolk. Once this is achieved you can become Thane.

In order to receive this quest you must first aid the current Jarl. If the Jarl is Igmund, then you must usually [kill a Forsworn leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Forsworn_Leader_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Forsworn Leader (Jarl)") and [Find Hrolfdir's Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Jarl_-_Hagravens) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Jarl - Hagravens)"); however, if he was ousted from [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") and reinstated following [The Battle for Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Sungard_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Sungard (Imperial)"), that is sufficient to begin this quest. If the Jarl is Thongvor, whether he was installed via [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") or [The Battle for Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Sungard_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Sungard (Stormcloaks)"), then the completion of that quest is sufficient to fulfill the prerequisite.

Once you have completed the prerequisite, speak with the Jarl again and he will ask you to [assist the people of the hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Making_Friends_and_Influencing_People "Skyrim:Making Friends and Influencing People"). You must assist five people in the hold, usually by completing [favor quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Favors "Skyrim:Favors") for them. Note that many of the quest givers are non-essential NPCs, so their deaths would result in a loss of potential quests to complete. If they die after you assist them, they still count towards your Thane status. You can also befriend merchants if you have the [Investor](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor") perk by investing in their stores.

Note that there are several favor quests involving members of Orc strongholds in the Reach; assisting Orcs living in strongholds does not count towards your Thane quest, but Orcs in Markarth do count.

You may consider completing [The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella") as successfully completing it befriends all four of the priestesses of Dibella, which is almost enough to qualify for thaneship alone. It also requires you to visit [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten"); resolving the [Sanuarach mine dispute](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanuarach_Mine_(quest) "Skyrim:Sanuarach Mine (quest)") there (for either side) will be enough to complete this requirement.

You must also purchase [Vlindrel Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Vlindrel_Hall "Skyrim:Vlindrel Hall"), which costs 8,000 gold. Simply purchasing it is enough, there is no requirement to decorate, although it becomes more useful if decorated.

### The Reach Favor Quests

Highlighted quests can be easily completed without any skill use. If any citizen offers multiple favor quests, only the first completed one will count towards Thaneship.

### The Reach Stores

[Investing](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor") 500 gold in certain stores will count towards Thaneship if you have not befriended the store's owner by other means. If the original owner dies and you had already invested in their store, you [can / cannot [*verification needed*]] also befriend their replacement.

| Merchant Name | Store Name | Store Location | Merchandise |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Bothela](/wiki/Skyrim:Bothela "Skyrim:Bothela") ([Muiri](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri "Skyrim:Muiri")) | [The Hag's Cure](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Hag%27s_Cure "Skyrim:The Hag's Cure") | [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | Apothecary |
| [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo") | in [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep") | [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | Spells |
| [Ghorza gra-Bagol](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghorza_gra-Bagol "Skyrim:Ghorza gra-Bagol") ([Tacitus Sallustius](/wiki/Skyrim:Tacitus_Sallustius "Skyrim:Tacitus Sallustius")) [*verification needed — investment bugged - does it affect Disposition?*] | at the forge near [The Hag's Cure](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Hag%27s_Cure "Skyrim:The Hag's Cure") | [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | Blacksmith |
| [Lisbet](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisbet "Skyrim:Lisbet") ([Imedhnain](/wiki/Skyrim:Imedhnain "Skyrim:Imedhnain")) | [Arnleif and Sons Trading Company](/wiki/Skyrim:Arnleif_and_Sons_Trading_Company "Skyrim:Arnleif and Sons Trading Company") | [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | General |
| [Moth gro-Bagol](/wiki/Skyrim:Moth_gro-Bagol "Skyrim:Moth gro-Bagol") [*verification needed — investment bugged - does it affect Disposition?*] | in [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep") | [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | Blacksmith |

### Other Quests

The following quests also increase the disposition of citizens of the Reach, and therefore count towards this objective:

- **[The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love")**: Help the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") spread the cause of love throughout Skyrim.
- **[The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella")**: Find a new [Sybil](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra") for the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella").
- [New Allegiances](/wiki/Skyrim:New_Allegiances "Skyrim:New Allegiances"): If you turn [Cairine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cairine "Skyrim:Cairine") into a Vampire.
- **[Private Lessons](/wiki/Skyrim:Private_Lessons "Skyrim:Private Lessons")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"): Teach [Lynea](/wiki/Skyrim:Lynea "Skyrim:Lynea") how to fish.

### Reward

After helping five inhabitants and purchasing [Vlindrel Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Vlindrel_Hall "Skyrim:Vlindrel Hall"), the journal tells you to return to the Jarl. The reward, the [Blade of the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blade_of_the_Reach "Skyrim:Blade of the Reach"), is a random, leveled, enchanted axe. There is a 50% chance that it will be a war axe (one-handed), and a 50% chance it will be a battleaxe (two-handed). You will also receive a housecarl named [Argis the Bulwark](/wiki/Skyrim:Argis_the_Bulwark "Skyrim:Argis the Bulwark"), who will be waiting for you at Vlindrel Hall.

## Bugs

- The misnamed [Blade of the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blade_of_the_Reach "Skyrim:Blade of the Reach") is an axe (not a blade).
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, fixes this bug.
- The weapon may not place properly on weapon racks or plaques. Even on racks it will place horizontally, with the blade part of the axe not showing.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- The dialogue option to start the thane quest may not appear. This happens if you have too many unfinished miscellaneous favor quests in your quest log. Do a few of these quests and the thane dialogue will appear.

## Quest Stages

| Thane of the Reach (Favor250) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Purchase a house in Markarth |
| 20 |  | *Objective 15:* Return to <Alias.ShortName=QuestGiver> |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 15, 25, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage Favor250 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest Favor250`.

| |  |  |  | | --- | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)") | **Concurrent** [Making Friends and Influencing People](/wiki/Skyrim:Making_Friends_and_Influencing_People "Skyrim:Making Friends and Influencing People") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)") | | Concurrent | [Making Friends and Influencing People](/wiki/Skyrim:Making_Friends_and_Influencing_People "Skyrim:Making Friends and Influencing People") | | |

Regain your thaneship

## Quest Giver

This is a radiant quest; however, unlike most of the other thane quests, you can only receive it when [Vignar Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Vignar_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Vignar Gray-Mane") is Jarl of Whiterun. If Balgruuf is the jarl, you can only become Thane of Whiterun by completing [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising").

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Assist the people of Whiterun Hold.
2. Purchase [Breezehome](/wiki/Skyrim:Breezehome "Skyrim:Breezehome").
3. Return to the jarl for your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

This is an umbrella quest for several other quests that must be completed if you wish to become Thane of Whiterun. In order for Vignar to be jarl, you have to have completed [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)") for the Stormcloaks. Completing this quest befriends him automatically.

Speak with the jarl and he will ask you to [assist the people of the hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Making_Friends_and_Influencing_People "Skyrim:Making Friends and Influencing People"). You must assist five people in the hold, usually by completing [favor quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Favors "Skyrim:Favors") for them. Note that many of the quest givers are non-essential NPCs, so their deaths would result in a loss of potential quests to complete. If they die after you assist them, they still count towards your Thane status. You can also befriend merchants if you have the [Investor](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor") perk by investing in their stores.

You must also purchase [Breezehome](/wiki/Skyrim:Breezehome "Skyrim:Breezehome"), which costs 5,000 gold, if you have not done so already. Simply purchasing it is enough, there is no requirement to decorate, although it becomes more useful if decorated.

### Whiterun Favor Quests

Highlighted quests can be easily completed without any skill use. If any citizen offers multiple favor quests, only the first completed one will count towards Thaneship.

### Whiterun Stores

[Investing](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor") 500 gold in certain stores will count towards Thaneship if you have not befriended the store's owner by other means. If the original owner dies and you had already invested in their store, you [can / cannot [*verification needed*]] also befriend their replacement.

### Other Quests

The following quests also increase the disposition of citizens of Whiterun, and therefore count towards this objective:

- **[Before the Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Storm "Skyrim:Before the Storm")**: Inform the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") about the dragon attack on [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen").
- **[A Blade in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Blade_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:A Blade in the Dark")**: Prove you are Dragonborn to [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine") by slaying the dragon [Sahloknir](/wiki/Skyrim:Sahloknir "Skyrim:Sahloknir").
- **[The Blessings of Nature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Blessings_of_Nature "Skyrim:The Blessings of Nature")**: Restore the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") for [Danica Pure-Spring](/wiki/Skyrim:Danica_Pure-Spring "Skyrim:Danica Pure-Spring").
- **[The Golden Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Golden_Claw "Skyrim:The Golden Claw")**: A [shopkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Lucan_Valerius "Skyrim:Lucan Valerius") wants you to retrieve his [prized possession](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Claw "Skyrim:Golden Claw") from a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Arvel_the_Swift "Skyrim:Arvel the Swift").
- **[Missing In Action](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_In_Action "Skyrim:Missing In Action")**: Rescue a [missing Stormcloak supporter](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorald_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Thorald Gray-Mane") from the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor").

### Reward

After helping five inhabitants and purchasing [Breezehome](/wiki/Skyrim:Breezehome "Skyrim:Breezehome"), the journal tells you to return to the jarl. The reward, the [Blade of Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Blade_of_Whiterun "Skyrim:Blade of Whiterun"), is a random, leveled, enchanted blade. There is a 50% chance that it will be a sword (one-handed), and a 50% chance it will be a greatsword (two-handed).

- - This is changed with version 2.1.3 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch").

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 15, 25, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage Favor253 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest Favor253`.

Become Thane of Winterhold

## Radiant Options

This is a radiant quest that you can receive from either [Korir](/wiki/Skyrim:Korir "Skyrim:Korir") or [Kraldar](/wiki/Skyrim:Kraldar "Skyrim:Kraldar"), whichever is the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)"). The jarl lives at the [Jarl's Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl%27s_Longhouse_(Winterhold) "Skyrim:Jarl's Longhouse (Winterhold)") in [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold").

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Befriend the Jarl of Winterhold.
2. Assist three people of Winterhold.
3. Return to the jarl for your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

This is an umbrella quest for several other quests that must be completed to become Thane of Winterhold. In order to receive this quest you must first aid the current jarl. If the jarl is Korir, then you must usually [Retrieve the Helm of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Jarl_-_Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Jarl - Caves)") for him first; however, if he was ousted from Winterhold during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") and reinstated following [The Battle for Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Kastav"), that is sufficient to begin this quest. If the jarl is Kraldar, whether he was installed via [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") or [Rescue from Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_from_Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:Rescue from Fort Kastav"), then the completion of that quest is sufficient to fulfill the prerequisite.

Once you have completed the prerequisite, speak with the jarl again and he will ask you to [assist the people of the hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Making_Friends_and_Influencing_People "Skyrim:Making Friends and Influencing People"). You must assist three people in the hold, usually by completing [favor quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Favors "Skyrim:Favors") for them. Note that many of the quest givers are non-essential NPCs, so their deaths would result in a loss of potential quests to complete. If they die after you assist them, they still count towards your Thane status. You can also befriend merchants if you have the [Investor](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor") perk by investing in their stores.

### Winterhold Favor Quests

Highlighted quests can be easily completed without any skill use.

| Quest Giver | Giver Location | Quest | Objective(s) |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Haran](/wiki/Skyrim:Haran "Skyrim:Haran") | [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"), [The Frozen Hearth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Frozen_Hearth "Skyrim:The Frozen Hearth") | **[A Few Words with You](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Few_Words_with_You "Skyrim:A Few Words with You")**: Do a favor by talking to someone about a problem. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant")) | - Talk to Ranmir about Haran - Tell Haran that Ranmir is taken care of |
| [Malur Seloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Malur_Seloth "Skyrim:Malur Seloth") | [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"), [Jarl's Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl%27s_Longhouse_(Winterhold) "Skyrim:Jarl's Longhouse (Winterhold)") | **[Some Light Theft](/wiki/Skyrim:Some_Light_Theft "Skyrim:Some Light Theft")**: Do a favor by stealing an item. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant")) | - Steal the Staff of Arcane Authority for Malur - Bring the Staff of Arcane Authority to Malur |
| [Thorgar](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorgar "Skyrim:Thorgar") | [Whistling Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Whistling_Mine "Skyrim:Whistling Mine") | **[Mine Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore")**: Get paid to [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") ore. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant")) |  |
| [Ranmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranmir "Skyrim:Ranmir") | [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"), [Birna's Oddments](/wiki/Skyrim:Birna%27s_Oddments "Skyrim:Birna's Oddments") | **[Quest all Drunks Have](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_all_Drunks_Have "Skyrim:Quest all Drunks Have")**: Make a drunk dance for joy. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant")) |  |

Note that completing [Drowned Sorrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Drowned_Sorrows "Skyrim:Drowned Sorrows") does not count towards this objective, as it does not affect anyone's disposition. Be sure to complete [Ranmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranmir "Skyrim:Ranmir")'s [Quest all Drunks Have](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_all_Drunks_Have "Skyrim:Quest all Drunks Have") before starting Drowned Sorrows, as he is removed from the game upon its completion.

### Winterhold Stores

[Investing](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor") 500 gold in certain stores will count towards Thaneship if you have not befriended the store's owner by other means.

| Merchant Name | Store Name | Store Location | Merchandise |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Birna](/wiki/Skyrim:Birna "Skyrim:Birna") | [Birna's Oddments](/wiki/Skyrim:Birna%27s_Oddments "Skyrim:Birna's Oddments") | [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") | General |

### Other Quests

The following quests also increase the disposition of citizens of Winterhold, and therefore count towards this objective:

- **[The Black Star](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Star "Skyrim:The Black Star")**: Help find and repair [Azura's Star](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star "Skyrim:Azura's Star").
- **[New Allegiances](/wiki/Skyrim:New_Allegiances "Skyrim:New Allegiances")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Turn the target into a [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### College Quests

Completing any quest which increases the disposition of the mages at the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") will also count towards this objective, including:

- **[Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor")**: Uncover an ancient Dwemer secret. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Brelyna's Practice](/wiki/Skyrim:Brelyna%27s_Practice "Skyrim:Brelyna's Practice")**: Help [Brelyna Maryon](/wiki/Skyrim:Brelyna_Maryon "Skyrim:Brelyna Maryon") by allowing her to practice her spells on you.
- **[Fetch me that Book!](/wiki/Skyrim:Fetch_me_that_Book! "Skyrim:Fetch me that Book!")**: Fetch a book for [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant")) (second time only)
- **[First Lessons](/wiki/Skyrim:First_Lessons "Skyrim:First Lessons")**: Join the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)").
- **[J'zargo's Experiment](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27zargo%27s_Experiment "Skyrim:J'zargo's Experiment")**: Help [a student](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27zargo "Skyrim:J'zargo") test out a fiery new spell.
- **[Onmund's Request](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund%27s_Request "Skyrim:Onmund's Request")**: Help [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") negotiate the return of a family amulet from [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Out of Balance](/wiki/Skyrim:Out_of_Balance "Skyrim:Out of Balance")**: Purify the focus points for magical energy around the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)").
- **[Restocking Soul Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Restocking_Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Restocking Soul Gems")**: Help [Sergius Turrianus](/wiki/Skyrim:Sergius_Turrianus "Skyrim:Sergius Turrianus") to fill his stock with [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems").

[Enchanting Pick-Up](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting_Pick-Up "Skyrim:Enchanting Pick-Up") and [Shalidor's Insights](/wiki/Skyrim:Shalidor%27s_Insights "Skyrim:Shalidor's Insights") do not count as they do not affect anyone's disposition.

### Reward

After helping three inhabitants, the journal tells you to return to the jarl. The reward, the [Blade of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Blade_of_Winterhold "Skyrim:Blade of Winterhold"), is a random, leveled, enchanted sword. There is a 50% chance that it will be a sword (one-handed), and a 50% chance it will be a greatsword (two-handed).

## Bugs

- Completing [Harsh Master](/wiki/Skyrim:Harsh_Master "Skyrim:Harsh Master") for [Kjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Kjar "Skyrim:Kjar") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") counts toward this quest because he is erroneously designated as a Winterhold citizen.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Thane of Winterhold (Favor257) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 15:* Return to <Alias.ShortName=QuestGiver> |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 10, 25, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage Favor257 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest Favor257`.

# Skyrim:Thane

## Overview

**Thane** is an honorary title presented by the [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of a [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") to individuals of high esteem. The bestowed title is one of both recognition and prestige. Thanes may be chosen due to their importance to the city or for their heroic deeds. It is possible to become a thane of every hold regardless of which side in the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") is chosen (although it is impossible to become Thane of [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") if no side is chosen). Each jarl has their own requirements for the title and may bestow the honor on multiple people.

## Benefits of Being a Thane

- Grants you a personal [housecarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl") [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") (if available).
- Grants you a symbolic weapon of the city.
- Guards will forgive any [bounty](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime#Bounties "Skyrim:Crime") of less than 2000 gold (once per hold). However, a crime can be pardoned twice if a hold is captured during the civil war and the new jarl appoints the player thane.

## Becoming a Thane

The general process for becoming a thane comes down to a relatively general formula with the exception of Whiterun, where it is initially achieved by completing the quest [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") and does not require the steps below to complete, unless you have joined the Stormcloaks and completed [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)").

1. You befriend the jarl through a quest or favors.
2. The jarl asks you to demonstrate your value to the hold by [assisting the people](/wiki/Skyrim:Making_Friends_and_Influencing_People "Skyrim:Making Friends and Influencing People") in the hold, five people in holds with major cities and three people in the other holds.
3. The jarl asks you to purchase a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") in the city if the hold is one of the five with major cities: Whiterun (Whiterun), The Rift (Riften), Eastmarch (Windhelm), Haafingar (Solitude), and The Reach (Markarth).
4. The jarl grants the title of thane and all that comes with it.

If [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") is installed, then the three minor holds of Falkreath (Falkreath), Hjaalmarch (Morthal), and The Pale (Dawnstar) will also appoint a housecarl and grant the right to purchase a plot of land on which you may [build your own residence](/wiki/Skyrim:Construction "Skyrim:Construction"). Your housecarl can be taken as your follower or will otherwise remain in the jarl's residence awaiting instructions. The same happens if you are granted the thaneship of Whiterun during the [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") quest. Thus, only Winterhold lacks the opportunity for the player to acquire a residence in the hold; likewise, there is no housecarl available for the player in Winterhold.

Progress made in assisting the people is dependent on disposition of citizens of the hold. Each citizen whose [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") is raised to friend counts towards the objective. If you raise someone's disposition before the objective to assist the people is given, that will still be taken into account. Note that if you befriend the same citizen twice, it only counts once for the thane quest. Also, if a friend dies, you do not lose progress (usually in those cases, you will have received an [Inheritance](/wiki/Skyrim:Inheritance "Skyrim:Inheritance").) In most cases, there is one quest for each citizen which will befriend him/her. Some citizens may have more than one quest which will befriend them. Many citizens have no specific quest available at all. A friend must be an ordinary citizen of the hold, not just living in it; members of [Khajiit caravans](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_Traders "Skyrim:Khajiit Traders") and [Orc strongholds](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") do not count towards the total. Befriending the Jarl also doesn't count as that is a prerequisite to being given the objective.

The thane quests and their general pieces are related below:

[^a](#note_Unending)If [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") has been used to change the jarls of holds, the new jarls will allow you to become thane without completing any other prerequisite quests, with the exception of the Jarl of the Rift.

[^b](#note_Weapon)All honorary weapons listed are randomly assigned enchanted melee weapons. More information can be found on [this page](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Enchanted_Weapons "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

[^c](#note_Whiterun)Dragon Rising grants thane status by itself. There are no further requirements to become Thane of Whiterun if Balgruuf is still Jarl of Whiterun, and there is no other way to become Thane of Whiterun while he is Jarl.

[^d](#note_Elisif)Elisif the Fair remains Jarl of Haafingar even if it is conquered by the Stormcloaks.

[^e](#note_Windhelm)It is impossible to become Thane of Eastmarch without taking one or the other side in the Civil War: you must either join the Stormcloaks to win Ulfric's favor and commit permanently to their side by conquering Whiterun for them (which is beyond the point-of-no-return that allows defecting to the Imperials), or join the Legion, win the civil war outright for the Empire (since the city cannot change hands during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending")), remove Ulfric from power in Windhelm and curry favor with his pro-Imperial replacement.

[†](#note_Blade_of_the_Rift)The "Blade of the Rift" is never actually given as a reward: instead, you will receive a generic un-renamed enchanted weapon.

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.

## NPC Thanes

NPCs that are thanes are typically identified through dialogue. There is no specific faction marking for thanes.

Thane Erikur of Haafingar

| Name | Hold | House | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Bryling](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling "Skyrim:Bryling") | [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | [Bryling's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling%27s_House "Skyrim:Bryling's House") | Owns [Rockwallow Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Rockwallow_Mine "Skyrim:Rockwallow Mine"). |
| [Dengeir of Stuhn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dengeir_of_Stuhn "Skyrim:Dengeir of Stuhn") | [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | [Dengeir's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Dengeir%27s_House "Skyrim:Dengeir's House") | Former Jarl of Falkreath, deposed by his nephew [Siddgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Siddgeir "Skyrim:Siddgeir"). Siding with the Stormcloaks will allow him to regain the title of Jarl. |
| [Erikur](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur "Skyrim:Erikur") | [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | [Erikur's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur%27s_House "Skyrim:Erikur's House") | Sister is [Gisli](/wiki/Skyrim:Gisli "Skyrim:Gisli"). |

[Mjoll the Lioness](/wiki/Skyrim:Mjoll_the_Lioness "Skyrim:Mjoll the Lioness") is declared by [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift")'s jarl, [Laila Law-Giver](/wiki/Skyrim:Laila_Law-Giver "Skyrim:Laila Law-Giver"), to be a champion of the people. Her virtue and heroic nature are extolled by Laila, but this only represents one facet of being a thane.

## Notes

- If the jarl that named you thane is replaced through the events of the Civil War or via [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"), you will lose the title, though you can regain it by speaking to the new jarl. You do not need to complete favor tasks a second time, because the new jarl is always grateful to you for your help in installing him or her and will accept that as a favor task in itself. The only exception is the Rift, where both Maven and Laila require you to complete a [non-repeatable task](/wiki/Skyrim:Supply_and_Demand "Skyrim:Supply and Demand") as a prerequisite for the title.
- If the jarl is replaced and you then regain your thaneship, the bounty forgiveness will reset and you will be able to use it a second time under the new jarl. As the holds of the Reach, Falkreath, Hjaalmarch, the Pale and Winterhold can change hands twice throughout the game, this theoretically allows you to clear your bounty three times in these holds.
- It is strongly recommended that before completing the Dark Brotherhood contract to kill Helvard, you either become [Thane of Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Falkreath "Skyrim:Thane of Falkreath") first, or do Siddgeir/Dengeir's quests later to regain their grace.
- If Erikur or Bryling die, their housecarls ([Melaran](/wiki/Skyrim:Melaran "Skyrim:Melaran") and [Irnskar Ironhand](/wiki/Skyrim:Irnskar_Ironhand "Skyrim:Irnskar Ironhand"), respectively) will replace them as thanes.
- If you lose your thane status in your hold (due to the jarl that granted it being removed by the Civil War or Season Unending), then your housecarl will still call you thane but you will be unable to use your status to avoid being arrested by the guards until it is reinstated.

# Skyrim:Thane

## Overview

**Thane** is an honorary title presented by the [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of a [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") to individuals of high esteem. The bestowed title is one of both recognition and prestige. Thanes may be chosen due to their importance to the city or for their heroic deeds. It is possible to become a thane of every hold regardless of which side in the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") is chosen (although it is impossible to become Thane of [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") if no side is chosen). Each jarl has their own requirements for the title and may bestow the honor on multiple people.

## Benefits of Being a Thane

- Grants you a personal [housecarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl") [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") (if available).
- Grants you a symbolic weapon of the city.
- Guards will forgive any [bounty](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime#Bounties "Skyrim:Crime") of less than 2000 gold (once per hold). However, a crime can be pardoned twice if a hold is captured during the civil war and the new jarl appoints the player thane.

## Becoming a Thane

The general process for becoming a thane comes down to a relatively general formula with the exception of Whiterun, where it is initially achieved by completing the quest [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") and does not require the steps below to complete, unless you have joined the Stormcloaks and completed [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)").

1. You befriend the jarl through a quest or favors.
2. The jarl asks you to demonstrate your value to the hold by [assisting the people](/wiki/Skyrim:Making_Friends_and_Influencing_People "Skyrim:Making Friends and Influencing People") in the hold, five people in holds with major cities and three people in the other holds.
3. The jarl asks you to purchase a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") in the city if the hold is one of the five with major cities: Whiterun (Whiterun), The Rift (Riften), Eastmarch (Windhelm), Haafingar (Solitude), and The Reach (Markarth).
4. The jarl grants the title of thane and all that comes with it.

If [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") is installed, then the three minor holds of Falkreath (Falkreath), Hjaalmarch (Morthal), and The Pale (Dawnstar) will also appoint a housecarl and grant the right to purchase a plot of land on which you may [build your own residence](/wiki/Skyrim:Construction "Skyrim:Construction"). Your housecarl can be taken as your follower or will otherwise remain in the jarl's residence awaiting instructions. The same happens if you are granted the thaneship of Whiterun during the [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") quest. Thus, only Winterhold lacks the opportunity for the player to acquire a residence in the hold; likewise, there is no housecarl available for the player in Winterhold.

Progress made in assisting the people is dependent on disposition of citizens of the hold. Each citizen whose [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") is raised to friend counts towards the objective. If you raise someone's disposition before the objective to assist the people is given, that will still be taken into account. Note that if you befriend the same citizen twice, it only counts once for the thane quest. Also, if a friend dies, you do not lose progress (usually in those cases, you will have received an [Inheritance](/wiki/Skyrim:Inheritance "Skyrim:Inheritance").) In most cases, there is one quest for each citizen which will befriend him/her. Some citizens may have more than one quest which will befriend them. Many citizens have no specific quest available at all. A friend must be an ordinary citizen of the hold, not just living in it; members of [Khajiit caravans](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_Traders "Skyrim:Khajiit Traders") and [Orc strongholds](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") do not count towards the total. Befriending the Jarl also doesn't count as that is a prerequisite to being given the objective.

The thane quests and their general pieces are related below:

[^a](#note_Unending)If [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") has been used to change the jarls of holds, the new jarls will allow you to become thane without completing any other prerequisite quests, with the exception of the Jarl of the Rift.

[^b](#note_Weapon)All honorary weapons listed are randomly assigned enchanted melee weapons. More information can be found on [this page](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Enchanted_Weapons "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

[^c](#note_Whiterun)Dragon Rising grants thane status by itself. There are no further requirements to become Thane of Whiterun if Balgruuf is still Jarl of Whiterun, and there is no other way to become Thane of Whiterun while he is Jarl.

[^d](#note_Elisif)Elisif the Fair remains Jarl of Haafingar even if it is conquered by the Stormcloaks.

[^e](#note_Windhelm)It is impossible to become Thane of Eastmarch without taking one or the other side in the Civil War: you must either join the Stormcloaks to win Ulfric's favor and commit permanently to their side by conquering Whiterun for them (which is beyond the point-of-no-return that allows defecting to the Imperials), or join the Legion, win the civil war outright for the Empire (since the city cannot change hands during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending")), remove Ulfric from power in Windhelm and curry favor with his pro-Imperial replacement.

[†](#note_Blade_of_the_Rift)The "Blade of the Rift" is never actually given as a reward: instead, you will receive a generic un-renamed enchanted weapon.

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.

## NPC Thanes

NPCs that are thanes are typically identified through dialogue. There is no specific faction marking for thanes.

Thane Erikur of Haafingar

| Name | Hold | House | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Bryling](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling "Skyrim:Bryling") | [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | [Bryling's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling%27s_House "Skyrim:Bryling's House") | Owns [Rockwallow Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Rockwallow_Mine "Skyrim:Rockwallow Mine"). |
| [Dengeir of Stuhn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dengeir_of_Stuhn "Skyrim:Dengeir of Stuhn") | [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | [Dengeir's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Dengeir%27s_House "Skyrim:Dengeir's House") | Former Jarl of Falkreath, deposed by his nephew [Siddgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Siddgeir "Skyrim:Siddgeir"). Siding with the Stormcloaks will allow him to regain the title of Jarl. |
| [Erikur](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur "Skyrim:Erikur") | [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | [Erikur's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur%27s_House "Skyrim:Erikur's House") | Sister is [Gisli](/wiki/Skyrim:Gisli "Skyrim:Gisli"). |

[Mjoll the Lioness](/wiki/Skyrim:Mjoll_the_Lioness "Skyrim:Mjoll the Lioness") is declared by [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift")'s jarl, [Laila Law-Giver](/wiki/Skyrim:Laila_Law-Giver "Skyrim:Laila Law-Giver"), to be a champion of the people. Her virtue and heroic nature are extolled by Laila, but this only represents one facet of being a thane.

## Notes

- If the jarl that named you thane is replaced through the events of the Civil War or via [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"), you will lose the title, though you can regain it by speaking to the new jarl. You do not need to complete favor tasks a second time, because the new jarl is always grateful to you for your help in installing him or her and will accept that as a favor task in itself. The only exception is the Rift, where both Maven and Laila require you to complete a [non-repeatable task](/wiki/Skyrim:Supply_and_Demand "Skyrim:Supply and Demand") as a prerequisite for the title.
- If the jarl is replaced and you then regain your thaneship, the bounty forgiveness will reset and you will be able to use it a second time under the new jarl. As the holds of the Reach, Falkreath, Hjaalmarch, the Pale and Winterhold can change hands twice throughout the game, this theoretically allows you to clear your bounty three times in these holds.
- It is strongly recommended that before completing the Dark Brotherhood contract to kill Helvard, you either become [Thane of Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Falkreath "Skyrim:Thane of Falkreath") first, or do Siddgeir/Dengeir's quests later to regain their grace.
- If Erikur or Bryling die, their housecarls ([Melaran](/wiki/Skyrim:Melaran "Skyrim:Melaran") and [Irnskar Ironhand](/wiki/Skyrim:Irnskar_Ironhand "Skyrim:Irnskar Ironhand"), respectively) will replace them as thanes.
- If you lose your thane status in your hold (due to the jarl that granted it being removed by the Civil War or Season Unending), then your housecarl will still call you thane but you will be unable to use your status to avoid being arrested by the guards until it is reinstated.

# Skyrim:That Was Always There

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Return a [ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola%27s_Gold_Ring "Skyrim:Viola's Gold Ring") to its rightful [owner](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano "Skyrim:Viola Giordano").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Revyn Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Revyn_Sadri "Skyrim:Revyn Sadri") |
| Location(s): | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") ([Sadri's Used Wares](/wiki/Skyrim:Sadri%27s_Used_Wares "Skyrim:Sadri's Used Wares"), [Viola Giordano's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano%27s_House "Skyrim:Viola Giordano's House")) |
| Reward: | Leveled gold (medium) |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Revyn Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Revyn_Sadri "Skyrim:Revyn Sadri"))  or  =-1 ([Revyn Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Revyn_Sadri "Skyrim:Revyn Sadri"))  =1 ([Viola Giordano](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano "Skyrim:Viola Giordano")) |
| ID: | Favor019 |

The dresser in Viola Giordano's House

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Revyn Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Revyn_Sadri "Skyrim:Revyn Sadri") to begin the quest and obtain [Viola's Gold Ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola%27s_Gold_Ring "Skyrim:Viola's Gold Ring").
2. Choose whether to:
   - Break into [Viola Giordano's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano%27s_House "Skyrim:Viola Giordano's House") and return the ring, *or*
   - Tell [Viola Giordano](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano "Skyrim:Viola Giordano") about the ring.

### The Accidental Fence

[Revyn Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Revyn_Sadri "Skyrim:Revyn Sadri") runs a pawnshop, [Sadri's Used Wares](/wiki/Skyrim:Sadri%27s_Used_Wares "Skyrim:Sadri's Used Wares"), in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm")'s Gray Quarter. Revyn tends to tell visitors to his store, somewhat overemphatically, that, "*All my goods are legitimate, which is more than I can say for some*". If you question him on it, he will change his story and confess that he bought a [ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola%27s_Gold_Ring "Skyrim:Viola's Gold Ring") before realizing that it matched the description of an item recently stolen from [Viola Giordano](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano "Skyrim:Viola Giordano").

Even if you offer to return the ring for Revyn, he is still worried. He insists that Viola can't be told, because she would surely report the crime to the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl"). Instead, he wants you to sneak into [Viola Giordano's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano%27s_House "Skyrim:Viola Giordano's House") and leave the ring.

Your quest log at this point suggests that you only have one option for how to proceed, namely to [return the ring](#Option_1:_Return_the_Ring). However, Revyn's dialogue hints at a second option: you can [tell Viola](#Option_2:_Tell_Viola) about the stolen ring.

### Option 1: Return the Ring

To return the ring, the first step is gaining entrance to Viola's house. Her house is a large manor located in the Valunstrad district, on the west side of town. The front door is locked with a difficult leveled lock (Expert or Master level). Alternatively, you can opt to pickpocket the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano%27s_House_Key "Skyrim:Viola Giordano's House Key") from Viola.

Once you enter the house, the dresser where you are expected to place the ring is located immediately to the right of the front door. Open the dresser, and select that you want to "Store" the ring in the dresser. This will trigger a quest update.

Return to Revyn to obtain your reward, a medium leveled amount of gold. In addition, Revyn's disposition towards you will increase. The most immediate implication is that you will be able to freely take all low-cost items in the store and sleep in his bed for free. You will also be able to buy training in Speech to level 50. He is the only Speech trainer that you can trade with (which you can do to get the gold back) without joining the [Volkihar vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard").

### Option 2: Tell Viola

The other option requires you to find Viola. She is frequently found walking the streets of Windhelm, or else at [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall") in the evenings. If you talk to her, you will have the option to tell Viola about the ring. She takes the ring but seems more interested in finding ways to punish Revyn than actually being happy to have the ring back. In particular, she promises to report this to the Jarl and get Revyn's taxes doubled or even tripled.

She will also reward you with a medium leveled amount of gold. Her disposition towards you will increase, one implication being that you can freely take all low-cost items in her house. This is also the only way to be able to marry her. On the other hand, Revyn's disposition will decrease. This will result in negative comments every time you enter his store, but he will still trade with you (and his other dialogue will be as friendly as otherwise).

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 400 |
| 10–19 | 600 |
| 20–29 | 800 |
| 30–39 | 1,000 |
| 40+ | 1,200 |

## Notes

- Because this is a favor quest which positively affects either Revyn or Viola's disposition, it will count towards the "Help the People" part of the [Thane of Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Eastmarch "Skyrim:Thane of Eastmarch") quest.
- After returning the ring in the drawer and getting the quest update, you can remove the ring and tell Revyn that you returned it. The quest will complete and you will still have Viola's ring, which is no longer flagged as a quest item.

## Quest Stages

| That Was Always There (Favor019) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Plant Viola's Gold Ring in Viola Giordano's House |
| 15 |  | *Objective 15:* Tell Revyn Viola's Gold Ring has been planted |
| 20 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 17, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage Favor019 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest Favor019`.

## Overview

Thaumaturgist's Hut

The **Thaumaturgist's Hut** is an [alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") shop in [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal").

The shop is located across from [Highmoon Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Highmoon_Hall "Skyrim:Highmoon Hall"), where its proprietor [Lami](/wiki/Skyrim:Lami "Skyrim:Lami") runs the shop during normal business hours (8am - 8pm). There are two floors, each with their own entrance. However, the doors are never locked, possibly because it has the only [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") available in Morthal. If you are on good terms with the owner, all the lower value [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") and [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") found here are free to take and [respawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") every few days. No one lives or sleeps here and there are no beds in the building.

### Exterior

There are two [swamp fungal pods](/wiki/Skyrim:Swamp_Fungal_Pod "Skyrim:Swamp Fungal Pod") near the building, one near the front door and the other around the back next to the stairs leading up to a balcony. The balcony winds around the building and at the front is the second entrance.

### Thaumaturgist's Hut

First floor

The main entrance is on the ground floor and enters into the shop. Opposite you is a fireplace, on the mantlepiece are several [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") sold by [Lami](/wiki/Skyrim:Lami "Skyrim:Lami"). To the right of this, coming out from the east wall is the counter. On the counter is a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and under the counter are three small [coin purses](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). Behind the counter against the south wall are a cupboard and set of shelves holding more potions and [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") sold by Lami and four bottles of wine, two bottles of alto wine and a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead").

Between the cupboard and shelves is a barrel of ingredients and a pile of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sacks. To the right of the door is a dresser holding more ingredients sold by Lami, a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"). Next to the dresser is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). To the left of the fireplace is a rack hanging from the ceiling holding four [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"). Under this is a barrel of food and to the left of the barrel is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"). On top of the lab are more ingredient and potions you can buy from Lami and a [weak frenzy poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Frenzy_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Frenzy Poison"). There are stairs against the north wall leading to the top floor. Under the stairs is a pile of firewood and several barrels, on top of these are even more ingredients sold by Lami.

Second floor

At the top of the stairs, against the east wall is a long wooden table and bench holding two bottles of alto wine, several loaves of bread, several wedges of cheese, two [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") that you can buy from Lami and two pieces of [salmon meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Meat "Skyrim:Salmon Meat") on a wooden plate. To the right, still against the same wall is a set of shelves holding an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"). Against the south wall is an unlocked chest with dressers on either side holding four common books, a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl") containing three bottles of [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma") that are sold by Lami, two bottles of alto wine and five loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). There is a door to the outside in the middle of the west wall and a square wooden table to the right. To the right of the table, above the stairs are two food barrels.

## Displayed Merchandise

The following items are sitting out in the store, for example on the store counters. They can be purchased from the merchant, or else can be stolen. Other items may also be present in the store, but those other items are not available for purchase. They [respawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") after ten days.

- Food: 3 Skooma
- Ingredients: 1 [Bone Meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), 2 Chicken's Egg, 2 [Creep Cluster](/wiki/Skyrim:Creep_Cluster "Skyrim:Creep Cluster"), 1 [Deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell"), 1 [Dragon's Tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue"), 2 [Ectoplasm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ectoplasm "Skyrim:Ectoplasm"), 2 [Fire Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts"), 1 [Frost Mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), 1 [Giant's Toe](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Toe "Skyrim:Giant's Toe"), 1 [Glow Dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust"), 1 [Grass Pod](/wiki/Skyrim:Grass_Pod "Skyrim:Grass Pod"), 3 [Hagraven Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Claw "Skyrim:Hagraven Claw"), 2 [Ice Wraith Teeth](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith_Teeth "Skyrim:Ice Wraith Teeth"), 2 [Lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), 1 [Purple Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"), 2 [Salt Pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), 1 [Thistle Branch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch"), 1 [Tundra Cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"), 1 [Vampire Dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Dust "Skyrim:Vampire Dust"), 1 [Void Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts"), 1 [White Cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap")
- Ingredients (req. [Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_(perk) "Skyrim:Merchant (perk)") perk): 1 [Torchbug Thorax](/wiki/Skyrim:Torchbug_Thorax "Skyrim:Torchbug Thorax")
- [Poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"): 1 [Weak Fear Poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Fear_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Fear Poison"), 2 Weak Frenzy Poison, 1 [Weak Paralysis Poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Paralysis_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Paralysis Poison")
- Potions: 1 [Potion of Brief Invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Brief_Invisibility "Skyrim:Potion of Brief Invisibility"), 4 [Potion of Cure Disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Potion of Cure Disease"), 1 [Potion of Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Destruction "Skyrim:Potion of Destruction"), 1 [Potion of Enhanced Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Enhanced_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Enhanced Stamina"), 1 [Potion of Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Lockpicking "Skyrim:Potion of Lockpicking"), 2 Potion of Minor Healing, 2 [Potion of Minor Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), 1 [Potion of Minor Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), 1 [Potion of Plentiful Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Healing"), 1 [Potion of Regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), 1 [Potion of Resist Cold](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Cold "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Cold"), 2 [Potion of Resist Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Fire"), 1 [Skirmisher's Potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Skirmisher%27s_Potion "Skyrim:Skirmisher's Potion")

## Notes

- Since Lami doesn't live here, the opening hours are approximate. She doesn't leave her [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorgen_and_Lami%27s_House "Skyrim:Jorgen and Lami's House") until around 8am and it may take her an hour to walk to the shop.
- A copy of the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Response to Bero's Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Response_to_Bero%27s_Speech "Skyrim:Response to Bero's Speech")* can be found on top of a shelf on the bottom floor, next to a troll skull.

The Aetherium Forge

**The Aetherium Forge** is an ancient Dwemer forge, guarded by several [Dwarven automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons"). Access is gained during the quest [Lost to the Ages](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_to_the_Ages "Skyrim:Lost to the Ages") via the [Ruins of Bthalft](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Bthalft "Skyrim:Ruins of Bthalft").

After defeating some lesser Dwarven automatons, you will encounter [The Forgemaster](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forgemaster "Skyrim:The Forgemaster"), a unique [Dwarven centurion](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Centurion "Skyrim:Dwarven Centurion") that has a Flame Cloak-like power and shoots flames or a fireball instead of steam. After defeating it, you can obtain extra materials in a nearby chest to use at the Aetherium Forge. There are three different items that you could create, but you can only use the forge once.

|  |
| --- |
| - The [Aetherial Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Aetherial_Crown "Skyrim:Aetherial Crown") is a [circlet](/wiki/Skyrim:Circlet "Skyrim:Circlet") that allows you to use two [standing stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Standing_Stone "Skyrim:Standing Stone") abilities simultaneously. - The [Aetherial Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Aetherial_Shield "Skyrim:Aetherial Shield") is a [heavy](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield") that makes enemies become ethereal (unable to attack or be attacked) for 15 seconds when shield bashed. - The [Aetherial Staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Aetherial_Staff "Skyrim:Aetherial Staff") is a [staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff "Skyrim:Staff") that summons a [Dwarven spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider") or [Dwarven sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sphere "Skyrim:Dwarven Sphere") for 60 seconds. |
