## Related Quests

- **[Lost to the Ages](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_to_the_Ages "Skyrim:Lost to the Ages")**: Search for the Dwemer's Aetherium Forge.

## The Aetherium Forge

You enter via a lift down from the Ruins of Bthalft; at the bottom, before activating a lever to the right of the gate to open it, turn to your right and jump over a low wall. Follow the wall around to the right to find a Dwemer [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") with an apprentice-level lock. Past the gate, in front of you is a stone pool of water with a piece of [Dwemer scrap metal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Scrap_Metal "Skyrim:Dwemer Scrap Metal") on the edge of the pool. As you follow the path down several flights of stairs, braziers will light your way. After you descend the third set of stairs, you will face the start of a rock bridge, while to the left, a path leads down to the water. Heading due south from the bottom of the ramp and staying against the wall at the bottom, underwater lies an unlootable skeleton with a [Dwarven sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sword "Skyrim:Dwarven Sword") and an empty random [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") nearby. Also, behind the waterfall to the west is an alcove above the water with an adept-locked chest.

Crossing the first span of the bridge, you will come to a stone wall with a large sculpture of a Dwemer face. Under the sculpture is a stone shelf holding a [Dwemer cog](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Cog "Skyrim:Dwemer Cog"), a [Dwemer gear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Gear "Skyrim:Dwemer Gear"), a piece of Dwemer scrap metal, a [large decorative Dwemer strut](/wiki/Skyrim:Large_Decorative_Dwemer_Strut "Skyrim:Large Decorative Dwemer Strut"), a [Dwemer gyro](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Gyro "Skyrim:Dwemer Gyro"), and two [rubies](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby "Skyrim:Ruby"). Behind the wall with the face sculpture, drop down to a ledge to find another apprentice-locked chest. Cross the second span of the bridge and pass under a stone arch. In front of you are two flights of stairs, separated by a large stone wall leading up. On the outside of the stairs are statues of [Dwarven spheres](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sphere "Skyrim:Dwarven Sphere"). Turning left and following the cliff edge, you will eventually come to a [juniper](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") tree; just to the right is an enchanted [Dwarven battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Dwarven Battleaxe"). Going back to the stairs and climbing the first flight leads to a higher level; between the two sets of stairs are four stone benches facing a statue very similar to the one that you had to place the shards into to gain access. To the right of the first flights of stairs is a raised area that can be accessed by climbing three or four steps up the second flights of stairs and jumping up. Among the rocks you will find an inert [Dwarven spider worker](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider_Worker "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider Worker") underneath another juniper tree.

Climbing the second flight of stairs will bring you to a courtyard area with a dead tree in the center. On the left against the south wall is a stone table and bench; on the table is a Dwemer cog, a piece of [solid Dwemer metal](/wiki/Skyrim:Solid_Dwemer_Metal "Skyrim:Solid Dwemer Metal"), a [large Dwemer strut](/wiki/Skyrim:Large_Dwemer_Strut "Skyrim:Large Dwemer Strut"), a piece of Dwemer scrap metal, a piece of [bent Dwemer scrap metal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bent_Dwemer_Scrap_Metal "Skyrim:Bent Dwemer Scrap Metal"), and a Dwemer gear. Farther along this wall, in a pile of rubble, you will find another adept-locked chest. Against the north wall opposite the first table and bench is a matching one; this one holds a [Dwarven bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Bow "Skyrim:Dwarven Bow") and a set of eleven arrows. To the left of this table is a stone arch that leads north to a stream being fed by a waterfall. There is a [glowing mushroom](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom") growing under the arch, and beyond it, there are one each of [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot") and [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), with a second fly amanita growing next to the water's edge at the start of a ramp leading down into the water. However, it might not be possible to interact with this growth. Following the shore east, you will find a [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") and another fly amanita growing, as well as two [silver ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein"). Just past the second vein is a stone arch with two more glowing mushrooms growing on it. In the water at the very bottom, before it drops over a waterfall, is a random, filled soul gem. There is an unlootable skeleton under the water against the west wall, with a random weapon and a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") next to it. There is also an expert-locked chest on the north shore of the stream. Going southwest from the arch will lead you to the second juniper tree seen earlier, providing a quick return to the courtyard.

The way forward is through a gate in the western wall. It has two [kinetic resonators](/wiki/Skyrim:Kinetic_Resonator "Skyrim:Kinetic Resonator") above it, one on either side; shooting both of these with a missile, either physical or magic, will open the gate. Passing through the gate will bring you to the top of a flight of stairs, with a stone bench on your right. At the bottom of the stairs is a set of doors to the south, with a [scuttle](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Scuttle "Skyrim:Dwarven Scuttle") on your left. In front of the scuttle is a [potion of ultimate healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Ultimate_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Ultimate Healing"), a random potion of healing, a random potion of magicka, a [Dwarven helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Helmet "Skyrim:Dwarven Helmet"), and an [elixir of resist fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Elixir_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Elixir of Resist Fire"). Through the doors, you get your first look at the forge.

In order to clear the damaging steam from the room, you will need to turn it off using [valves](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Valve "Skyrim:Traps") on raised platforms on either side of you. There are shallow alcoves above the two valves, from which a series of Dwarven spiders and spheres will attack you. The Aetherium forge is directly in front of you. On the bottom level against the east wall is a stone table with an unlocked chest built in; on the table are two random potions (one of which is a healing potion), a pair of [Dwarven gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Dwarven Gauntlets"), and an enchanted [Dwarven greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Greatsword "Skyrim:Dwarven Greatsword"). Against the west wall is a similar stone table with another unlocked chest. On this table are three [Dwarven metal ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Metal_Ingot "Skyrim:Dwarven Metal Ingot"), a large decorative Dwemer strut, a piece of Dwemer scrap metal, a Dwemer gyro, and a [centurion dynamo core](/wiki/Skyrim:Centurion_Dynamo_Core "Skyrim:Centurion Dynamo Core"). The chest contains all the items you will need to craft any one of the possible Aetherial items listed in the [Smithing](#Smithing) section of this page.

On either side of the forge are ramps leading down to the lava. With high enough health, [fire resistance](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Resist Fire"), or the [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") or [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") shouts, you can reach three additional areas featuring loot across the lava. To access the first two areas, turn outwards from the ramps and follow the walls along to the end, where you will reach two unlocked gates that open outwards and allow access to the two areas, each of which contains an unlocked chest and several pieces of Dwemer metalwork scattered on the ground. You can then follow the paths up to gates that allow you to drop back onto the bottom level near the two stone tables. The third accessible lava area hides an unlocked chest up a ramp behind the large rock pillar you can see in the southeast corner of the room; stay to the right-hand side of the pillar to go up the ramp.

Once you have spoken with [Katria](/wiki/Skyrim:Katria "Skyrim:Katria") after using the forge, the [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_to_the_Ages "Skyrim:Lost to the Ages") ends, and the stairs that dropped and trapped you in this room will rise back into place, allowing you to leave.

## Notes

- Multiple soul gems can be found underwater near the entrance and near the sealed gate.
- The spheres and spider will repeatedly turn the valves back on, letting steam escape from the central floor vent. If you step onto the steam, it causes two effects (listed under the Active Effects tab): "Lingering Steam Damage" and "Steam Damage", though the effects are identical. The description of the effects states: STEAM DAMAGE/RESTORATION +8 Steam Damage 2 secs, +2 Lingering Steam Damage 3 secs, +10 Steam Construct Healing 2 secs. These effects also stack each second you remain in the steam, and the constructs are healed by the steam effects.
- The lava deals 150 initial damage (referred to as "Massive Fire Damage" by the game), plus 17 damage per second over 4 seconds. This effect is applied (and stacks) every second you're touching the lava, which will burn quickly through most health bars, if not kill you outright. It also has unique visual and audio effects: the screen will become very bright, blurry, and colored almost exclusively red and yellow, and a loud burning and crackling sound will play. If you use the Become Ethereal shout to traverse the lava, the screen effect is still applied even though you will take no damage from the lava, which combined with the shout's bright visual effects results in most environmental shapes and details being heavily blurred and bathed in white. In addition to its massive damage-dealing potential, you can also drown in the lava if you submerse yourself in it.
- [Ahzidal's Boots of Waterwalking](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal%27s_Boots_of_Waterwalking "Skyrim:Ahzidal's Boots of Waterwalking"), potions of waterwalking, and the waterwalking ability of the [Vampire Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Lord "Skyrim:Vampire Lord") form will not help you safely traverse the lava, as you will still incur the large fire damage as soon as you step onto it. However, since you can cast spells, you may be able to out-heal the damage and survive. The Mist Form of the Vampire Lord will allow you to cross the lava without damage.

## Bugs

- Stepping out onto the lava sometimes allows you to see the applied effect of the blurriness in your Active Effects tab, listed as "IMAGE LAVASPACE +1 24000" and the duration is 24000 hours. Stepping onto dry land removes the effect from the tab. **?**
- Rarely, the blurred out reds and yellows may remain on your screen after you exit the lava. Entering the lava again (to reapply the effect) and exiting again can fix it. **?**

# Skyrim:The Affairs of Hagravens

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **After discovering an [imprisoned hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Melka "Skyrim:Melka"), you must help her reclaim her lost tower.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Melka](/wiki/Skyrim:Melka "Skyrim:Melka") |
| Location(s): | [Blind Cliff Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Blind_Cliff_Cave "Skyrim:Blind Cliff Cave") |
| Reward: | [Eye of Melka](/wiki/Skyrim:Eye_of_Melka "Skyrim:Eye of Melka") |
| ID: | dunBlindCliffQST |
| Suggested Level: | 14 |

Melka needs your help

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Find [Melka](/wiki/Skyrim:Melka "Skyrim:Melka") imprisoned in [Blind Cliff Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Blind_Cliff_Cave "Skyrim:Blind Cliff Cave").
2. Protect her from [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") as you travel through the tower.
3. Kill [Petra](/wiki/Skyrim:Petra "Skyrim:Petra").

### A Hagraven in Need

Upon entering [Blind Cliff Bastion](/wiki/Skyrim:Blind_Cliff_Bastion "Skyrim:Blind Cliff Bastion") you will see the hagraven [Melka](/wiki/Skyrim:Melka "Skyrim:Melka") in a cage. As you approach her, she will ask you to free her and help her reclaim her tower from another hagraven, [Petra](/wiki/Skyrim:Petra "Skyrim:Petra"). To release Melka, pull the chain near the cage. After leaving the cage she will then lead you through her tower. The first room displays a central stone slab adorned with three handles; Melka will tell you that the middle one is the correct one to use. Pull the handle and go through the gate it opens. Follow the short path into a room inhabited by a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). There will then be a gate with a tunnel full of [swinging blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Blades "Skyrim:Swinging Blades"). Melka will mention a lever that will stop the blades: she will then pull a handle on the floor that lowers a section of a wall, revealing another lever to do just that.

### Reclaiming the Tower

Move through the tunnel and go up the stairs. After the stairs you will pass a section of wall that moves away when the nearby handle is pulled. Through the newly cleared section of wall are some ingots and a chest. The next room has an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), and is referred to by Melka as her "parlor". Follow the path past the quicksilver ore. The next room contains Petra and two Forsworn. Killing them and Petra will result in Melka rewarding you with the unique staff, [Eye of Melka](/wiki/Skyrim:Eye_of_Melka "Skyrim:Eye of Melka"). If Melka died anywhere along the way you can simply loot the staff from her corpse.

## Notes

- You can also just kill Melka for the staff, but you will still have the objective to kill Petra and you will have lost your guide.
- If you run ahead of Melka (or she gets stuck somewhere and halts long enough), it is possible to kill Petra, complete the quest, leave the dungeon, and not obtain the staff by talking to Melka and demanding a reward. Though rare, this can result in a bug where Melka randomly shows up wherever you are to talk to you, as the quest objective of her being scripted by her AI package to move to you, force-greet and engage in dialogue (dunBlindCliffForceGreetAndRewardPlayer) has not been completed.

## Bugs

- If you kill Petra before freeing Melka, the quest does not complete and remains in your list of quests.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, addresses this issue. This fix later got reworked in Version 4.2.4 due to a previously faulty stage check.
- Completing this quest counts towards the [Sideways](/wiki/Skyrim:Sideways "Skyrim:Sideways") [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements"), even though it is not a [Side Quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Side_Quests "Skyrim:Side Quests"), i.e., it does not have a separate entry in your quest log

  **Mod Notes**: Quest stage 100 of the quest calls AchievementsQuest.IncSideQuests(), even though the quest Type is "Miscellaneous" instead of "Side Quests"

  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- The quest might not properly complete its objectives due to the quest checking a wrong prerequisite stage upon the death of either Petra or Melka.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.4, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| The Affairs of Hagravens (dunBlindCliffQST) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 15 |  | *Objective 15:* Kill the Hagraven Petra |
| 20 |  | *Objective 15:* Kill the Hagraven Petra |
| 100 | ☑ |  |
| 200 |  | The Hagraven Melka is dead. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 11, 30, 40, 45, 50, 60, 256.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage dunBlindCliffQST stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest dunBlindCliffQST`.

# Skyrim:The Apprentice Stone

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Doomstone.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Doomstone.png) | Standing Stone: The Apprentice Stone ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Apprentice+Stone)) | | |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DoomstoneTundraMarsh01 | |
| Region | |
| [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | |
| Location | |
| On an island in the marsh, just north of [Fort Snowhawk](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Snowhawk "Skyrim:Fort Snowhawk"), west-northwest of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). | |

The Apprentice Stone

**The Apprentice Stone** is one of the thirteen [Standing Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Standing_Stones "Skyrim:Standing Stones") scattered across Skyrim.

.jpg)

The Apprentice Stone when it's activated

*Those under the sign of The Apprentice recover Magicka faster, but are more susceptible to Magicka damage.* Activating the Apprentice Stone increases [magicka regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Regenerate_Magicka "Skyrim:Regenerate Magicka") by 100% and increases [weakness to magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Weakness_to_Magic "Skyrim:Weakness to Magic") by 100%.

The stone is set in the typical arrangement of standing stones on the northeast end of a small marsh archipelago. Little else is found here other than plants typical to the marshes of [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch"). A [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") plant is growing just to the west of the stone structure, at the base of a large tree. Another is at the base of the Apprentice stone itself. [Swamp fungal pods](/wiki/Skyrim:Swamp_Fungal_Pod "Skyrim:Swamp Fungal Pod") are also growing in the stone's circle and more can be found at the base of a tree just to the right of the circle of stones. A [nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") is found on the shoreline to the southeast of the circle.

## Notes

- Although the loading screen tip states the Apprentice Stone doubles both magicka regeneration and magicka, only magicka regeneration is doubled.
- East-southeast of the Stone, a Nordic burial pit has partially sunk into the swamp, and has been taken over by several [mudcrabs](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab "Skyrim:Mudcrab"). A novice treasure chest, several burial urns, and a copy of the [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Locked Room](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Locked_Room "Skyrim:The Locked Room")* can be found here.

# Skyrim:The Arcanaeum

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Library: The Arcanaeum ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Arcanaeum)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| WinterholdCollegeArcanaeum | |
| Location | |
| [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") | |

Inside The Arcanaeum

**The Arcanaeum** is the library located within the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"), zealously maintained by [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub").

Collated over hundreds of years, the College's library contains a wealth of information, placed at the fingertips of those who require it - albeit under the ever-watchful eye of Urag gro-Shub. It is located on the first floor of the main college building, between the [Hall of the Elements](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Elements "Skyrim:Hall of the Elements") and the [Arch-Mage's Quarters](/wiki/Skyrim:Arch-Mage%27s_Quarters "Skyrim:Arch-Mage's Quarters"). If you choose to join the College, you may find yourself adding significantly to the collection of books available, and may even be gifted with some as rewards.

### Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") |

## Related Quests

- **[A Matter of Pride](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Matter_of_Pride "Skyrim:A Matter of Pride")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldbrand "Skyrim:Goldbrand"): Obtain the legendary katana [Goldbrand](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldbrand_(item) "Skyrim:Goldbrand (item)").
- **[Creature of Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Creature_of_Legend "Skyrim:Creature of Legend")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horses "Skyrim:Wild Horses"): Track down and tame the last living [Unicorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Unicorn "Skyrim:Unicorn").
- **[Discerning the Transmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane")**: Uncover the secrets of the mysterious Dwemer lockbox.
- **[Elder Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Knowledge "Skyrim:Elder Knowledge")**: Recover an [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Scroll "Skyrim:Elder Scroll") to learn an [Ancient Secret](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrend "Skyrim:Dragonrend").
- **[Fetch me that Book!](/wiki/Skyrim:Fetch_me_that_Book! "Skyrim:Fetch me that Book!")**: Fetch a book for [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Forgotten Vale Books Quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale_Books_Quest "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale Books Quest")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Bring the Ancient Falmer Tome to [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub").
- **[Hitting the Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Hitting_the_Books "Skyrim:Hitting the Books")**: Find the books needed to identify the artifact found in [Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal "Skyrim:Saarthal").
- **[Scroll Scouting](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_Scouting "Skyrim:Scroll Scouting")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Obtain information on the Dragon Elder Scroll.
- **[Shalidor's Insights](/wiki/Skyrim:Shalidor%27s_Insights "Skyrim:Shalidor's Insights")**: Discover the writings of Shalidor and benefit from his wisdom. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Swift as an Arrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Swift_as_an_Arrow "Skyrim:Swift as an Arrow")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Archer_Pack "Skyrim:Arcane Archer Pack"): Learn how to craft and use [Telekinesis Arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis_Arrow "Skyrim:Telekinesis Arrow").

## The Arcanaeum

There are four entrances to the Arcanaeum: one from the antechamber in the **Hall of Elements**, one from the **Arch-mage's Quarters**, and two from the roof of the College. It is a large circular room with large locked and unlocked non-respawning bookcases lining most of the walls. By the entrances are five unlocked bookcases; however, everything in the Arcanaeum is owned, and taking items is considered stealing. There is a [mammoth tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Tusk "Skyrim:Mammoth Tusk") on top of one of the unlocked bookcases, with a round wooden table and chairs nearby. There are many tables and chairs arranged in small groups around the room, with stacks of common and less common books on every available surface. There are many bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") as well as [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet") on the tables, but strictly no [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food").

The counter is at the far end, where [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") can always be found, overseeing anyone within the Arcanaeum. He is very protective of the books found in the Arcanaeum, and will repeat warnings to take care of any books found here every time you talk to him. With the [Arcane Archer Pack](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Archer_Pack "Skyrim:Arcane Archer Pack") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, [*Spell Tome: Telekinesis Arrows*](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Telekinesis_Arrows "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Telekinesis Arrows") and [*Telekinesis Arrows Research Notes*](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis_Arrows_Research_Notes "Skyrim:Telekinesis Arrows Research Notes") can be found atop the counter next to Urag. Under the counter are two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), and behind it against the rear wall is a locked display case containing four rare books; however, the lock cannot be picked, and no key exists in-game to unlock either the various locked bookcases or the display case.

Farther around to the left is the non-respawning investigator's chest, which is master-locked. The [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Investigator%27s_Key "Skyrim:Investigator's Key") to open it is found on a table in [the Midden](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Midden "Skyrim:The Midden") along with a copy of the [*Midden Incident Report*](/wiki/Skyrim:Midden_Incident_Report "Skyrim:Midden Incident Report") regarding the disappearance and subsequent deaths of four previous students. Inside the chest are four rings that are needed for the gauntlet in **the Midden**, as part of the unmarked quest [Forgotten Names](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Names "Skyrim:Forgotten Names").

There are partition walls segregating the outer ring of the room from the central reading area. You will often find one or more of the college trainers in the Arcanaeum reading. Urag gro-Shub, like other [Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc"), is able to make you [Blood-Kin](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood-Kin "Skyrim:Blood-Kin") to the Orcs, once you have completed a couple quests for him.

## Notes

- Urag will sell you a variety of books that weren't fit to be added to the Arcanaeum's collection.
- When completing the quest [Alduin's Bane](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Alduin's Bane"), you can sell the [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Scroll "Skyrim:Elder Scroll") to Urag for 2000 gold. However, if you have the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") add-on installed, you will need the Elder Scroll for this questline. You can buy it back from him if needed, but you will not be able to sell it again.
- Like all other bookcases in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), books can be read from the unlocked bookcases with no repercussions, but as they are marked as owned, taking them is considered stealing.
- The books inside the display case are (from left to right): [*Arcana Restored*](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcana_Restored "Skyrim:Arcana Restored"), [*Imperial Report on Saarthal*](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Report_on_Saarthal "Skyrim:Imperial Report on Saarthal"), [*Herbane's Bestiary: Automatons*](/wiki/Skyrim:Herbane%27s_Bestiary:_Automatons "Skyrim:Herbane's Bestiary: Automatons"), and [*The Falmer: A Study*](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Falmer:_A_Study "Skyrim:The Falmer: A Study").
- The name "Arcanaeum" is possibly an allusion to the Belgian [Mundaneum](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mundaneum "wikipedia:Mundaneum").

## Bugs

- Urag may always greet you as though you're in the Arcaneum, even if he isn't there himself.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.
- After A Matter of Pride is finished, some [Boethiah Cultists](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah_Cultist "Skyrim:Boethiah Cultist") may respawn in the Arcanaeum when the area resets. From there, they can follow you wherever you go, and they can appear anywhere, including inside player homes.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.629, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:The Arms of Chaos

## Overview

You must face the forces of Oblivion to reforge these items

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Go to [Skytemple Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Skytemple_Ruins "Skyrim:Skytemple Ruins") and take *[Hyenril's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Hyenril%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Hyenril's Journal")*, the [Arm of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Arm_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Arm of the Moon"), the [Arm of the Sun](/wiki/Skyrim:Arm_of_the_Sun "Skyrim:Arm of the Sun"), and the [Warlock's Mark](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock%27s_Mark "Skyrim:Warlock's Mark").
2. Go to the [East Empire Company offices](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_(place) "Skyrim:East Empire Company (place)") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") and read *[Loss of the Sea Stallion](/wiki/Skyrim:Loss_of_the_Sea_Stallion "Skyrim:Loss of the Sea Stallion")*.
3. Locate the [Sovereign Band](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovereign_Band "Skyrim:Sovereign Band") within a coffin at the bottom of [Pilgrim's Trench](/wiki/Skyrim:Pilgrim%27s_Trench "Skyrim:Pilgrim's Trench").
4. Find the summoning circle east of Skytemple Ruins to summon and defeat three [Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora "Skyrim:Dremora").
5. Craft the three items using a [Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") and [Staff Enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_Enchanter "Skyrim:Staff Enchanter").

## Detailed Walkthrough

A young mage has perished, her work uncompleted

### A Dead Mage

This quest will automatically begin upon reading *[Hyenril's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Hyenril%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Hyenril's Journal")* at the [Skytemple Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Skytemple_Ruins "Skyrim:Skytemple Ruins") north of the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"). The ruins are usually swarming with undead [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"), although these shouldn't pose much of a threat. You must locate the corpse of [Hyenril](/wiki/Skyrim:Hyenril "Skyrim:Hyenril"), a dead mage found within one of the ruins. On the table in front of her, you will find *[Hyenril's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Hyenril%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Hyenril's Journal")* along with two broken staves: the [Arm of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Arm_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Arm of the Moon") and the [Arm of the Sun](/wiki/Skyrim:Arm_of_the_Sun "Skyrim:Arm of the Sun"). Hidden beneath the table is the [Warlock's Mark](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock%27s_Mark "Skyrim:Warlock's Mark"), a mundane necklace.

Reading the journal will identify these items as the property of Hyenril's former master, Ellane, who spent long years attempting to restore the two staves, which were originally created in imitation of the legendary [Staff of Chaos](/wiki/Lore:Staff_of_Chaos "Lore:Staff of Chaos") but were destroyed by their original creator. It will also reveal that Sigil Stones will be needed to restore the three items and unlock their true power. Take all three items to progress the quest; the Warlock's Mark is small and really can be difficult to see, so you may need to rely on your HUD pointer.

### Sunken Treasure

Locate the master's watery grave

In order to obtain the required Sigil Stones, you will need to track down Ellane's ring of summoning. Unfortunately, Ellane was still wearing this ring when Hyenril shipped her body back home for burial aboard a vessel called the *Sea Stallion*. Your first stop is the [East Empire Company offices](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_(place) "Skyrim:East Empire Company (place)") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), where you will find a letter entitled *[Loss of the Sea Stallion](/wiki/Skyrim:Loss_of_the_Sea_Stallion "Skyrim:Loss of the Sea Stallion")* on a table next to a potion of waterbreathing. The ship apparently sank to the bottom of [Pilgrim's Trench](/wiki/Skyrim:Pilgrim%27s_Trench "Skyrim:Pilgrim's Trench") off the coast of Skyrim before it delivered its cargo.

Head to Pilgrim's Trench and prepare for a deep dive to find Ellane's coffin, which can be found atop a rocky outcropping on the sea floor. Inside you will find a copy of *[Final Lesson](/wiki/Skyrim:Final_Lesson "Skyrim:Final Lesson")*, *[Master Ellane's Last Words](/wiki/Skyrim:Master_Ellane%27s_Last_Words "Skyrim:Master Ellane's Last Words")*, and the [Sovereign Band](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovereign_Band "Skyrim:Sovereign Band"), an enchanted ring which fortifies your [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka").

### The Guardians of the Sigil Stones

The Daedric altar

With the ring in hand, you will be directed to a stone Daedric summoning circle on the same island as Skytemple Ruins. You must descend from the peak where the ruins are located and go to the eastern shore of the island to find it. Approach the center of the altar and you will be given the option to summon Daedra. Once you activate it, three [Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora "Skyrim:Dremora") will appear in quick succession, with a new one being summoned each time you defeat the last:

- [Dremora Sehtkynaz](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_Sehtkynaz "Skyrim:Dremora Sehtkynaz"), an ice mage who can summon a [Frost Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Atronach "Skyrim:Frost Atronach"), guardian of the [Blue Sigil Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Sigil_Stone "Skyrim:Blue Sigil Stone");
- [Dremora Lyrkynaz](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_Lyrkynaz "Skyrim:Dremora Lyrkynaz"), a shock mage who can summon a [Storm Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Atronach "Skyrim:Storm Atronach"), guardian of the [Green Sigil Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Sigil_Stone "Skyrim:Green Sigil Stone"); and
- [Dremora Sovereign](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_Sovereign "Skyrim:Dremora Sovereign"), a fire-wielding warrior who can summon a [Flame Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Atronach "Skyrim:Flame Atronach"), guardian of the [Orange Sigil Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Sigil_Stone "Skyrim:Orange Sigil Stone").

Survive the encounter, then loot the bodies of the Dremora to obtain the three Sigil Stones needed to restore your items' enchantments. They also each have [Daedra Hearts](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart") on them. The Warlock's Mark can be reforged at any [forge or anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"). The Arm of the Moon and Arm of the Sun require access to a [Staff Enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_Enchanter "Skyrim:Staff Enchanter"); in the base game, the only one in existence is located behind a locked door in [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)") and can only be accessed after you complete the quest [Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward"). You can avoid this prerequisite if you have access to a Staff Enchanter elsewhere, such as the one added by the [Myrwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch "Skyrim:Myrwatch") or [Bloodchill Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodchill_Manor "Skyrim:Bloodchill Manor") Creations.

Once you have crafted the enchanted versions of all three items, the quest will complete and you will have in your possession several powerful artifacts.

## Notes

- It is possible to skip the visit to Windhelm entirely if you have already looted the coffin in Pilgrim's Trench. You will immediately be directed to summon the Dremora.
- The Dremora Sovereign wields a [Daedric Sword of the Inferno](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Sword_of_the_Inferno "Skyrim:Daedric Sword of the Inferno") at all levels, a powerful piece of equipment if you can best all three Dremora at a low level.

## Bugs

- Crafting the staffs using the Myrwatch Staff Enchanter is most beneficial, as it is bugged and grants 20 times more [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") experience than it is supposed to. This is due to the Staff Enchanter in Tel Mithryn having a hidden perk (`DLC2StaffEnchantingMult`) that reduces the experience gained by 95%; the Staff Enchanter in Myrwatch has a different Editor ID and thus is unaffected by the perk. As a result, crafting the Arms of Chaos at Myrwatch will result in you possibly jumping more than 20 Enchanting levels.
  - This bug was fixed by an [Anniversary Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Anniversary_Edition "Skyrim:Anniversary Edition") update to this Creation.
- When you are crafting the Arm of the Moon the message that appears says the Arm of the Sun has been completed, and vice versa. **?**
- The Warlock's Mark can also be glitched in the middle of the table and there seems to be no way of dislodging it.
  - You can reach The Warlock's Mark by standing on the back of the table in the alcove and looking at the place it's marker is. This does not always work.
  - You can disable the table in the console. Do a quick save. Within the console click on the table. It should show something like `fexxx83d`. Type `disable`. Exit the console and pick up the necklace. Re-enter the console and type `enable` (with the same `fexxx83d` still showing) and the table will reappear. You will have the necklace and the quest will update.
  - Cast the spell 'Raise Zombie' on Hyenril's corpse and lead them out of the ruins until they turn to ash. Fast Travel to a major hold like Whiterun and wait 30 days in game. Return to the ruins and the amulet should be on the ground under the table.
- The [Arm of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Arm_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Arm of the Moon"), the [Arm of the Sun](/wiki/Skyrim:Arm_of_the_Sun "Skyrim:Arm of the Sun"), and the [Warlock's Mark](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock%27s_Mark "Skyrim:Warlock's Mark") can still have weight while considered quest items.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccPEWSSE002_Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccPEWSSE002_Quest`.

# Skyrim:The Atronach Stone

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Doomstone.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Doomstone.png) | Standing Stone: The Atronach Stone ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Atronach+Stone)) | | |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DoomstoneVolcanicTundra | |
| Region | |
| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | |
| Location | |
| South of [Bonestrewn Crest](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonestrewn_Crest "Skyrim:Bonestrewn Crest") East-Northeast of [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing") | |

The Atronach Stone

**The Atronach Stone** is one of the thirteen [Standing Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Standing_Stones "Skyrim:Standing Stones") scattered across Skyrim.

.jpg)

The Atronach Stone when it's activated

*"Those under the sign of The Atronach absorb a portion of incoming spell damage and have a larger pool of Magicka, but recover it more slowly."*

The stone adds a passive power that increases [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") by 50 points and adds 50% [Spell Absorption](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Absorption "Skyrim:Spell Absorption"), but decreases [magicka regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Regenerate_Magicka "Skyrim:Regenerate Magicka") by 50%.

The Atronach a useful Stone for mages thanks to its sizable [Fortify Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Magicka "Skyrim:Fortify Magicka") effect, while the Spell Absorption can be utilized by any character wishing to reduce damage and effects from incoming magic. The reduced magicka regeneration can be overcome with [perks](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration#Skill_Perks "Skyrim:Restoration"), [potions and enchantments](/wiki/Skyrim:Regenerate_Magicka "Skyrim:Regenerate Magicka"), or by simply fortifying magicka even further (see Notes).

## The Atronach Stone

The stone is located almost due south of [Bonestrewn Crest](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonestrewn_Crest "Skyrim:Bonestrewn Crest"), east-northeast of [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing") in the southern-most part of the hot springs. It is found at the top of a mound with several other stones jutting out at an angle around it, surrounded by roiling volcanic pools. At its base is a steaming, shallow pool where a couple of [jazbay grape](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes") plants are growing. Other nearby vegetation that can be harvested include some [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") plants and [creep clusters](/wiki/Skyrim:Creep_Cluster "Skyrim:Creep Cluster").

## Notes

- With no other modifiers, this Stone reduces your base magicka regen from 3% per second to 1.5% per second out of combat.
- Because magicka regenerates at a percent rate of your total magicka, increasing total magicka actually increases the amount of magicka recovered per second. A character with 200 magicka and 50% reduced regeneration recovers the same amount of magicka per second as a character with 100 magicka and base magicka regen.
- [High Elves](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") have a natural affinity for The Atronach Stone, combining their already high magicka pool with the [Highborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Highborn "Skyrim:Highborn") power to nullify the reduced magicka regen.
- The Atronach Stone is one of only a few methods of obtaining the rare Spell Absorption effect.
  - Combining it with the [Breton's](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [Dragonskin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonskin "Skyrim:Dragonskin") power grants 100% Spell Absorption, making the player completely immune to magic for 60 seconds. This can be used to trivialize some of the most powerful enemies in the game, such as [Dragon Priests](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest"), who deal damage exclusively through use of magic.
- If you choose to forge the [Aetherial Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Aetherial_Crown "Skyrim:Aetherial Crown") during [Lost to the Ages](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_to_the_Ages "Skyrim:Lost to the Ages"), The Atronach Stone can be combined with [The Apprentice Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Apprentice_Stone "Skyrim:The Apprentice Stone") to achieve 50% Spell Absorption, +50 magicka, and 50% magicka regeneration, with the downside of 100% [weakness to magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Weakness_to_Magic "Skyrim:Weakness to Magic").
- The Spell Absorb effect also has a chance of absorbing incoming diseases. This is because diseases are a magical effect.
- You can take advantage of otherwise mundane magic effects to recharge your magicka. Jumping up and down on a forge, for instance, will provide a small but noticeable boost to magicka regeneration.

## Bugs

- The Atronach Stone has a 50% chance of causing all [Summoning](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration_Spells "Skyrim:Conjuration Spells") spells and powers to fail. See [Spell Absorption](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Absorption#Bugs "Skyrim:Spell Absorption") for details.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.

The Bannered Mare

**The Bannered Mare** is an [inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Skyrim:Inns") located in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun")'s market area in the Plains District.

The Bannered Mare interior

The inn has two stories split into multiple rooms. On the first floor there is the common room, a small bedroom, and the kitchen. The second floor contains three bedrooms split across two areas. Sitting in any seat in the inn will cause [Hulda](/wiki/Skyrim:Hulda "Skyrim:Hulda") to call [Saadia](/wiki/Skyrim:Saadia "Skyrim:Saadia") to serve you, and she will then seek you out and offer to sell [food and drinks](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food").

## Residents

| Residents | When |
| --- | --- |
| [Hulda](/wiki/Skyrim:Hulda "Skyrim:Hulda") | Always |
| [Saadia](/wiki/Skyrim:Saadia "Skyrim:Saadia") | Until completion of [In My Time of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need") if you side with the [Alik'r](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27r_Warrior "Skyrim:Alik'r Warrior"), or always if you side with her |
| [Mikael](/wiki/Skyrim:Mikael "Skyrim:Mikael") | Always |
| [Sinmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinmir "Skyrim:Sinmir") | Until [Whiterun is captured by the Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)") |
| [Uthgerd the Unbroken](/wiki/Skyrim:Uthgerd_the_Unbroken "Skyrim:Uthgerd the Unbroken") | If she is not following you or [recruited into the blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades"), or made steward of any of the houses you build[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") |

| [Rexus](/wiki/Skyrim:Rexus "Skyrim:Rexus") | After [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!") is started |

## Related Quests

- **[Argonian Ale Extraction](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Ale_Extraction "Skyrim:Argonian Ale Extraction")**: [Brenuin](/wiki/Skyrim:Brenuin "Skyrim:Brenuin") longs for the taste of [Argonian Ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Ale "Skyrim:Argonian Ale"). Can you steal some for him?
- **[Breaching Security](/wiki/Skyrim:Breaching_Security "Skyrim:Breaching Security")**: Kill and frame the [son](/wiki/Skyrim:Gaius_Maro "Skyrim:Gaius Maro") of a high-ranking [Imperial guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro").
- **[Dampened Spirits](/wiki/Skyrim:Dampened_Spirits "Skyrim:Dampened Spirits")**: Put [Maven Black-Briar's](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar") competition out of business.
- **[A Few Words with You](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Few_Words_with_You "Skyrim:A Few Words with You")**: Do a favor by talking to someone about a problem. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Fight! Fight!](/wiki/Skyrim:Fight!_Fight! "Skyrim:Fight! Fight!")**: Prove your strength by wagering on a fist fight with another. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!")**: One of the biggest [contracts](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)") in [Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") history is yours to fulfill.
- **[In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need")**: Find a [Redguard woman](/wiki/Skyrim:Saadia "Skyrim:Saadia") who is on the run from [her past](/wiki/Lore:Taneth "Lore:Taneth").
- **[Pets of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Pets_of_Skyrim_(quest) "Skyrim:Pets of Skyrim (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Pets_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Pets of Skyrim"): Find trained pets around Skyrim.
- **[When the Cat's Away](/wiki/Skyrim:When_the_Cat%27s_Away "Skyrim:When the Cat's Away")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Silver "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Silver"): Find a stash of [silver](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver "Skyrim:Silver") armor.
- **[The Whispering Door](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Whispering_Door "Skyrim:The Whispering Door")**: Investigate [Nelkir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nelkir "Skyrim:Nelkir")'s story of a Whispering Lady behind a locked door.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

It is by the stairs leading up to the Gildergreen tree. There are stone steps leading up to the main entrance, where there is a  "Loot") Loot [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") carved into the wall to the right of the entrance door. There is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") next to the rear entrance that takes you directly into the kitchen. Once you have completed the special [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") quest: [Imitation Amnesty](/wiki/Skyrim:Imitation_Amnesty "Skyrim:Imitation Amnesty"), there is a Thieves' Cache barrel behind the inn, which is marked with the  "Cache") Cache shadowmark carved into the side of it.

### The Bannered Mare

The common room

The common room centers around a fire pit in the middle of the room, next to which are two benches and a chair. [Mikael](/wiki/Skyrim:Mikael "Skyrim:Mikael") stands next to the chair when performing, and any of the town's residents may dance while he performs. [Sinmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinmir "Skyrim:Sinmir") will stay in this area, alternating between sitting, standing, and occasionally dancing. On either side of the front door are small tables with three chairs. There is another table and two chairs against the south wall and another against the north wall. Just past the entrance to the kitchen area are two more chairs. In the southeast corner are two chairs, where [Uthgerd](/wiki/Skyrim:Uthgerd_the_Unbroken "Skyrim:Uthgerd the Unbroken") sits. On this table is a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Maven "Skyrim:Letter from Maven") from Maven to Christophe. Everything on the tables around the common room is displayed merchandise for sale that can be bought or stolen, except the [plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate"), [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"), [bowls](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl") and a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd").

To the south of the fire is the bar with two stools with [Hulda](/wiki/Skyrim:Hulda "Skyrim:Hulda") leaning on the counter. Behind the bar there are two cupboards holding a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina")\*, a [mammoth tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Tusk "Skyrim:Mammoth Tusk"), a sample of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita")\*, and a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") as well as more items for sale that can be stolen or bought. There are a couple of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels against the west wall with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing leveled items between them, while against the east wall is a narrow table holding an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword") and more [Displayed Merchandise](#Displayed_Merchandise). Hanging from a beam behind the counter are two bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), two [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"). Everything on the counter is displayed merchandise, except for a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). Under the counter is a copy of *[Fall from Glory](/wiki/Skyrim:Fall_from_Glory "Skyrim:Fall from Glory")*.

The eastern main floor bedroom consists of a single owned bed in the southeast corner, with an end table beside it holding a plate, bowl and goblet. Opposite the doorway, against the east wall is a small cupboard containing clutter, with a low table and chair in the northeast corner and a wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") against the west wall.

Bannered Mare's kitchen

The kitchen consists of a fire pit with a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") over it against the west wall. A second entrance is to the right of it. A table and two chairs are in the northwest corner, with wall shelves holding plates and other clutter above it. Against the south wall is a set of shelves holding more displayed merchandise, with several food sacks on top. In the southeast corner is a food barrel with a cupboard to the left against the east wall holding more items for sale and the unique [Argonian Ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Ale "Skyrim:Argonian Ale"), which is required for a [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Ale_Extraction "Skyrim:Argonian Ale Extraction") received from [Brenuin](/wiki/Skyrim:Brenuin "Skyrim:Brenuin"). To the left of the cupboard is a table. On the table is the business ledger, an apprentice-locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") containing random items and various items displayed for sale. Rising from the northeast corner along the east wall is a flight of stairs that lead to the top floor, with several barrels and sacks of foodstuffs underneath them.

At the top of the stairs there is an landing with a small wardrobe against the west wall. To the north is a wooden door into [Saadia's](/wiki/Skyrim:Saadia "Skyrim:Saadia") room. It consists of an owned single bed in the northeast corner, with an end table and washbasin beside it. At the foot of the bed against the north wall is a wardrobe, with an unlocked chest containing leveled items on top of it. To the left of the door as you enter is a small square table and two chairs, with a small coin purse on the table. The southern bedroom is Hulda's. It consists of a single owned bed in the southeast corner, with a copy of *[Thief of Virtue](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_of_Virtue "Skyrim:Thief of Virtue")* under the bed. To the right is a chair and an end table. At the foot of the bed against the south wall is a narrow table, with a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute") and a couple of [cups](/wiki/Skyrim:Cup "Skyrim:Cup") on top. Against the east wall is a dresser with a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum") and some pottery on top. If you [chop wood](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood") for Hulda, her bed becomes usable along with the rentable one.

Room for rent

In the northeastern corner of the common room there is a flight of stairs, with crates and sacks under it, leading up to the rentable room in the establishment. At the top of the stairs is a small landing with a cupboard in front of you and the door to a bedroom on your right. There is a large double bed against the west wall, with an end table to the right and a doorway to a balcony overlooking the common room to the left. A second end table is to the left of the doorway to the balcony and opposite against the east wall is a dresser, with a washbasin to the left. On the balcony is a cupboard against the south wall and a low table and two low chairs to the north.

## Displayed Merchandise

The following items are sitting out in the store, on the store counter, in the cupboards behind the counter, on the tables around the common room, and even in the kitchen. Low-value items can be taken after selling more than 100 coins worth of firewood to Hulda. Other items can be purchased from the merchant or can be stolen. Other items may also be present in the store, but those other items are not available for purchase. They [respawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") after ten days.

|  |
| --- |
| - **Food**: 5 bottles of [Ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), 11 bottles of [Alto Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), 1 [Apple Pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"), 1 [Baked Potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), 1 [Boiled Creme Treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"), 8 loaves of [Bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), 2 [Cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), 3 [Eidar Cheese Wedges](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), 1 [Eidar Cheese Wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), 3 [Goat Cheese Wedges](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), 4 [Goat Cheese Wheels](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), 5 [Green Apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), 2 portions of [Grilled Leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), 2 [Honey Nut Treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat"), 2 [Leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), 2 bottles of [Nord Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), 4 [Potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), 2 joints of [Raw Beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef"), 5 [Red Apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), 5 pieces of [Salmon Meats](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Meat "Skyrim:Salmon Meat"), 1 [Salmon Steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), 4 [Sliced Eidar Cheeses](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), 3 [Sliced Goat Cheeses](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"), 3 [Sweet Rolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), 9 [Tomatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato"), 2 haunches of [Venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison"), 11 bottles of [Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") |

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in the inn's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") or stolen. They are restocked every two days.

| Count | Item |
| --- | --- |
| 4 | [Honningbrew Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead") |
| 7 | Random [drinks](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Beverages "Skyrim:Food") |
| 10 | Random inn [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") |
| 1 | [Salt Pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") |

## Notes

- There is a  "Loot") Loot [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to the bottom right of the entrance door. There is a mammoth tusk, two unlocked chests, a strongbox, and many food items in the store. The store also contains the unique [Argonian Ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Ale "Skyrim:Argonian Ale"), found on the kitchen cupboard.
- Selling [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood") to Hulda makes low value items freely available, including use of the two beds (Hulda's and rentable) which will then grant the [well rested](/wiki/Skyrim:Well_Rested "Skyrim:Well Rested") bonus.
- The items marked with "\*" become displayed merchandise, once you have the Merchant speech perk.
- All containers in the area, with the exception of some barrels and food sacks, are non-respawning.
- The game has quite a difficult time determining who the inn's backup innkeeper is supposed to be, as this was seemingly changed numerous times throughout development:
  - Saadia is a potential member of the JobbInnkeeper faction, which means she can become a full member if the actual innkeeper dies. She also holds that same potential status in the JobRentRoom faction, and in the unused quest [Supply Line](/wiki/Skyrim:Supply_Line "Skyrim:Supply Line"), the backup innkeeper dialogue was assigned to her. Saadia was likely skipped for this backup role due to possible outcomes of her quest [In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need").
  - [Olfina Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Olfina_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Olfina Gray-Mane") is not a member of any of the relevant factions like Saadia, but her class is set to "Food vendor", like the average innkeeper, and she actually has the required scripts attached to rent out beds at the Bannered Mare. Also, both her boyfriend [Jon Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Jon_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Jon Battle-Born"), and owner of the [Drunken Huntsman](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Drunken_Huntsman "Skyrim:The Drunken Huntsman"), [Elrindir](/wiki/Skyrim:Elrindir "Skyrim:Elrindir"), will refer to Olfina as the new innkeeper of the Bannered Mare if Hulda is dead. This was likely changed after Olfina was made possible Stormcloak housecarl.
  - Mikael has the dialogue for the rumors Hulda usually gives out, something neither Saadia nor Olfina have. Besides this, he is also a potential member of the three required factions, just like Saadia was. However, unlike Olfina, there is no dialogue for other NPCs that mention Mikael running the inn, neither does he possess the required script to rent out beds. Despite this, Mikael seems to be the most likely candidate to take over in the final game.
  - Ysolda has dialogue implying she wants to buy the inn from Hulda, while the latter also has dialogue implying she wants to sell to Ysolda. In the `DialogueWhiterun` quest that contains aliases for important people in town, Ysolda is marked as the "InnkeeperBackup", but also as the "PawnshopOwnerBackup". Ysolda also starts out a spart of the Belethor's Goods service faction. While it seems she was more likely intended to take over Belethor's store, she lacks the finished scripting to take over either store.
- During [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun"), the building will have a barricade across the main entrance and both doors will be expert-locked. However, if you pick the lock, both Hulda and Saadia will have their normal speech options, welcoming you and are willing to trade.
  - Installing the [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") add-on and adopting [Lucia](/wiki/Skyrim:Lucia "Skyrim:Lucia") before the battle has begun will cause her to be transferred here until the battle is over. This happens because her editor location is here and CWCitizensFlee will pick her up in one of the aliases.

## Bugs

- You may only need to pay for the rented bed once, as it does not always revert to being owned after 24 hours.
- The goblet may clip through the plate on the bar stool next to where Mikael performs. **?**
- You cannot sit on the bench nearest the counter.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- Mikael and Saadia don't own their proper beds here and may sometimes be unable to sleep.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, fixes this bug.
- Ysolda will still ask [Olfina Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Olfina_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Olfina Gray-Mane") if she works in the inn even if they're IN the building while Olfina is working. In addition, [Carlotta Valentia](/wiki/Skyrim:Carlotta_Valentia "Skyrim:Carlotta Valentia") and her daughter [Mila](/wiki/Skyrim:Mila_Valentia "Skyrim:Mila Valentia") have a conversation about getting to eat at the inn even if they're already inside.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.0, fixes this bug.
- When you open the main entry door, the ring on the right door seems to disappear for a moment.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.9, fixes this bug.
- During [Dampened Sprits](/wiki/Skyrim:Dampened_Spirits "Skyrim:Dampened Spirits"), [Eimar](/wiki/Skyrim:Eimar "Skyrim:Eimar") has some lines at the Bannered Mare that don't make sense for him to use while he's here. One wasn't conditioned to the location he's in, and the other was using an incorrect function to check if the latter is finished or not.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.7, fixes this bug.
- Sometimes Rexus will not be here but will still be in Volunruud.
- If you aim the camera up when looking at the main firepit, the flame will appear to go out, but the heat visual effect will stay. **?**
- Sometimes when you run into Mikael while he plays on his lute he will put away his lute, but you will still hear it.
- If both Saadia and Hulda are dead and you've married Ysolda you can sleep in any of the owned beds despite them being tagged as such. **?**

# Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Amol

Imperial Archers attacking a Stormcloak Soldier.

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Report for duty to [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") at the [Eastmarch Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Eastmarch Imperial Camp").
2. Join the Legion soldiers staging for the attack.
3. Clear the fort of Stormcloak rebels.

### Report for Duty

Report for duty to [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") at the [Eastmarch Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Eastmarch Imperial Camp"), where she will give you orders to rendezvous with a group of Imperial soldiers preparing to attack [Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Amol "Skyrim:Fort Amol") and to assist in the assault.

### Join the Soldiers Preparing the Assault

Make your way to Fort Amol and meet with the group of soldiers. As you approach the group, they will begin the assault.

### Take the Fort

Assist your fellow soldiers in clearing the fort of Stormcloak rebels while the game updates you with the percentage of enemies remaining. The battle takes place in the exterior parts of the fort only, in the courtyard and on the walls. The entrance is blocked by wooden barricades, but these can be easily brought down by melee attacks.

Once you have killed all Stormcloak rebels the quest will be completed and the [Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim") questline will resume, prompting you to report to Legate Rikke. When you do so she will reward you with a leveled amount of gold and automatically start the next quest in the series, [Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm").

## Notes

- After completion of this quest, like any Civil War quest under [Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim"), unmarked by in-game references, you can approach Legate Rikke for a [medium leveled gold reward](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Gold_Rewards "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"); this is not always recommended, as entering her cell sets up the next quest in the series and, if triggered improperly, causes the missing *"Reporting for duty."* dialogue option (see [this](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim#Bugs "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim") bug section). Return to Legate Rikke to receive the leveled gold reward only when you want to start the next quest in the series and skip the reward when the game doesn't prompt you to return to her. Don't approach Rikke between quests of different holds.

## Bugs

- Occasionally you may be wrongly given a Stormcloak quest, [The Battle for Fort Snowhawk](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Snowhawk_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Snowhawk (Stormcloaks)"). In this case, Imperial soldiers will not appear near the fort, making it impossible to join them. The fort is empty, making it impossible to take it. Although it may appear that necromancers took the fort before the battle, no necromancers appear either. Proceeding directly to Fort Amol and killing all of the Stormcloak soldiers there will not complete the quest either.
- When you go to Regain Eastmarch and you have to talk to Legate Rikke, sometimes you don't get the option to "Report for Duty". This disables you from continuing the quest until you can get that option. Sometimes when you go to Join the Men, you can't find them and they are not there. When you go to take Fort Amol, you can't find the Stormcloaks. This leads to the quest being unable to finish.
  -  Use the command `player.setstage CWFortSiegeFort 100` as it spawns the Stormcloaks and the Imperials, however make sure to do it at the Imperial rendezvous point, since the Stormcloaks will be hostile.
  - Simply exiting conversation and talking to Legate Rikke again may offer the option.
  - If Rikke offers dialogue other than "Report for duty", such as "Why did you join the Imperials" (or similar), select those conversations first. The "Report for duty" dialogue option may then appear.
  - If a dragon attacks the Imperial Camp, this will cause all of the inhabitants (including Legate Rikke) to attack the dragon. After the dragon has been dispatched, the "Report for Duty" dialogue option will appear.
  - Conjuring an atronach in the middle of camp, then killing it may also fix this.
  - Not Fast Traveling to Fort Amol, but walking to the location from another combined with a reduced inventory and confirming the presence of walking Stormcloaks and interacting with them (not attacking or killing until the battle) after the Battle of Fort Sungard, again before talking to General Tullius, again before talking to Legate Rikke to start the 'Battle of Fort Amol' quest and then walking to Fort Amol has resolved the disappearing soldiers issue for some.
  -  Travel to Fort Amol and kill every necromancer. After that, sleep in one of the beds and Stormcloaks should occupy the Fort. Use `movetoqt CWObj` to directly teleport to Rikke. If the option doesn't show, talk to Tullius in Castle Dour by entering the following command in the console `coc SolitudeCastleDour`, and then go to Rikke with the previous command.
  - See talk page for other possible fixes.

## Quest Stages

| The Battle for Fort Amol (CWFortSiegeFort) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Legate Rikke has sent me to assist in taking Fort Amol from the enemy. *Objective 10:* Join the men attacking Fort Amol |
| 50 |  | *Objective 100:* Take over Fort Amol by defeating the enemy (<Global=CWPercentPoolRemainingDefender>% Remaining) |
| 9000 | ☑ | We have succeeded in taking Fort Amol from the enemy. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 100, 200, 300, 400, 500, 910, 920, 950, 1000, 2000, 9200, 9999.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CWFortSiegeFort stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CWFortSiegeFort`.

# Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Dunstad (Imperial)

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. This article is about the Imperial version of this mission. For the Stormcloak version, see [The Battle for Fort Dunstad (Stormcloaks)](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Dunstad_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Dunstad (Stormcloaks)").
