.jpg)

A Stormcloak defending Fort Dunstad

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Get your orders from Legate Rikke at the Pale Imperial Camp.
2. Rendezvous with the legionnaires southeast of [Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dunstad "Skyrim:Fort Dunstad").
3. Clear the fort of Stormcloak rebels.
4. Report the news to General Tullius.

### Receiving the Quest

After completing A False Front, report for duty again to Legate Rikke at the Pale Imperial Camp.

Having learned that the Stormcloak-held Fort Dunstad is in need of reinforcements, she will command you to help to take the fort while it is vulnerable. She will instruct you to rendezvous with a task force of Imperial soldiers who are staging near the fort, southeast of your location. She will mark the meeting point on your map, and you will update your journal to note this objective.

### Join the Men Attacking the Fort

| A Route to the Rendezvous Point |
| --- |
| Walk westward out of the camp until you encounter a paved road running north-south. This can be difficult to see when visibility is poor. If you see it, turn left onto it; otherwise, head south from a short distance west of the camp, bearing to the east if necessary to navigate past obstacles. If you are following the paved road, you will pass two rocky areas to your left. There is an easily found iron ore vein in the second of these.  You will soon reach another paved road. Turn left on this. After a moderate distance, the road will take you on a significant descent down the mountain. Keep your eye on the paving stones to avoid losing your way. Eventually, the pavement will end at a T-intersection with the major road running between Whiterun and Dawnstar. Turn right onto this, heading upwards again. Follow this road generally south, around a few bends alternatively to the south and east, until you come upon the task force. |

02.jpg)

A group of legionnaires preparing to converge on the fort

As you approach the waiting soldiers, they will charge toward the fort. Your objective becomes to take it over from the rebels. As your team engages the Stormcloaks holding the fort, you will receive regular updates on the percentage of enemies remaining.

### Take Fort Dunstad

The entire battle will take place in the exterior areas of the fort.

If you have not yet developed an eye for distinguishing between Imperial friendlies and rebel enemies, the Stormcloaks are easily identified by their pointed helmets.

The battle will comprise multiple pairs and small clusters of engagements, with both sides using melee weapons and archery attacks. These engagements occur at multiple points in the two courtyard-like areas, and along the elevated wooden platforms around the semi-perimeter.

If you let them, your group will essentially take care of the battle for you. If you hang back and take the most passive approach to the fight, you may need only to restore your health once or twice when you are targeted. If you want to prioritize acquiring weapons and armor off of fallen soldiers, you should search them quickly because their bodies will disappear shortly after falling.

Often, there are actually some Stormcloaks remaining (or respawning) after the battle has been formally won, which you can engage and loot. Also, if you so wish, you may kill the remaining Imperials as well in order to loot them without getting a bounty.

When it's reported that all the rebels have been killed, you will have completed the objective of taking the fort and the quest itself.

### Report to General Tullius

Your objective then becomes to report to General Tullius at Castle Dour to receive your reward, but doing so technically occurs under the overarching [Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim") quest. After you have taken the fort, The Battle for Fort Dunstad will clear from your journal. If you didn't flee the battle, Tullius will promote you to [Praefect](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion#Ranks "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") along with a leveled sword (see [Bugs](#Bugs)).

## Notes

- If [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") is given to the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") then this quest will not be given to you.
- Completing this quest will exile [Skald](/wiki/Skyrim:Skald "Skyrim:Skald") and his courtiers to the [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings"), and install [Brina Merilis](/wiki/Skyrim:Brina_Merilis "Skyrim:Brina Merilis") as [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of The Pale.
- After completion of this quest, like any Civil War quest under [Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim"), unmarked by in-game references, you can approach Legate Rikke for a [medium leveled gold reward](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Gold_Rewards "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"); this is not always recommended, as entering her cell sets up the next quest in the series and, if triggered improperly, causes the missing *"Reporting for duty."* dialogue option (see [this](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim#Bugs "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim") bug section). Return to Legate Rikke to receive the leveled gold reward only when you want to start the next quest in the series and skip the reward when the game doesn't prompt you to return to her. Don't approach Rikke between quests of different holds.

## Bugs

- After the quest, [Compelling Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Compelling_Tribute_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Compelling Tribute (Imperial)") becomes available and activates (even if it doesn't appear in your journal) upon your next load of the cell of [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") (usually relocated to [Rift Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Rift Imperial Camp")). If you do so prior to reporting to [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius") (for example to get the leveled gold reward for this quest) the game activates [Compelling Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Compelling_Tribute_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Compelling Tribute (Imperial)") incorrectly causing a [bug](/wiki/Skyrim:Compelling_Tribute_(Imperial)#Bugs "Skyrim:Compelling Tribute (Imperial)") by generating and extra non-quest item copy of the [incriminating letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Incriminating_Letter_(Anuriel) "Skyrim:Incriminating Letter (Anuriel)"). **?**
  - Avoid Rift Imperial Camp and Legate Rikke, go straight to report to General Tullius instead. Upon your next approach to Legate Rikke, [Complelling Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Compelling_Tribute_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Compelling Tribute (Imperial)") will have set up correctly. This skips the leveled gold reward for this quest.
- Sometimes you can travel to the Pale Imperial Camp and there will be a quest marker in the camp itself, which does nothing on approaching it. **?**
  - This can sometimes be fixed by waiting for a few hours at that location. Eventually, Legate Rikke will arrive and the quest marker moves to her. You can then approach her and continue the quest.
- If you kill all the guards outside the fort before you are given this quest, and take the quest during the time it takes the guards to respawn, the quest will be bugged. Imperial soldiers won't appear near the fort, and the whole fort is going to be empty. On the quests page, you won't be able to press the button to show the quest location on the map and it will say you have failed to meet the Imperial soldiers and you have to take the fort yourself, with 100% remaining, except there are no soldiers in the fort. **?**
  -  Open the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") and type `setstage CWFortSiegeFort 10`. This should force the Stormcloaks and Imperials to spawn.
  -  To fix this you will have to complete the quest using the console command `completequest CWFortSiegeFort` and then getting the quest from Rikke.
  -  You can also advance the quest to completion with console command `setstage CWFortSiegeFort 9000` which advances the attack on the Fort to success and updates the objective to report to Tullius.
  - This can also occur even if you have never been to the fort. Imperial soldiers won't appear near the fort, the whole fort is empty, and on the quests page you can't press the button to show the quest location on the map.
- Sometimes Stormcloaks will get stuck in place. They will not always be able to attack you, and you can not attack them either. They are essentially unkillable. **?**
  - There is a work around where you must open the console and use the kill command on them.

## Quest Stages

| The Battle for Fort Dunstad (CWFortSiegeFort) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Legate Rikke has sent me to assist in taking Fort Dunstad from the enemy. *Objective 10:* Join the men attacking Fort Dunstad |
| 50 |  | *Objective 100:* Take over Fort Dunstad by defeating the enemy (<Global=CWPercentPoolRemainingDefender>% Remaining) |
| 9000 | ☑ | We have succeeded in taking Fort Dunstad from the enemy. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 100, 200, 300, 400, 500, 910, 920, 950, 1000, 2000, 9200, 9999.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CWFortSiegeFort stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CWFortSiegeFort`.

Overview of [Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dunstad "Skyrim:Fort Dunstad")

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Get your orders from [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") at the [Pale Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Pale_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Pale Stormcloak Camp").
2. Meet the Stormcloaks east of the fort.
3. Take the fort.

### Receiving Orders

You will only be assigned this quest if you chose to give [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") to the Imperial Legion during the quest [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"). Go to the [Pale Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Pale_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Pale Stormcloak Camp") and talk to [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist"). Galmar will tell you to go to [Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dunstad "Skyrim:Fort Dunstad") and meet the Stormcloaks preparing for the attack.

### Assaulting the Fort

Head northwest and join up with the men east of the fort. Speak to the leader of this force and he will agree to attack as soon as you are ready. If necessary, take a few moments to prepare and then lead the charge up the southeastern road. All Imperial forces must be eliminated. Your journal will keep track of the percentage of enemies left. While a straightforward battle beginning at the front entrance and working into the fort may be preferable for melee fighters, the fort also has several towers which are ideal for archers and ranged attacks.

### Conquering Hero

Once the enemy is fully vanquished, head back to [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") and [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak"). He bestows upon you the title of Bone-Breaker and gives you a leveled weapon in honor of this new rank. You are now also able to purchase a [home](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjerim "Skyrim:Hjerim") in Windhelm. Your next assignment will be the [Liberation of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim").

## Notes

- Completing this quest will exile [Brina Merilis](/wiki/Skyrim:Brina_Merilis "Skyrim:Brina Merilis") and [Horik Halfhand](/wiki/Skyrim:Horik_Halfhand "Skyrim:Horik Halfhand") to the [The Winking Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Winking_Skeever "Skyrim:The Winking Skeever"), and re-install [Skald](/wiki/Skyrim:Skald "Skyrim:Skald") as [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of The Pale.

## Bugs

- It may not be possible to obtain this quest. During Phase Two of the negotiations in [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending#Allied_with_the_Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Season Unending"), the option to give up Dawnstar is never offered, even if the score is negative. **?**

The battle begins

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Report for duty to [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") at the [Rift Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Rift Imperial Camp").
2. Join the Legion soldiers staging for the attack.
3. Clear the fort of Stormcloak rebels.

### Report for Duty

Report for duty to [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") at the [Rift Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Rift Imperial Camp"), where she will give you orders to rendezvous with a group of Imperial soldiers preparing to attack [Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greenwall "Skyrim:Fort Greenwall") and to assist in the assault.

### Join the Soldiers Preparing the Assault

Make your way to Fort Greenwall. The fort is just north of Riften, and the soldiers are waiting just southeast of the fort. As you approach the group, they will storm the southeast entrance to the fort.

### Take the Fort

Assist your fellow soldiers in clearing the fort of Stormcloak rebels while the game updates you with the percentage of enemies remaining. The battle takes place in the exterior parts of the fort only, in the courtyard and on the walls. The entrance is blocked by wooden barricades, but these can be easily brought down by melee attacks.

Once you have killed all Stormcloak rebels, the quest will be completed.

### Report to General Tullius

Your objective then becomes to report to General Tullius at Castle Dour to receive your reward, but doing so technically occurs under the overarching [Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim") quest. After you have taken the fort, The Battle for Fort Greenwall will clear from your journal. If you didn't flee the battle, Tullius will promote you to [Tribune](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion#Ranks "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") along with a leveled sword (see [Bugs](#Bugs)).

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is unlocked at the end of this quest:

-  **[War Hero](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Hero "Skyrim:War Hero")** (10 points/Bronze) — Capture [Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard "Skyrim:Fort Sungard") or [Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greenwall "Skyrim:Fort Greenwall")

## Notes

- Corpses will disappear shortly after death, so you may wish to loot them as you go to avoid missing out.
- If [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") is given to the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") then this quest will not be given to you.
- Even after you are told that 0% of the defenders remain and that you have won, there may still be several Stormcloak survivors who flee northeast along the road in the direction of the mining settlement of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone"). If you decide to pursue them, be careful of who you target, especially in the dark, since you can easily kill some of the local guards of Shor's Stone by mistake and incur a bounty in the Rift.
- Once the battle begins at the fort, Rikke leaves The Rift Imperial Camp and it is instead commanded by [Legate Fasendil](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Fasendil "Skyrim:Legate Fasendil"). After the battle is finished and the quest clears in the journal, the Rift Imperial Camp will be packed up and abandoned.
- Completing this quest will exile [Laila Law-Giver](/wiki/Skyrim:Laila_Law-Giver "Skyrim:Laila Law-Giver") and her courtiers to the [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings"), and install [Maven Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar") as [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of The Rift.
- After completion of this quest, like any Civil War quest under [Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim"), unmarked by in-game references, you can approach Legate Rikke for a [medium leveled gold reward](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Gold_Rewards "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"); this is not always recommended, as entering her cell sets up the next quest in the series and, if triggered improperly, causes the missing *"Reporting for duty."* dialogue option (see [this](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim#Bugs "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim") bug section). Return to Legate Rikke to receive the leveled gold reward only when you want to start the next quest in the series and skip the reward when the game doesn't prompt you to return to her. Don't approach Rikke between quests of different holds.

## Bugs

- After [The Battle for Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Dunstad_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Dunstad (Imperial)"), if General Tullius will promote you to Praefect rank you are actually promoted to Tribune with related leveled shield. It is not possible to get the actual Praefect rank. Since you already are, this will also "skip" the actual promotion to Tribune after The Battle for Fort Greenwall. **?**

  **Mod Notes**: mistake in the script TIF\_\_000CE0E8: there is "3", should be "2".

## Quest Stages

| The Battle for Fort Greenwall (CWFortSiegeFort) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Legate Rikke has sent me to assist in taking Fort Greenwall from the enemy. *Objective 10:* Join the men attacking Fort Greenwall |
| 50 |  | *Objective 100:* Take over Fort Greenwall by defeating the enemy (<Global=CWPercentPoolRemainingDefender>% Remaining) |
| 9000 | ☑ | We have succeeded in taking Fort Greenwall from the enemy. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 100, 200, 300, 400, 500, 910, 920, 950, 1000, 2000, 9200, 9999.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CWFortSiegeFort stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CWFortSiegeFort`.

# Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Greenwall (Stormcloaks)

## Overview

Stormcloaks and Imperials battling in Fort Greenwall.

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Get your orders from [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") at the [Rift Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Rift Stormcloak Camp").
2. Meet the Stormcloaks south of the fort.
3. Take the fort.

## Detailed Walkthrough

You will only receive this quest if you chose to give [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") to the Imperial Legion during the quest [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"). Go to the [Rift Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Rift Stormcloak Camp") and talk to [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist"). Galmar will tell you to go to [Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greenwall "Skyrim:Fort Greenwall") and meet the Stormcloaks preparing for the attack. Meet with the men south of the fort, and then attack the fort. Your journal will keep track of the percentage of enemies left. Once all the Imperials are dead, you will have to head back to [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") for the next part in the [Liberation of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim") quest.

## Notes

- This quest will take the place of [The Battle for Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Sungard_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Sungard (Stormcloaks)").
- Completing this quest will re-install [Laila Law-Giver](/wiki/Skyrim:Laila_Law-Giver "Skyrim:Laila Law-Giver") as [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of The Rift.

## Quest Stages

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CWFortSiegeFort stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CWFortSiegeFort`.

The Imperial Legion's last bastion before you take the battle to the capital

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Get your orders from [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist").
2. Meet the Stormcloaks preparing for battle.
3. Eliminate the Imperials.
4. Return to Galmar.

## Detailed Walkthrough

[Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") will order you to join the men preparing to attack [Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad"). When you reach the staging area, your fellow Stormcloaks will storm the fort. Your objective is to eliminate all the Imperial soldiers and your journal will track the percentage of completion. Wooden barricades will block the entrance to the fort—these are easily destroyed in a few hits.

After you have eliminated the Imperials, the quest will be complete and you will have to return to Galmar for the final assault on Solitude to [liberate Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim") from Empire control.

## Notes

- Both bodies and alive soldiers will disappear as you walk out of the fort area.
- Not all the enemies are present at the start of the mission; more will spawn when certain numbers are killed.
- The Imperial soldiers will occasionally drop one of the Divines' amulets (excluding Talos).
- You will generally see surviving Imperial soldiers, even when your screen indicates they are all dead. It is not necessary to kill these to finish the quest.

## Bugs

- Stormcloaks and Imperials do not show up at Fort Hraggstad. A similar bug can happen at the other fort quests.
  -  Open the console and type `setstage 00083042 10`. This should force the Stormcloaks and Imperials to spawn.
  - Walking to the fort from the camp to avoid a load screen also seems to work.

Imperial and Stormcloak soldiers battling on the Fort Kastav Balcony

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Get your orders from [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") at the [Winterhold Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Winterhold Stormcloak Camp").
2. Meet the Stormcloaks west of the fort.
3. Take the fort.

## Detailed Walkthrough

You will only receive this quest if you chose to give [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") to the Imperial Legion during the quest [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"). Go to the [Winterhold Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Winterhold Stormcloak Camp") and talk to [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist"). Galmar will tell you to go to [Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:Fort Kastav") and meet the Stormcloaks preparing for the attack. Meet with the men west of the fort, and then attack the fort. Your journal will keep track of the percentage of enemies left. Once all the Imperials are dead, you will have to head back to [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") for the next part in the [Liberation of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim") quest.

## Notes

- Completing this quest will exile [Kraldar](/wiki/Skyrim:Kraldar "Skyrim:Kraldar") and [Thonjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Thonjolf "Skyrim:Thonjolf") to the [Erikur's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur%27s_House "Skyrim:Erikur's House"), and re-install [Korir](/wiki/Skyrim:Korir "Skyrim:Korir") as [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of Winterhold.

## Quest Stages

| The Battle for Fort Kastav (CWFortSiegeFort) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Galmar Stone-Fist has sent me to assist in taking Fort Kastav from the enemy. *Objective 10:* Join the men attacking Fort Kastav |
| 50 |  | *Objective 100:* Take over Fort Kastav by defeating the enemy (<Global=CWPercentPoolRemainingDefender>% Remaining) |
| 9000 | ☑ | We have succeeded in taking Fort Kastav from the enemy. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 100, 200, 300, 400, 500, 910, 920, 950, 1000, 2000, 9200, 9999.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CWFortSiegeFort stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CWFortSiegeFort`.

# Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Neugrad

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by multiple users, *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [The honorablest](/wiki/User:The_honorablest "User:The honorablest"), *not checked* |

Stormcloaks attacking the player in Fort Neugrad

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Get your orders from Legate Rikke at the Falkreath Imperial Camp.
2. Rendezvous with the legionnaires north of [Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Fort Neugrad").
3. Clear the fort of Stormcloak rebels.
4. Report the news to General Tullius.

### Report for Duty

When speaking to [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius") he will make a bitter comment about your decision to give up [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"). He will then direct you to [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") at the [Falkreath Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Falkreath Imperial Camp"). She will give you orders to rendezvous with a group of Imperial soldiers preparing to attack [Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Fort Neugrad") and to assist in the assault.

### Join the Soldiers Preparing the Assault

Make your way to Fort Neugrad. The fort is located a small ways west of hold capital [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"), and the soldiers are waiting just southwest of the fort. As you approach the group, they will draw their weapons and attack the fort.

### Take the Fort

Assist your fellow soldiers in clearing the fort of Stormcloak rebels while the game updates you with the percentage of enemies remaining. The battle takes place in the exterior parts of the fort only, in the courtyard and on the walls.

Once you have killed all Stormcloak rebels, the quest will be completed. The [Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim") quest will update and prompt you to return to General Tullius to report your success and receive your reward.

## Notes

- Only if [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") is given to the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") this quest will be given to you.
- Completing this quest will exile [Dengeir of Stuhn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dengeir_of_Stuhn "Skyrim:Dengeir of Stuhn") and [Tekla](/wiki/Skyrim:Tekla "Skyrim:Tekla") to [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall"), and re-install [Siddgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Siddgeir "Skyrim:Siddgeir") as [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of Falkreath.
- After completion of this quest, like any Civil War quest under [Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim"), unmarked by in-game references, you can approach Legate Rikke for a [medium leveled gold reward](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Gold_Rewards "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"); this is not always recommended, as entering her cell sets up the next quest in the series and, if triggered improperly, causes the missing *"Reporting for duty."* dialogue option (see [this](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim#Bugs "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim") bug section). Return to Legate Rikke to receive the leveled gold reward only when you want to start the next quest in the series and skip the reward when the game doesn't prompt you to return to her. Don't approach Rikke between quests of different holds.

## Quest Stages

- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CWFortSiegeFort stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CWFortSiegeFort`.

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Report for duty to [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") at the [Hjaalmarch Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch Imperial Camp").
2. Join the Legion soldiers gathering for the attack.
3. Clear the fort of Stormcloak rebels.

### Report for Duty

When speaking to [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius") he will make a bitter comment about your decision to give up [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"). He will then direct you to [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") at the [Hjaalmarch Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch Imperial Camp"). She will give you orders to rendezvous with a group of Imperial soldiers preparing to attack [Fort Snowhawk](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Snowhawk "Skyrim:Fort Snowhawk") and to assist in the assault.

### Join the Soldiers Preparing the Assault

Make your way to Fort Snowhawk. The fort is located a small ways west of hold capital [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"), and the soldiers are waiting just southwest of the fort. As you approach the group, they will draw their weapons and attack the fort.

### Take the Fort

Assist your fellow soldiers in clearing the fort of Stormcloak rebels while the game updates you with the percentage of enemies remaining. The battle takes place in the exterior parts of the fort only, in the courtyard and on the walls.

Once you have killed all Stormcloak rebels, the quest will be completed. The [Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim") quest will update and prompt you to return to General Tullius to report your success and receive your reward.

## Notes

- If [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") is given to the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") then this quest will not be given to you.
- Completing this quest will send [Sorli the Builder](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorli_the_Builder "Skyrim:Sorli the Builder") and her courtiers back to [Stonehills](/wiki/Skyrim:Stonehills "Skyrim:Stonehills"), and re-install [Idgrod Ravencrone](/wiki/Skyrim:Idgrod_Ravencrone "Skyrim:Idgrod Ravencrone") as [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of Hjaalmarch.
- After completion of this quest, like any Civil War quest under [Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim"), unmarked by in-game references, you can approach Legate Rikke for a [medium leveled gold reward](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Gold_Rewards "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"); this is not always recommended, as entering her cell sets up the next quest in the series and, if triggered improperly, causes the missing *"Reporting for duty."* dialogue option (see [this](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim#Bugs "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim") bug section). Return to Legate Rikke to receive the leveled gold reward only when you want to start the next quest in the series and skip the reward when the game doesn't prompt you to return to her. Don't approach Rikke between quests of different holds.

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Get your orders from [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist").
2. Meet the men preparing for the attack.
3. Defeat the Imperials.
4. Return to [Ulfric](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak").

## Detailed Walkthrough

[Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") will tell you to meet the Stormcloak soldiers southwest of [Fort Snowhawk](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Snowhawk "Skyrim:Fort Snowhawk") and to help them attack the fort. When you arrive, the soldiers will begin to storm the fort and your journal will tell you to kill all the Imperials and keep track of the percentage left. There will be some wooden barricades blocking the entrance to the fort—three hits from a weapon or Destruction spell will destroy them. Fight alongside your Stormcloak brothers and finish off the Imperial soldiers. After the Imperials have been defeated, the quest will end and you will have to head back to [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") for the next part of [Liberation of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim").

## Notes

- Completing this quest will exile [Idgrod Ravencrone](/wiki/Skyrim:Idgrod_Ravencrone "Skyrim:Idgrod Ravencrone"), her family, and courtiers to the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace"), and install [Sorli the Builder](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorli_the_Builder "Skyrim:Sorli the Builder") as [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of Hjaalmarch.
- Completing this quest will also complete the quest [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") and advance the quest [The Fallen](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fallen "Skyrim:The Fallen") to the objective "Learn Shout to call Odahviing".
- If [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") is given to the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") then this quest will not be given to you.

## Quest Stages

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CWFortSiegeFort stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CWFortSiegeFort`.

# Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Sungard (Imperial)

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. Imperial and Stormcloak Soldiers battling at Fort Sungard

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Report for duty to [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") at the [Reach Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Reach_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Reach Imperial Camp").
2. Join the Legion soldiers gathering for the attack.
3. Clear the fort of Stormcloak rebels.

### Report for Duty

When speaking to [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius") he will make a bitter comment about your decision to give up [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"): *"Hurry over to our military camp tucked away in the Reach. Ulfric's been enjoying those silver mines for far too long. And, soldier. You better help win me back Markarth, or die trying. It was your brilliant strategy to give it over to the rebels in the first place."* [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") can now be found at the [Reach Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Reach_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Reach Imperial Camp"), northeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). She will give you orders to rendezvous with a group of Imperial soldiers preparing to attack [Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard "Skyrim:Fort Sungard") and to assist in the assault.

### Join the Soldiers Preparing the Assault

Fort Sungard is located far east of Markarth, and the soldiers are waiting just northeast of the fort. As you approach the group, they will draw their weapons and take off on a running pace towards the fort entrance.

### Take the Fort

Assist your fellow soldiers in clearing the fort of Stormcloak rebels while the game updates you with the percentage of enemies remaining. The battle takes place in the exterior parts of the fort only, in the courtyard and on the walls.

Once you have killed all Stormcloak rebels, the quest will be completed. The [Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim") quest will update and prompt you to return to General Tullius to report your success and receive your reward.

## Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is unlocked at the end of this quest:

-  **[War Hero](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Hero "Skyrim:War Hero")** (10 points/Bronze) — Capture [Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard "Skyrim:Fort Sungard") or [Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greenwall "Skyrim:Fort Greenwall")

If you did not give [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") to the Imperials during Season Unending, you will already have gotten this achievement from [The Battle for Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Greenwall_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Greenwall (Imperial)").

## Notes

- Only if [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") is given to the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") this quest will be given to you.
- Completing this quest will exile [Thongvor Silver-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Thongvor_Silver-Blood "Skyrim:Thongvor Silver-Blood") and his courtiers to the [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings"), and re-install [Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund") as [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of The Reach.
- After completion of this quest, like any Civil War quest under [Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim"), unmarked by in-game references, you can approach Legate Rikke for a [medium leveled gold reward](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Gold_Rewards "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"); this is not always recommended, as entering her cell sets up the next quest in the series and, if triggered improperly, causes the missing *"Reporting for duty."* dialogue option (see [this](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim#Bugs "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim") bug section). Return to Legate Rikke to receive the leveled gold reward only when you want to start the next quest in the series and skip the reward when the game doesn't prompt you to return to her. Don't approach Rikke between quests of different holds.

Imperial and Stormcloak Soldiers battling at Fort Sungard

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Get your orders from [Galmar](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist").
2. Meet the men preparing for the attack.
3. Take the fort.

### Battle for the fort

After finishing the previous quest and returning to [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist"), he will ask you to meet the men preparing for an attack on [Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard "Skyrim:Fort Sungard"). Head over to the men just north of the fort, and when you reach them they will start running to the fort. Your journal will tell you to take over Fort Sungard by defeating the enemy, and it will keep track of the percentage of enemies left. Simply head up to the fort and assist the Stormcloak soldiers in defeating the Imperials. There are a few wooden barricades out the front of the fort—three hits from a weapon will destroy them. After you have taken the percentage of troops left to kill to zero, the quest will end and you will have to return to [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") for the next part of [Liberation of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim").

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is unlocked at the end of this quest:

-  **[War Hero](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Hero "Skyrim:War Hero")** (10 points/Bronze) — Capture [Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard "Skyrim:Fort Sungard") or [Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greenwall "Skyrim:Fort Greenwall")

## Notes

- Soldiers' bodies disappear shortly after they have been killed.
- If [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") is given to the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") then this quest will not be given to you.
- Completing this quest will send [Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund") to the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace"), and install [Thongvor Silver-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Thongvor_Silver-Blood "Skyrim:Thongvor Silver-Blood") as [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of The Reach.
- Once this quest is finished, the favor quest [Search and Seizure](/wiki/Skyrim:Search_and_Seizure "Skyrim:Search and Seizure") for [Ondolemar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ondolemar "Skyrim:Ondolemar") will be permanently unavailable. If this quest is finished while Search and Seizure is active, you will fail the favor quest immediately. In addition, Ondolemar will perish. His remains will be buried in the [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Markarth) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Markarth)") in Markarth.

## Bugs

- If you approach [Jarl Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund"), [Raerek](/wiki/Skyrim:Raerek "Skyrim:Raerek"), or [Faleen](/wiki/Skyrim:Faleen "Skyrim:Faleen") in the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace") after this quest has been completed, they may attack you on sight. Since all three are essential, they cannot be killed. After the civil war has ended, they will revert back to their non-hostile behavior. **?**
- The Thalmor Soldiers who followed Ondolemar before this quest will continue to respawn in [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep") after the Stormcloaks take Markarth.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:The Bedlam Job

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Beezer1029](/wiki/User:Beezer1029 "User:Beezer1029"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Kiz](/wiki/User:Kiz "User:Kiz"), checked by [Beezer1029](/wiki/User:Beezer1029 "User:Beezer1029") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Thieves Guild.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Thieves_Guild.png) | **Steal a set amount of gold's worth of items.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") |
| Location(s): | [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(place) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (place)"), [Major cities](/wiki/Skyrim:Cities "Skyrim:Cities") |
| Reward: | [Leveled Gold](#Mischief_Managed) |
| ID: | TGRNT |

*"Just steal whatever we can until we've made an impression."*

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Steal 500 gold in goods from the target city.
2. Return to Delvin.

### No Rest for the Wicked

After joining the Thieves Guild, [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") will tell you that he handles all the [fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fishing_Job "Skyrim:The Fishing Job"), [numbers](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Numbers_Job "Skyrim:The Numbers Job"), and bedlam jobs. The purpose of these small side jobs is to help the Guild rebuild and retake their influence around Skyrim. Ask him for a bedlam job and he will explain: *"Sometimes we like to remind a city that we mean business, so we hit it hard. Just steal whatever we can until we've made an impression. Simple right? Almost. The catch is it doesn't count if anyone sees you take it. The message needs to be clear; we work in the shadows. Steal from anywhere in the hold, and you even get to keep everythin' you stole. So, you in?"*

### A State of Bedlam

If you accept the job, Delvin will name one of the five major [cities](/wiki/Skyrim:Cities#Major_Cities "Skyrim:Cities") in Skyrim, although you can actually steal from anywhere in the specified [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds"). [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") in [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") can also be a target for the job if [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") is installed (see [bugs](#Bugs)).

| Major City | Hold |
| --- | --- |
| [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") |
| [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") | [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") |
| [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") | [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") |
| [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") | [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") |
| [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") | [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") |
| [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") [DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") | [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") |

Your objective is to lift five hundred gold worth of general loot without being seen by anyone or caught by the guards.
If you are [caught](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime#Getting_Arrested "Skyrim:Crime") by the guards, the job is forfeited. There is no penalty from the Thieves' Guild; only the inconvenience of being imprisoned, and paying an out-of-pocket fine. You may begin the job again at any time, once you speak with Delvin.
Additionally, if you want to quit the job, whether to acquire a different job or a different city, you can tell Delvin at any time. He grumbles, but there is no actual penalty, no matter how many jobs you quit.

### Mischief Managed

Once you have accumulated the targeted amount of stolen goods from the city or hold, return to Delvin to a leveled amount of gold. You can repeat this quest as often as you like.

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1-5 | 50 |
| 6-10 | 100 |
| 11-15 | 150 |
| 16-20 | 200 |
| 21-26 | 250 |
| 27-31 | 300 |
| 32-36 | 350 |
| 37-41 | 400 |
| 42+ | 500 |

## Notes

- Unlike the [Sweep Job](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Sweep_Job "Skyrim:The Sweep Job") or similar collection quests, this quest will *not* have a visible counter telling you how far you have progressed, but you *will* be notified when you have stolen enough goods.
- It is not necessary to get arrested to fail this quest - merely being detected while breaking the law is sufficient. This includes trespassing and lockpicking (unless you have [Quick Hands](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking#Quick_Hands "Skyrim:Lockpicking")).
- Your loot generally needs to be items that are placed in the world itself, or they won't count towards this quest. Items in display cases are fair game (as long as you aren't caught picking the cases open), but items looted from storage containers (chests, wardrobes, dressers, basically anything where you open an item menu to take stuff) will not count.
  - Picking pockets, even if successful, also does not count towards this quest.
- [Stones of Barenziah](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned") seem to be a special case for this quest: picking one up from an owned house in the hold related to the job will complete the Steal objective immediately, despite the stones showing a value of 200 and not being marked as "stolen".
- You are not required to hand over the items you've stolen as part of turning in the quest. This means you can either keep the items for yourself, or [fence](/wiki/Skyrim:Fence_(merchant) "Skyrim:Fence (merchant)") them to gain extra money on top of the quest reward.
- Stealing an item only works once. You cannot drop the item and pick it up again for the next Bedlam Job.
  - However, some items do respawn if you've been away from the town long enough. Others don't...

## Bugs

- It is impossible to complete this quest if you are sent to Raven Rock.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
  -  On a PC, you can complete the quest manually via the command console using the following console command: `setstage TGRNT 50`. Play on anything else and you're out of luck.
  - If you do get the job in Raven Rock, and don't have the Unofficial Patch installed, the only way to clear it and to receive other jobs from Delvin is to either tell him that you want to quit, or intentionally get caught. There are no negative consequences for quitting.
- You may sometimes be able to complete the quest after stealing less than 500 gold worth of items. **?**

## Quest Stages

| The Bedlam Job (TGRNT) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I've been told to steal 500 gold in goods from <Alias=City> without witnesses. Items I'm seen stealing won't count towards my total, so I need to keep out of sight. I need to complete this job without getting caught and spending time in jail. *Objective 10:* Steal 500 gold in goods from <Alias=City> |
| 50 |  | I've stolen 500 gold in goods from <Alias=City>. *Objective 20:* Return to Delvin |
| 200 | ☑ | I've successfully completed this job and been allowed to keep everything I've stolen. |
| 250 | ☒ | During the course of this task, I was arrested and sent to the local jail. I've therefore failed the job. |
| ☒ | Before the task could be completed, I decided to quit. I've therefore failed the job and forfeited any pay I might have received. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TGRNT stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TGRNT`.

Exterior of the Bee and Barb

**The Bee and Barb** is an [inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Skyrim:Inns") located in the center of city of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), next to the marketplace.

[Keerava](/wiki/Skyrim:Keerava "Skyrim:Keerava") and [Talen-Jei](/wiki/Skyrim:Talen-Jei "Skyrim:Talen-Jei"), an [Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") bartender, work here. [Marcurio](/wiki/Skyrim:Marcurio "Skyrim:Marcurio") is a mercenary for hire that can usually be found sitting in the southwest corner on a wooden bench. There is only one [interior zone](#The_Bee_and_Barb) in the location.

## Residents

| Name |
| --- |
| [Keerava](/wiki/Skyrim:Keerava "Skyrim:Keerava") [Innkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Innkeeper") [Food and Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Food and Drink")  [Talen-Jei](/wiki/Skyrim:Talen-Jei "Skyrim:Talen-Jei")  [Marcurio](/wiki/Skyrim:Marcurio "Skyrim:Marcurio")\* |

\* If he is not following you or made steward of any of the houses you build [HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire").

## Patrons

The people who frequent the Bee and Barb are:

- **[Aerin](/wiki/Skyrim:Aerin "Skyrim:Aerin")** — An Imperial who arrives at the inn around noon to sit and have dinner with Mjoll, leaving with her six hours later.
- **[Indaryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Indaryn "Skyrim:Indaryn")** — A Dunmer who helps run the [Black-Briar Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Meadery "Skyrim:Black-Briar Meadery"), who visits the inn every day.
- **[Louis Letrush](/wiki/Skyrim:Louis_Letrush "Skyrim:Louis Letrush")** — A Breton frequenting the inn before finishing the quest [Promises to Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Promises_to_Keep "Skyrim:Promises to Keep").
- **[Marcurio](/wiki/Skyrim:Marcurio "Skyrim:Marcurio")** — A [sellsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers#Hirelings "Skyrim:Followers") who sits on a bench by the southern entrance.
- **[Maven Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar")** — The matriarch of the Black-Briar family who will occasionally be found sitting next to a table upstairs in an alcove near the staircase.
- **[Mjoll the Lioness](/wiki/Skyrim:Mjoll_the_Lioness "Skyrim:Mjoll the Lioness")** — The "champion of the hold" who arrives at the inn at around noon to sit and have dinner with Aerin; she and Aerin will leave The Bee and Barb around 6pm.
- **[Romlyn Dreth](/wiki/Skyrim:Romlyn_Dreth "Skyrim:Romlyn Dreth")** — A Dunmer employee of the Black-Briar Meadery who comes to the inn after finishing his shift and usually sits by the bar, attempting to sell you his cheap [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead").
- **[Sapphire](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_(person) "Skyrim:Sapphire (person)")** — A member of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") who leans against a wall near the staircase.
- **[Vulwulf Snow-Shod](/wiki/Skyrim:Vulwulf_Snow-Shod "Skyrim:Vulwulf Snow-Shod")** — A loyal [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") supporter who arrives at the inn at noon to sit and have several drinks before leaving at 6pm.

## Related Quests

- **[Blue in the Face](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_in_the_Face "Skyrim:Blue in the Face")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblins "Skyrim:Goblins"): Investigate rumors of the Blue God's return.
- **[Sealing the Deal](/wiki/Skyrim:Sealing_the_Deal "Skyrim:Sealing the Deal")**: Find three [flawless amethysts](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Amethyst "Skyrim:Flawless Amethyst") for [Talen-Jei](/wiki/Skyrim:Talen-Jei "Skyrim:Talen-Jei")'s engagement ring.
- **[Taking Care of Business](/wiki/Skyrim:Taking_Care_of_Business "Skyrim:Taking Care of Business")**: Collect some debts for the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").

### Exterior

The Bee and Barb has two entrances, one positioned next to [Marise Aravel's](/wiki/Skyrim:Marise_Aravel "Skyrim:Marise Aravel") cart near the marketplace, and the other north of this door. The Bee and Barb looks out of shape, as the upstairs area is bigger than the common room, and thus it has wooden supports holding up the first floor. The front of The Bee and Barb can be seen from the entrance to [Haelga's Bunkhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga%27s_Bunkhouse "Skyrim:Haelga's Bunkhouse").

### The Bee and Barb

[Talen-Jei](/wiki/Skyrim:Talen-Jei "Skyrim:Talen-Jei") will normally be found working on the ground floor, sometimes sweeping. The common room consists of three tables, each with chairs, where the visitors of the tavern will sit to drink and eat. These hold three [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a couple of wedges of cheese, a few loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a [boiled creme treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"), a [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll") and a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"). [Keerava](/wiki/Skyrim:Keerava "Skyrim:Keerava") will be found behind the L-shaped counter, which is by a fireplace in a small corner of the tavern to the west. On the counter are two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), two boiled creme treats, an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie") and several pieces of cheese, with a small and a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") found underneath. On the mantelpiece over the fireplace is a bottle of Nord mead. Two stools are next to the counter.

[Sapphire](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_(person) "Skyrim:Sapphire (person)"), a member of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), will be found leaning against a wall in the tavern area until you complete a [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Stabilized "Skyrim:Stabilized") for [Shadr](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadr "Skyrim:Shadr"). There is a set of shelves holding clutter, two dressers with a bottle of alto wine, and a wooden bowl containing a [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") and [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") on one of them. There is a doorway to a storage area in the northwest corner of the common room. In this room are several [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels, a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand and, against the east wall, a long wooden table holding a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"), a couple of loaves of bread, a cabbage, a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and a couple of sacks of foodstuffs. Above the table is a wall shelf holding a couple of [goat cheese wheels](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), and hanging from the ceiling above is a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braid, two bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam").

There is a door in the middle of the east wall that leads to a flight of stairs down to the cellar, with several barrels of food around the top of the stairs. At the bottom, the cellar is one big storage area with a pile of firewood and [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") under the stairs, several food and mead barrels and sacks around the cellar along with a couple of baskets, one containing potatoes and the other a mixture of [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"). Hanging from the ceiling are three garlic braids, two bunches of elves ear, a bunch of frost mirriam and a couple of racks holding three [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") and another rabbit. Against the west wall are a couple of large vats and a set of shelves holding two bottles of alto wine, two bottles of wine and four bottles of Nord mead. To the south, against the wall, are two sets of shelves and a cupboard that only holds clutter. On the shelves are several pieces of cheese, a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a bunch of elves ear, some more potatoes, two cabbages and a couple of loaves of bread, with a bowl of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal") on top of one of the sets of shelves.

Above the staircase leading down to the cellar is a flight of wooden stairs leading up to the second floor. There are a couple of food barrels by the top of the stairs as well as a door through onto a large landing with a door to the south, one to the west, a third in the northwest corner and finally a fourth that is apprentice-locked to the north. To the right of this last door is a long wooden table with several pieces of cheese, a loaf of bread and a bottle of wine on top with two chairs beside it. This is where you will first be introduced to [Maven Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar") during the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") quest line.

Talen-Jei's bedroom is to the south and consists of a single owned bed in the southwest corner with a chair beside it and against the south wall a dresser with a copy of *[A Dream of Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dream_of_Sovngarde "Skyrim:A Dream of Sovngarde")* and a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Mara_Smiles_Upon_You! "Skyrim:Mara Smiles Upon You!") on top. The note is a reply from [Drifa](/wiki/Skyrim:Drifa "Skyrim:Drifa") regarding the Priests of [Mara](/wiki/Lore:Mara "Lore:Mara") being able to perform the traditional Argonian wedding ceremony for [him and Keerava](/wiki/Skyrim:Sealing_the_Deal "Skyrim:Sealing the Deal"). The bedroom to the west, which is the room you can rent from Keerava, consists of a single owned bed against the north wall with a chair beside the bed and an empty unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") against the west wall. The third bedroom consists of a single owned bed against the west wall, with a dresser with copies of *[Nightingales: Fact or Fiction?](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingales:_Fact_or_Fiction%3F "Skyrim:Nightingales: Fact or Fiction?")* and *[Of Crossed Daggers](/wiki/Skyrim:Of_Crossed_Daggers "Skyrim:Of Crossed Daggers")* on top. The door with the apprentice lock is Keerava's bedroom and consists of a single owned bed in the northeastern corner, with an end table beside it holding a bottle of alto wine. At the foot of the bed is an unlocked chest containing nothing. To the left of the chest, further along the north wall, is a small square wooden table and chair. This table holds the [business ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger"), a bottle of wine and an apprentice-locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") containing random items. Against the west wall is a tall wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes").

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in the inn's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be pickpocketed or stolen. They are restocked every two days.

| Count | Item | Sold By |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 12 | Random [drinks](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Beverages "Skyrim:Food") | Keerava |
| 8 | Random inn [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") | Keerava |
| 1 | [Salt Pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") | Keerava |
| 3 | [Cliff Racers](/wiki/Skyrim:Cliff_Racer "Skyrim:Cliff Racer") | Talen-Jei |
| 3 | [Velvet LeChances](/wiki/Skyrim:Velvet_LeChance "Skyrim:Velvet LeChance") | Talen-Jei |
| 3 | [White-Gold Towers](/wiki/Skyrim:White-Gold_Tower "Skyrim:White-Gold Tower") | Talen-Jei |

## Notes

- There is a  "Loot") Loot [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to the right of the entrance door. In Keerava's room, there is a chest.
- Three unique drinks are available for purchase, all named for various famous things: the [Cliff Racer](/wiki/Skyrim:Cliff_Racer "Skyrim:Cliff Racer") named for the [extinct bird](/wiki/Lore:Cliff_Racer "Lore:Cliff Racer"), the [Velvet LeChance](/wiki/Skyrim:Velvet_LeChance "Skyrim:Velvet LeChance") named for a notorious [assassin](/wiki/Lore:Lucien_Lachance "Lore:Lucien Lachance"), and the [White-Gold Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:White-Gold_Tower "Skyrim:White-Gold Tower") named for the [tower](/wiki/Lore:White-Gold_Tower "Lore:White-Gold Tower") in the Imperial City. These are found under potions when carried.
- All containers in the area, with the exception of some barrels and sacks, are non-respawning and safe to store items in.
- It is the only major city inn that does not have a bard. It's possible that Louis Letrush was originally meant to fill this role, as he's part of the bard class and has a bed at the inn, but there is no other evidence pointing to either him or anyone else conclusively.
- The inn's name is possibly a reference to the occurrences described in the book [The Real Barenziah, Part III](/wiki/Lore:The_Real_Barenziah,_Part_III "Lore:The Real Barenziah, Part III") found in *[Daggerfall](/wiki/Daggerfall:Daggerfall "Daggerfall:Daggerfall")*.
